Efficient Reasoning on the Edge
Authors: Yelysei Bondarenko, Thomas Hehn, Rob Hesselink, Romain Lepert, Fabio Valerio Massoli, Evgeny Mironov, Leyla Mirvakhabova, Tribhuvanesh Orekondy, Spyridon Stasis, Andrey Kuzmin, Anna Kuzina, Markus Nagel, Ankita Nayak, Corrado Rainone, Ork de Rooij, Paul N Whatmough, Arash Behboodi, Babak Ehteshami Bejnordi
First: 2026-03-17T17:59:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T17:59:51+00:00
Comments: Project page: https://qualcomm-ai-research.github.io/llm-reasoning-on-edge/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) with chain-of-thought reasoning achieve state-of-the-art performance across complex problem-solving tasks, but their verbose reasoning traces and large context requirements make them impractical for edge deployment. These challenges include high token generation costs, large KV-cache footprints, and inefficiencies when distilling reasoning capabilities into smaller models for mobile devices. Existing approaches often rely on distilling reasoning traces from larger models into smaller models, which are verbose and stylistically redundant, undesirable for on-device inference. In this work, we propose a lightweight approach to enable reasoning in small LLMs using LoRA adapters combined with supervised fine-tuning. We further introduce budget forcing via reinforcement learning on these adapters, significantly reducing response length with minimal accuracy loss. To address memory-bound decoding, we exploit parallel test-time scaling, improving accuracy at minor latency increase. Finally, we present a dynamic adapter-switching mechanism that activates reasoning only when needed and a KV-cache sharing strategy during prompt encoding, reducing time-to-first-token for on-device inference. Experiments on Qwen2.5-7B demonstrate that our method achieves efficient, accurate reasoning under strict resource constraints, making LLM reasoning practical for mobile scenarios. Videos demonstrating our solution running on mobile devices are available on our project page.
中文标题/摘要
标题：边缘设备的高效推理
采用思维链推理的大语言模型在复杂问题解决任务中实现了最先进的性能，但其冗长的推理轨迹和庞大的上下文需求使其难以在边缘设备部署。这些挑战包括高昂的令牌生成成本、庞大的键值缓存占用，以及将推理能力蒸馏到移动设备小型模型时的效率低下。现有方法通常依赖将大型模型的推理轨迹蒸馏到小型模型，这些轨迹冗长且存在风格冗余，不利于设备端推理。本研究提出一种轻量级方法，通过结合监督微调的LoRA适配器实现小型大语言模型的推理能力。我们进一步通过强化学习对这些适配器实施预算强制策略，在最小精度损失下显著缩短响应长度。针对内存受限的解码场景，我们利用并行测试时缩放技术，以微小延迟代价提升精度。最后，我们提出动态适配器切换机制（仅在需要时激活推理）及提示编码期间的键值缓存共享策略，从而降低设备端推理的首令牌生成延迟。基于Qwen2.5-7B的实验表明，我们的方法在严格资源限制下实现了高效精准的推理，使大语言模型推理技术切实适用于移动场景。项目页面提供了在移动设备运行方案的演示视频。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of deploying large language models (LLMs) with chain-of-thought reasoning on resource-constrained edge devices, where verbose reasoning traces and large context requirements lead to high token costs and memory inefficiency. The proposed method combines LoRA adapters with supervised fine-tuning to enable reasoning in small LLMs, introduces budget forcing via reinforcement learning to shorten responses, employs parallel test-time scaling to improve accuracy with minimal latency, and implements dynamic adapter-switching and KV-cache sharing to optimize on-device inference. Experimental results on Qwen2.5-7B show that this approach achieves efficient and accurate reasoning under strict resource constraints, making LLM reasoning practical for mobile deployment.
本文针对具有思维链推理能力的大语言模型在资源受限的边缘设备上部署的挑战，其冗长的推理轨迹和大上下文需求会导致高令牌成本和内存低效。所提出的方法结合LoRA适配器和监督微调，使小型大语言模型具备推理能力；通过强化学习引入预算强制以缩短响应长度；采用并行测试时缩放以最小延迟提升精度；并实现动态适配器切换和KV缓存共享来优化设备端推理。在Qwen2.5-7B上的实验结果表明，该方法在严格资源限制下实现了高效准确的推理，使得大语言模型推理在移动场景中变得实用。
Stochastic Resetting Accelerates Policy Convergence in Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Jello Zhou, Vudtiwat Ngampruetikorn, David J. Schwab
First: 2026-03-17T17:50:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T17:50:32+00:00
Comments: 18 pages, 17 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Stochastic resetting, where a dynamical process is intermittently returned to a fixed reference state, has emerged as a powerful mechanism for optimizing first-passage properties. Existing theory largely treats static, non-learning processes. Here we ask how stochastic resetting interacts with reinforcement learning, where the underlying dynamics adapt through experience. In tabular grid environments, we find that resetting accelerates policy convergence even when it does not reduce the search time of a purely diffusive agent, indicating a novel mechanism beyond classical first-passage optimization. In a continuous control task with neural-network-based value approximation, we show that random resetting improves deep reinforcement learning when exploration is difficult and rewards are sparse. Unlike temporal discounting, resetting preserves the optimal policy while accelerating convergence by truncating long, uninformative trajectories to enhance value propagation. Our results establish stochastic resetting as a simple, tunable mechanism for accelerating learning, translating a canonical phenomenon of statistical mechanics into an optimization principle for reinforcement learning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：随机重置加速强化学习中的策略收敛
随机重置——即动态过程间歇性地被重置至固定参考状态——已成为优化首次通过特性的有效机制。现有理论主要针对静态、非学习过程。本文探讨随机重置如何与强化学习相互作用，其中底层动态通过经验自适应。在表格网格环境中，我们发现即使重置不减少纯扩散智能体的搜索时间，仍能加速策略收敛，这揭示了超越经典首次通过优化的新机制。在基于神经网络价值近似的连续控制任务中，随机重置在探索困难且奖励稀疏的情况下能提升深度强化学习性能。与时序折扣不同，重置通过截断冗长无效轨迹以增强价值传播，在保持最优策略的同时加速收敛。本研究将随机重置确立为一种可调节的简易学习加速机制，将统计力学的典型现象转化为强化学习的优化原理。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the established role of stochastic resetting in optimizing first-passage times for static processes, this paper investigates its interaction with reinforcement learning, where dynamics adapt through experience. The method applies stochastic resetting, which intermittently returns an agent to a fixed state, to both tabular grid environments and a continuous control task using neural-network-based value approximation. Key experimental results show that resetting accelerates policy convergence in grid worlds even without reducing diffusive search time, revealing a novel mechanism beyond classical first-passage optimization, and it improves deep reinforcement learning performance in sparse-reward settings by truncating uninformative trajectories to enhance value propagation, all while preserving the optimal policy.
本文的动机源于随机重置在优化静态过程首达时间中的已知作用，旨在探究其与强化学习（其中动态通过经验自适应）的相互作用。方法是将随机重置（间歇地将智能体返回到固定状态）应用于表格网格环境和基于神经网络价值近似的连续控制任务。主要实验结果表明，在网格世界中，重置加速了策略收敛，即使没有减少扩散搜索时间，这揭示了超越经典首达优化的新机制；在稀疏奖励设置中，它通过截断无信息轨迹以增强价值传播，提升了深度强化学习的性能，同时保持了最优策略不变。
Learning to Present: Inverse Specification Rewards for Agentic Slide Generation
Authors: Karthik Ragunath Ananda Kumar, Subrahmanyam Arunachalam
First: 2026-03-17T17:45:53+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T17:45:53+00:00
Comments: 12 pages, 11 figures, 13 tables, 26 references. Code: https://github.com/pushing-the-frontier/slide-forge-llm Dataset: https://huggingface.co/datasets/KarthikRagunathAnandaKumar/sliderl-multi-turn-rollouts
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Automated presentation generation remains a challenging task requiring coherent content creation, visual design, and audience-aware communication. This work proposes an OpenEnv-compatible reinforcement learning environment where LLM agents learn to research topics, plan content, and generate professional HTML slide presentations through tool use. We introduce a multi-component reward system combining structural validation, render quality assessment, LLM-based aesthetic scoring, content quality metrics, and an inverse specification reward that measures how faithfully generated slides convey their intended purpose. The inverse specification reward, an "inverse task" where an LLM attempts to recover the original specification from generated slides, provides a holistic quality signal. Our approach fine-tunes Qwen2.5-Coder-7B via GRPO, training only 0.5% of parameters on prompts derived from expert demonstrations collected using Claude Opus 4.6. Experiments on 48 diverse business briefs across six models demonstrate that our fine-tuned 7B model achieves 91.2% of Claude Opus 4.6's quality while improving 33.1% over the base model. The six-model comparison reveals that instruction adherence and tool-use compliance, rather than raw parameter count, determine agentic task performance. We contribute SlideRL, an open-source dataset of 288 multi-turn rollout trajectories across all six models: https://huggingface.co/datasets/KarthikRagunathAnandaKumar/sliderl-multi-turn-rollouts Code: https://github.com/pushing-the-frontier/slide-forge-llm
中文标题/摘要
标题：学习呈现：面向智能幻灯片生成的逆向规范奖励机制
自动化演示文稿生成是一项需要连贯内容创作、视觉设计和受众感知沟通的挑战性任务。本研究提出一个兼容OpenEnv的强化学习环境，使LLM智能体能够通过学习研究主题、规划内容并利用工具生成专业的HTML幻灯片演示。我们引入了一个多组件奖励系统，结合结构验证、渲染质量评估、基于LLM的审美评分、内容质量指标，以及衡量生成幻灯片对预期目标传达忠实度的逆向规范奖励。该逆向规范奖励采用“逆向任务”形式，即通过LLM尝试从生成幻灯片中还原原始任务规范，从而提供整体质量信号。我们的方法通过GRPO对Qwen2.5-Coder-7B进行微调，仅使用Claude Opus 4.6收集的专家演示提示中0.5%的参数进行训练。在48个多样化商业简报上对六个模型的实验表明，微调后的7B模型达到Claude Opus 4.6质量的91.2%，同时较基础模型提升33.1%。六模型对比揭示：指令遵循度和工具使用合规性（而非原始参数量）决定智能体任务性能。我们开源了SlideRL数据集，包含所有六个模型的288条多轮次推演轨迹：https://huggingface.co/datasets/KarthikRagunathAnandaKumar/sliderl-multi-turn-rollouts 代码：https://github.com/pushing-the-frontier/slide-forge-llm
Summary / 总结
This work addresses the challenge of automated presentation generation by developing a reinforcement learning environment where LLM agents learn to create professional HTML slide presentations through tool use. The method introduces a multi-component reward system, including a novel inverse specification reward where an LLM attempts to recover the original task specification from the generated slides, providing a holistic quality signal. The approach fine-tunes the Qwen2.5-Coder-7B model via GRPO on a small subset of parameters using expert demonstrations. Experimental results on 48 diverse business briefs show the fine-tuned 7B model achieves 91.2% of the quality of the much larger Claude Opus 4.6 model and a 33.1% improvement over its base version, demonstrating that instruction adherence and tool-use compliance are more critical than model size for agentic task performance.
本研究针对自动化演示文稿生成的挑战，提出了一个强化学习环境，使大语言模型智能体能够通过工具使用来学习创建专业的HTML幻灯片演示。该方法引入了一个多组件奖励系统，包括一种新颖的逆向规范奖励，即让一个大语言模型尝试从生成的幻灯片中恢复原始任务规范，从而提供全面的质量信号。该方法使用专家演示数据，通过GRPO对Qwen2.5-Coder-7B模型仅0.5%的参数进行微调。在48个不同商业简报上的实验结果表明，微调后的7B模型达到了大型模型Claude Opus 4.6质量的91.2%，并比其基础版本提升了33.1%，这证明了对于智能体任务性能而言，指令遵循和工具使用合规性比模型参数量更为关键。
Anticipatory Planning for Multimodal AI Agents
Authors: Yongyuan Liang, Shijie Zhou, Yu Gu, Hao Tan, Gang Wu, Franck Dernoncourt, Jihyung Kil, Ryan A. Rossi, Ruiyi Zhang
Venue: CVPR 2026
First: 2026-03-17T16:55:11+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T16:55:11+00:00
Comments: Published at CVPR 2026 Findings Track
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent advances in multimodal agents have improved computer-use interaction and tool-usage, yet most existing systems remain reactive, optimizing actions in isolation without reasoning about future states or long-term goals. This limits planning coherence and prevents agents from reliably solving high-level, multi-step tasks. We introduce TraceR1, a two-stage reinforcement learning framework that explicitly trains anticipatory reasoning by forecasting short-horizon trajectories before execution. The first stage performs trajectory-level reinforcement learning with rewards that enforce global consistency across predicted action sequences. The second stage applies grounded reinforcement fine-tuning, using execution feedback from frozen tool agents to refine step-level accuracy and executability. TraceR1 is evaluated across seven benchmarks, covering online computer-use, offline computer-use benchmarks, and multimodal tool-use reasoning tasks, where it achieves substantial improvements in planning stability, execution robustness, and generalization over reactive and single-stage baselines. These results show that anticipatory trajectory reasoning is a key principle for building multimodal agents that can reason, plan, and act effectively in complex real-world environments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：多模态AI智能体的前瞻性规划
多模态智能体的最新进展提升了计算机交互与工具使用能力，但现有系统大多仍属被动响应型，仅孤立优化单步动作而缺乏对未来状态或长期目标的推理。这限制了规划的一致性，使智能体难以可靠解决高层次、多步骤任务。我们提出TraceR1——一个两阶段强化学习框架，通过在执行前预测短期轨迹来显式训练前瞻性推理能力。第一阶段执行轨迹级强化学习，其奖励机制确保预测动作序列的全局一致性；第二阶段进行基于执行的强化微调，利用冻结工具智能体的执行反馈来优化步骤级准确性与可执行性。TraceR1在涵盖在线/离线计算机使用基准及多模态工具使用推理任务的七项基准测试中均取得显著提升，在规划稳定性、执行鲁棒性和泛化能力上大幅超越被动响应型及单阶段基线模型。结果表明，前瞻性轨迹推理是构建能在复杂现实环境中有效推理、规划与行动的多模态智能体的核心原则。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the reactive nature of existing multimodal AI agents, which limits their ability to plan coherently for multi-step tasks, this paper introduces TraceR1, a two-stage reinforcement learning framework that trains agents to forecast short-horizon trajectories before execution to enable anticipatory reasoning. The method first uses trajectory-level reinforcement learning to enforce global consistency across predicted action sequences, followed by grounded reinforcement fine-tuning with execution feedback from frozen tool agents to refine step-level accuracy. Experimental results across seven benchmarks in online/offline computer-use and multimodal tool-use tasks show that TraceR1 substantially improves planning stability, execution robustness, and generalization over reactive and single-stage baselines, demonstrating the value of anticipatory reasoning for effective agent performance in complex environments.
针对现有多模态AI智能体多为反应式、难以连贯规划多步骤任务的问题，本文提出了TraceR1，一个两阶段强化学习框架，通过在执行前预测短期轨迹来训练智能体的前瞻性推理能力。该方法首先进行轨迹级强化学习以确保预测行动序列的全局一致性，随后利用冻结工具智能体的执行反馈进行接地强化微调，以提升步骤级准确性和可执行性。在涵盖在线/离线计算机使用和多模态工具使用推理的七个基准测试中，实验结果表明TraceR1在规划稳定性、执行鲁棒性和泛化能力上均显著优于反应式及单阶段基线方法，证明了前瞻性轨迹推理对于构建能在复杂现实环境中有效推理、规划与行动的多模态智能体的关键作用。
When Should a Robot Think? Resource-Aware Reasoning via Reinforcement Learning for Embodied Robotic Decision-Making
Authors: Jun Liu, Pu Zhao, Zhenglun Kong, Xuan Shen, Peiyan Dong, Fan Yang, Lin Cui, Hao Tang, Geng Yuan, Wei Niu, Wenbin Zhang, Xue Lin, Gaowen Liu, Yanzhi Wang, Dong Huang
First: 2026-03-17T15:38:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T15:38:50+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Embodied robotic systems increasingly rely on large language model (LLM)-based agents to support high-level reasoning, planning, and decision-making during interactions with the environment. However, invoking LLM reasoning introduces substantial computational latency and resource overhead, which can interrupt action execution and reduce system reliability. Excessive reasoning may delay actions, while insufficient reasoning often leads to incorrect decisions and task failures. This raises a fundamental question for embodied agents: when should the agent reason, and when should it act? In this work, we propose RARRL (Resource-Aware Reasoning via Reinforcement Learning), a hierarchical framework for resource-aware orchestration of embodied agents. Rather than learning low-level control policies, RARRL learns a high-level orchestration policy that operates at the agent's decision-making layer. This policy enables the agent to adaptively determine whether to invoke reasoning, which reasoning role to employ, and how much computational budget to allocate based on current observations, execution history, and remaining resources. Extensive experiments, including evaluations with empirical latency profiles derived from the ALFRED benchmark, show that RARRL consistently improves task success rates while reducing execution latency and enhancing robustness compared with fixed or heuristic reasoning strategies. These results demonstrate that adaptive reasoning control is essential for building reliable and efficient embodied robotic agents.
中文标题/摘要
标题：机器人何时应思考？基于强化学习的资源感知推理在具身机器人决策中的应用
具身机器人系统日益依赖基于大语言模型（LLM）的智能体，以支持其在与环境交互过程中的高层推理、规划与决策。然而，调用LLM推理会带来显著的计算延迟与资源开销，可能中断动作执行并降低系统可靠性。过度推理会延迟行动，而推理不足则常导致错误决策与任务失败。这引发了一个具身智能体的根本性问题：智能体应在何时推理，又在何时行动？本研究提出RARRL（基于强化学习的资源感知推理），一种用于具身智能体资源感知编排的分层框架。RARRL并非学习底层控制策略，而是学习在智能体决策层运作的高层编排策略。该策略使智能体能够根据当前观察、执行历史与剩余资源，自适应地决定是否调用推理、采用何种推理角色以及分配多少计算预算。大量实验（包括基于ALFRED基准衍生的实际延迟配置文件评估）表明，相较于固定或启发式推理策略，RARRL在持续提升任务成功率的同时，有效降低了执行延迟并增强了系统鲁棒性。这些结果证明，自适应推理控制对于构建可靠高效的具身机器人智能体至关重要。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of balancing computational cost and decision quality in embodied robotic systems that use large language models (LLMs) for reasoning, where excessive reasoning causes latency and insufficient reasoning leads to failures. The authors propose RARRL, a hierarchical reinforcement learning framework that learns a high-level orchestration policy to adaptively decide when to invoke reasoning, which reasoning role to use, and how much computational budget to allocate based on observations, history, and resources. Experimental evaluations using latency profiles from the ALFRED benchmark demonstrate that RARRL improves task success rates while reducing execution latency and enhancing robustness compared to fixed or heuristic strategies, highlighting the importance of adaptive reasoning control for efficient robotic agents.
本文针对具身机器人系统使用大语言模型进行推理时面临的平衡计算成本与决策质量的挑战，即过度推理会导致延迟，而推理不足则引发任务失败。作者提出了RARRL，一种分层强化学习框架，通过学习高层编排策略，使机器人能根据当前观察、执行历史和剩余资源自适应地决定何时调用推理、使用何种推理角色以及分配多少计算预算。基于ALFRED基准的延迟配置文件进行的实验评估表明，与固定或启发式推理策略相比，RARRL提高了任务成功率，同时减少了执行延迟并增强了鲁棒性，这证明了自适应推理控制对于构建高效可靠具身机器人的重要性。
Aletheia: What Makes RLVR For Code Verifiers Tick?
Authors: Vatsal Venkatkrishna, Indraneil Paul, Iryna Gurevych
First: 2026-01-17T22:30:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T15:26:31+00:00
Comments: 21 pages, 6 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multi-domain thinking verifiers trained via Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) are a cornerstone of modern post-training. However, their adoption in code generation has lagged behind execution feedback due to the prohibitive costs of the full RLVR pipeline. In this work, we ablate three primary drivers of RLVR performance and cost: intermediate thinking traces, learning from negative samples, and on-policy training. We introduce Aletheia, a controlled, execution-grounded testbed to facilitate a contamination-free analysis of code verifiers across disparate model sizes and covariate shifts. Our analysis reveals that the optimal training recipe is scale-dependent: on-policy learning is the primary performance driver for small verifiers, whereas thinking traces become the most vital factor for larger sizes. Furthermore, we show that negative samples stabilize training at large sizes, and scaling inference-time compute cannot compensate for any core RLVR component. These findings provide a compute-optimal roadmap for practitioners, offering concrete strategies to simplify verifier training based on model size. Consequently, our work establishes a foundation for scalable supervision, enabling efficiently trained code verifiers to reliably supervise much larger code generation policies.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Aletheia：代码验证器中RLVR机制的核心驱动因素探究
通过可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）训练的多领域思维验证器是现代后训练的核心组件，但其在代码生成中的应用因完整RLVR流程的高昂成本而落后于执行反馈。本研究通过消融实验分析了影响RLVR性能与成本的三个关键因素：中间思维轨迹、负样本学习以及同策略训练。我们提出了Aletheia——一个基于执行反馈的受控测试平台，用于对不同模型规模和协变量偏移下的代码验证器进行无干扰分析。研究发现最优训练方案具有规模依赖性：同策略学习是小型验证器的主要性能驱动因素，而思维轨迹在较大规模模型中成为最关键要素。此外，负样本能提升大规模训练的稳定性，且增加推理时计算资源无法弥补任何核心RLVR组件的缺失。这些发现为实践者提供了计算最优化的技术路线图，提出了根据模型规模简化验证器训练的具体策略。本研究由此为可扩展监督奠定了基础，使高效训练的代码验证器能够可靠地监督更大规模的代码生成策略。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates the key factors driving the performance and cost of Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) for training code verifiers, which have seen limited adoption due to high computational expenses. The authors introduce Aletheia, a controlled testbed, to systematically ablate three core components: intermediate thinking traces, learning from negative samples, and on-policy training. Their experiments reveal that the optimal training strategy depends on model scale; for smaller verifiers, on-policy learning is the primary performance driver, while for larger models, thinking traces become most critical, with negative samples aiding training stability. The results demonstrate that scaling inference compute cannot substitute for any core RLVR component, providing a compute-optimal roadmap to simplify verifier training based on model size.
本文研究了在训练代码验证器中驱动强化学习与可验证奖励（RLVR）性能和成本的关键因素，该技术因计算成本高昂而应用受限。作者引入了Aletheia这一受控测试平台，系统性地分析了三个核心组件：中间思维轨迹、从负样本中学习以及在线策略训练。实验结果表明，最佳训练策略取决于模型规模；对于较小验证器，在线策略学习是主要性能驱动因素，而对于较大模型，思维轨迹变得最为关键，负样本则有助于提升训练稳定性。研究证明，增加推理计算资源无法替代任何核心RLVR组件，从而为基于模型规模简化验证器训练提供了计算最优的路线图。
What if Pinocchio Were a Reinforcement Learning Agent: A Normative End-to-End Pipeline
Authors: Benoît Alcaraz
First: 2026-03-17T15:21:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T15:21:17+00:00
Comments: PhD thesis
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In the past decade, artificial intelligence (AI) has developed quickly. With this rapid progression came the need for systems capable of complying with the rules and norms of our society so that they can be successfully and safely integrated into our daily lives. Inspired by the story of Pinocchio in ``Le avventure di Pinocchio - Storia di un burattino'', this thesis proposes a pipeline that addresses the problem of developing norm compliant and context-aware agents. Building on the AJAR, Jiminy, and NGRL architectures, the work introduces \pino, a hybrid model in which reinforcement learning agents are supervised by argumentation-based normative advisors. In order to make this pipeline operational, this thesis also presents a novel algorithm for automatically extracting the arguments and relationships that underlie the advisors' decisions. Finally, this thesis investigates the phenomenon of \textit{norm avoidance}, providing a definition and a mitigation strategy within the context of reinforcement learning agents. Each component of the pipeline is empirically evaluated. The thesis concludes with a discussion of related work, current limitations, and directions for future research.
中文标题/摘要
标题：假如匹诺曹是强化学习智能体：一种规范化的端到端流程
过去十年间，人工智能（AI）发展迅速。随着这一快速进展，需要系统能够遵守社会规则与规范，以便成功且安全地融入日常生活。受《匹诺曹历险记——一个木偶的故事》启发，本论文提出了一种流程，旨在解决开发符合规范且具备情境感知能力的智能体的问题。基于AJAR、Jiminy和NGRL架构，本研究引入了\pino——一种混合模型，其中强化学习智能体受基于论证的规范顾问监督。为使该流程可操作，论文还提出了一种新颖算法，用于自动提取支撑顾问决策的论证与关系。最后，论文研究了“规范规避”现象，在强化学习智能体背景下给出了定义及缓解策略。流程的每个组件均经过实证评估。论文以相关研究、当前局限性和未来方向的讨论作结。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for AI systems to adhere to societal norms for safe integration, this thesis proposes an end-to-end pipeline for developing norm-compliant, context-aware reinforcement learning agents, inspired by the Pinocchio story. The method introduces Pino, a hybrid model where reinforcement learning agents are supervised by argumentation-based normative advisors, building on prior architectures like AJAR and Jiminy, and includes a novel algorithm for automatically extracting the arguments behind advisory decisions. Experimental results empirically evaluate each pipeline component, investigate norm avoidance with a defined mitigation strategy, and demonstrate the pipeline's effectiveness in fostering normative compliance, while also discussing limitations and future research directions.

Refining Few-Step Text-to-Multiview Diffusion via Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Ziyi Zhang, Li Shen, Deheng Ye, Yong Luo, Huangxuan Zhao, Meng Liu, Wei Yu, Lefei Zhang
Venue: CVPR 2026
First: 2025-05-26T15:11:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T15:09:09+00:00
Comments: Accepted to CVPR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Text-to-multiview (T2MV) diffusion models have shown great promise in generating multiple views of a scene from a single text prompt. While few-step backbones enable real-time T2MV generation, they often compromise key aspects of generation quality, such as per-view fidelity and cross-view consistency. Reinforcement learning (RL) finetuning offers a potential solution, yet existing approaches designed for single-image diffusion do not readily extend to the few-step T2MV setting, as they neglect cross-view coordination and suffer from weak learning signals in few-step regimes. To address this, we propose MVC-ZigAL, a tailored RL finetuning framework for few-step T2MV diffusion models. Specifically, its core insights are: (1) a new MDP formulation that jointly models all generated views and assesses their collective quality via a joint-view reward; (2) a novel advantage learning strategy that exploits the performance gains of a self-refinement sampling scheme over standard sampling, yielding stronger learning signals for effective RL finetuning; and (3) a unified RL framework that extends advantage learning with a Lagrangian dual formulation for multiview-constrained optimization, balancing single-view and joint-view objectives through adaptive primal-dual updates under a self-paced threshold curriculum that harmonizes exploration and constraint enforcement. Collectively, these designs enable robust and balanced RL finetuning for few-step T2MV diffusion models, yielding substantial gains in both per-view fidelity and cross-view consistency. Code is available at https://github.com/ZiyiZhang27/MVC-ZigAL.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过强化学习优化少步文本到多视角扩散模型
文本到多视角扩散模型在根据单一文本提示生成场景多视角图像方面展现出巨大潜力。虽然少步主干网络能实现实时生成，但常以牺牲生成质量（如单视角保真度和跨视角一致性）为代价。强化学习微调提供了一种潜在解决方案，但现有针对单图像扩散的方法难以直接适用于少步多视角场景，因其忽略跨视角协调且在少步机制下学习信号薄弱。为此，我们提出MVC-ZigAL——专为少步文本到多视角扩散模型设计的强化学习微调框架。其核心创新在于：（1）构建联合建模所有生成视角并通过联合视角奖励评估整体质量的新MDP形式化方法；（2）利用自优化采样方案相对于标准采样的性能增益，设计能产生更强学习信号的新型优势学习策略；（3）通过拉格朗日对偶形式扩展优势学习的统一强化学习框架，在协调探索与约束执行的自适应阈值课程下，实现单视角与联合视角目标的平衡优化。这些设计共同实现了对少步文本到多视角扩散模型的稳健平衡微调，在单视角保真度与跨视角一致性上均取得显著提升。代码发布于https://github.com/ZiyiZhang27/MVC-ZigAL。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the quality degradation in per-view fidelity and cross-view consistency when using few-step diffusion backbones for real-time text-to-multiview (T2MV) generation. The authors propose MVC-ZigAL, a reinforcement learning (RL) finetuning framework tailored for few-step T2MV models, which introduces a novel Markov Decision Process formulation that jointly models all generated views with a joint-view reward, a self-refinement sampling strategy to strengthen learning signals, and a unified Lagrangian dual framework to balance single-view and joint-view objectives adaptively. Experimental results demonstrate that the method achieves substantial improvements in both per-view image quality and consistency across multiple views.
本文针对实时文本到多视角生成中，少步扩散模型常导致单视角保真度和跨视角一致性下降的问题，提出了一种专为少步文本到多视角模型设计的强化学习微调框架MVC-ZigAL。该方法的核心包括：一种联合建模所有生成视角并评估其整体质量的新马尔可夫决策过程；一种利用自优化采样方案增强学习信号的优势学习策略；以及一个通过拉格朗日对偶公式平衡单视角与联合视角目标的自适应优化框架。实验结果表明，该方法在单视角图像质量和跨视角一致性方面均取得了显著提升。
A Scalable Approach to Solving Simulation-Based Network Security Games
Authors: Michael Lanier, Yevgeniy Vorobeychik
First: 2026-02-18T16:07:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T14:41:01+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We introduce MetaDOAR, a lightweight meta-controller that augments the Double Oracle / PSRO paradigm with a learned, partition-aware filtering layer and Q-value caching to enable scalable multi-agent reinforcement learning on very large cyber-network environments. MetaDOAR learns a compact state projection from per node structural embeddings to rapidly score and select a small subset of devices (a top-k partition) on which a conventional low-level actor performs focused beam search utilizing a critic agent. Selected candidate actions are evaluated with batched critic forwards and stored in an LRU cache keyed by a quantized state projection and local action identifiers, dramatically reducing redundant critic computation while preserving decision quality via conservative k-hop cache invalidation. Empirically, MetaDOAR attains higher player payoffs than SOTA baselines on large network topologies, without significant scaling issues in terms of memory usage or training time. This contribution provide a practical, theoretically motivated path to efficient hierarchical policy learning for large-scale networked decision problems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：一种可扩展的基于仿真的网络安全博弈求解方法
本文提出MetaDOAR，一种轻量级元控制器，通过引入基于学习的、分区感知的过滤层与Q值缓存机制，扩展了双Oracle/PSRO范式，从而支持在超大规模网络环境中进行可扩展的多智能体强化学习。MetaDOAR从节点结构嵌入中学习紧凑的状态投影，快速评分并选择一小部分设备（top-k分区），由传统底层执行器结合评论家智能体进行聚焦束搜索。候选动作通过批量评论家前向传播评估，并存储在以量化状态投影和局部动作标识为键的LRU缓存中，通过保守的k跳缓存失效策略，在保持决策质量的同时显著减少冗余的评论家计算。实验表明，在大型网络拓扑中，MetaDOAR在内存使用和训练时间未出现显著扩展问题的前提下，获得了优于现有先进基线的玩家收益。该研究为大规模网络化决策问题的高效分层策略学习提供了兼具理论依据与实践可行性的路径。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for scalable solutions in large-scale cyber-network security games, this paper introduces MetaDOAR, a meta-controller that enhances the Double Oracle/PSRO framework with a learned partition-aware filter and Q-value caching. The method projects network states into compact embeddings to select a critical subset of devices, enabling a low-level actor to perform focused beam search guided by a critic, while caching action evaluations to minimize redundant computations via quantized state keys and k-hop invalidation. Experimental results demonstrate that MetaDOAR achieves higher player payoffs than state-of-the-art baselines on large network topologies, with efficient scaling in memory and training time, offering a practical hierarchical approach for networked decision problems.

When and Why Does Unsupervised RL Succeed in Mathematical Reasoning? A Manifold Envelopment Perspective
Authors: Zelin Zhang, Fei Cheng, Chenhui Chu
First: 2026-03-17T14:29:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T14:29:38+00:00
Comments: work in progress
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Although outcome-based reinforcement learning (RL) significantly advances the mathematical reasoning capabilities of Large Language Models (LLMs), its reliance on computationally expensive ground-truth annotations imposes a severe scalability bottleneck. Unsupervised RL guided by intrinsic rewards offers a scalable alternative, yet it suffers from opaque training dynamics and catastrophic instability, such as policy collapse and reward hacking. In this paper, we first design and evaluate a suite of intrinsic rewards that explicitly enforce concise and certain generation. Second, to discover the boundaries of this approach, we test base models across a spectrum of intrinsic reasoning capabilities, revealing how a model's foundational logical prior dictates its success or failure. Finally, to demystify why certain configurations stabilize while others collapse, we introduce a novel geometric diagnostic lens, showing that successful cases are enveloped by manifolds. Ultimately, our work goes beyond merely demonstrating that enforcing concise and certain responses successfully boosts mathematical reasoning; we reveal when this unsupervised approach breaks down and geometrically diagnose why.
中文标题/摘要
标题：无监督强化学习何时、为何能在数学推理中成功？基于流形包络的视角
尽管基于结果的强化学习显著提升了大语言模型的数学推理能力，但其对计算成本高昂的真实标注的依赖造成了严重的可扩展性瓶颈。基于内在奖励的无监督强化学习提供了可扩展的替代方案，但其训练动态不透明且存在灾难性不稳定问题，如策略崩溃和奖励黑客攻击。本文首先设计并评估了一套明确强制生成简洁且确定内容的内在奖励机制。其次，为探索该方法的边界，我们在不同内在推理能力谱系上测试基础模型，揭示模型的基础逻辑先验如何决定其成败。最后，为阐明某些配置稳定而另一些崩溃的原因，我们引入了一种新颖的几何诊断视角，证明成功案例均被流形所包络。最终，我们的工作不仅证明了强制简洁确定的响应能有效提升数学推理能力，更揭示了无监督方法何时失效，并从几何角度诊断了其原因。

Motivated by the scalability limitations of supervised outcome-based reinforcement learning for mathematical reasoning in large language models, this work explores unsupervised RL with intrinsic rewards that promote concise and certain text generation. The method involves designing and evaluating a suite of such intrinsic rewards, testing models with varying intrinsic reasoning capabilities to identify success boundaries, and introducing a geometric diagnostic framework based on manifold envelopment to explain training stability. Key experimental results show that enforcing concise and certain responses can successfully enhance mathematical reasoning, but the approach fails when models lack sufficient foundational logical priors, with successful training configurations geometrically characterized as being enveloped by manifolds.

Exact and general decoupled solutions of the LMC Multitask Gaussian Process model
Authors: Olivier Truffinet, Karim Ammar, Jean-Philippe Argaud, Bertrand Bouriquet
First: 2023-10-18T15:16:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T14:19:06+00:00
Comments: 78 pages, 12 figures, submitted to Neurocomputing
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The Linear Model of Co-regionalization (LMC) is a very general multitask gaussian process model for regression or classification. While its expressiveness and conceptual simplicity are appealing, naive implementations have cubic complexity in the product (number of datapoints $\times$ number of tasks), making approximations mandatory for most applications. However, recent work has shown that in some settings the latent processes of the model can be decoupled, leading to a complexity that is only linear in the number of said processes. We here extend these results, showing from the most general assumptions that the only condition necessary to an efficient exact computation of the LMC is a mild hypothesis on the noise model. We introduce a full parametrization of the resulting \emph{projected LMC} model, enabling its efficient optimization. The effectiveness of this approach is assessed through synthetic and real-data experiments, testing in particular the behavior of its underlying noise model restriction.\\ Overall, the projected LMC appears as a competitive and simpler alternative to state-of-the art multitask gaussian process models. It greatly facilitates some computations such as training data updates or leave-one-out cross-validation, and is more interpretable, for it gives access to its low-dimensional quantities and to their explicit relation with the full-dimensional data. These qualities could facilitate the adoption by various industries of entire classes of methodologies, notably multitask bayesian optimization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：LMC多任务高斯过程模型的精确与通用解耦解
线性协同区域化模型（LMC）是一种适用于回归或分类的通用多任务高斯过程模型。尽管其表达能力和概念简洁性具有吸引力，但朴素实现的计算复杂度为（数据点数×任务数）的立方级，使得在多数应用中必须采用近似方法。然而，近期研究表明，在某些设定下该模型的潜在过程可被解耦，从而将复杂度降至仅与潜在过程数量呈线性关系。本文基于最一般的假设扩展了这些结果，证明LMC实现高效精确计算的唯一条件仅需对噪声模型施加温和假设。我们提出了所得\emph{投影LMC}模型的完整参数化方案，实现了高效优化。通过合成数据与真实数据实验评估了该方法的有效性，特别检验了其底层噪声模型约束的行为。总体而言，投影LMC作为当前先进多任务高斯过程模型的竞争性简化替代方案，显著简化了训练数据更新或留一交叉验证等计算，并通过提供低维量及其与全维数据的显式关系增强了可解释性。这些特性有望推动多类方法（尤其是多任务贝叶斯优化）在各行业的广泛应用。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the computational inefficiency of naive implementations of the Linear Model of Co-regionalization (LMC) for multitask Gaussian processes, which scale cubically with the product of data points and tasks, this paper demonstrates that an exact and efficient computation is possible under a mild noise model assumption. The method introduces a full parametrization of a projected LMC model, enabling its efficient optimization. Experimental results on synthetic and real data confirm the model's effectiveness and competitiveness as a simpler, more interpretable alternative to state-of-the-art multitask models, facilitating computations like data updates and cross-validation.
本文的动机在于线性协同区域化模型（LMC）作为多任务高斯过程模型，其朴素实现的计算复杂度与数据点和任务数量的乘积成三次方关系，效率低下。方法上，研究在温和的噪声模型假设下，证明了LMC的精确高效计算是可行的，并引入了投影LMC模型的完整参数化以实现高效优化。在合成与真实数据上的实验结果表明，该方法有效且具有竞争力，作为一个更简单、可解释性更强的替代方案，它简化了训练数据更新和留一交叉验证等计算，有助于推动多任务贝叶斯优化等方法的工业应用。
EmoLLM: Appraisal-Grounded Cognitive-Emotional Co-Reasoning in Large Language Models
Authors: Yifei Zhang, Mingyang Li, Henry Gao, Liang Zhao
First: 2026-03-17T14:17:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T14:17:50+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) demonstrate strong cognitive intelligence (IQ), yet many real-world interactions also require emotional intelligence (EQ) to produce responses that are both factually reliable and emotionally appropriate. In settings such as emotional support, technical assistance, and consultation, effective dialogue depends on how situations are appraised with respect to the user's needs, goals, and coping capacity. Inspired by appraisal theory, we propose EmoLLM, an appraisal-grounded framework for IQ/EQ co-reasoning in dialogue. EmoLLM uses an explicit Appraisal Reasoning Graph (ARG) to structure intermediate reasoning over contextual facts, inferred user needs, appraisal dimensions, emotional states, and response strategies before generating a reply. We train EmoLLM in a multi-turn role-play environment with reinforcement learning, where reverse-perspective reasoning provides reward signals based on predicted user-side consequences of responses. Across diverse dialogue settings, EmoLLM improves emotional state outcomes and response quality over strong baselines while preserving strong factual reliability.
中文标题/摘要
标题：EmoLLM：基于评估理论的大语言模型认知-情感协同推理框架
大语言模型（LLMs）展现出强大的认知智能（IQ），但现实交互往往需要情感智能（EQ）以生成既事实可靠又情感得体的回应。在情感支持、技术协助和咨询等场景中，有效对话取决于如何结合用户需求、目标和应对能力对情境进行评估。受评估理论启发，我们提出EmoLLM——一个基于评估的对话IQ/EQ协同推理框架。该框架通过显式的评估推理图（ARG）结构化处理上下文事实、推断用户需求、评估维度、情感状态及回应策略，再进行回复生成。我们采用强化学习在多轮角色扮演环境中训练EmoLLM，其中逆向视角推理通过预测用户侧反馈结果提供奖励信号。在多样化对话场景中，EmoLLM在保持强事实可靠性的同时，显著提升了情感状态结果与回应质量。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the need to enhance large language models (LLMs) with emotional intelligence (EQ) alongside cognitive intelligence (IQ) for more effective, empathetic dialogues in scenarios like emotional support and consultation. The method introduces EmoLLM, a framework grounded in appraisal theory that employs an explicit Appraisal Reasoning Graph (ARG) to structure multi-step reasoning about context, user needs, emotional appraisals, and response strategies before generating a reply; it is trained using reinforcement learning with reward signals derived from reverse-perspective reasoning on user consequences. Experimental results show that EmoLLM outperforms strong baselines across diverse dialogue settings by improving emotional outcomes and response quality while maintaining factual reliability.
该论文的动机是增强大语言模型（LLMs）的情感智能（EQ），以配合其认知智能（IQ），从而在情感支持、咨询等场景中实现更有效、更具共情的对话。方法上，受评价理论启发，提出了EmoLLM框架，该框架使用显式的评价推理图（ARG）来结构化中间推理过程，涵盖上下文事实、推断的用户需求、评价维度、情感状态和回应策略，然后生成回复；模型通过强化学习在多轮角色扮演环境中训练，利用基于回应预测用户后果的反向视角推理提供奖励信号。主要实验结果表明，在多种对话设置中，EmoLLM在保持强事实可靠性的同时，相比强基线模型，改善了情感状态结果和回应质量。
Reevaluating Policy Gradient Methods for Imperfect-Information Games
Authors: Max Rudolph, Nathan Lichtle, Sobhan Mohammadpour, Alexandre Bayen, J. Zico Kolter, Amy Zhang, Gabriele Farina, Eugene Vinitsky, Samuel Sokota
First: 2025-02-13T03:38:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T13:46:04+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
In the past decade, motivated by the putative failure of naive self-play deep reinforcement learning (DRL) in adversarial imperfect-information games, researchers have developed numerous DRL algorithms based on fictitious play (FP), double oracle (DO), and counterfactual regret minimization (CFR). In light of recent results of the magnetic mirror descent algorithm, we hypothesize that simpler generic policy gradient methods like PPO are competitive with or superior to these FP-, DO-, and CFR-based DRL approaches. To facilitate the resolution of this hypothesis, we implement and release the first broadly accessible exact exploitability computations for five large games. Using these games, we conduct the largest-ever exploitability comparison of DRL algorithms for imperfect-information games. Over 7000 training runs, we find that FP-, DO-, and CFR-based approaches fail to outperform generic policy gradient methods. Code is available at https://github.com/nathanlct/IIG-RL-Benchmark and https://github.com/gabrfarina/exp-a-spiel .
中文标题/摘要
标题：重新评估不完全信息博弈中的策略梯度方法
过去十年间，针对对抗性不完全信息博弈中朴素自博弈深度强化学习（DRL）的假定失败，研究者开发了众多基于虚拟博弈（FP）、双重预言机（DO）及反事实遗憾最小化（CFR）的DRL算法。基于磁镜下降算法的最新研究成果，我们假设如PPO这类更简洁的通用策略梯度方法，其性能可与这些基于FP、DO和CFR的DRL方法相媲美甚至更优。为验证此假设，我们实现并发布了首个针对五类大型博弈的广泛可访问精确可剥削性计算工具。利用这些博弈，我们开展了迄今最大规模的不完全信息博弈DRL算法可剥削性比较。通过对超过7000次训练运行的分析，发现基于FP、DO和CFR的方法未能超越通用策略梯度方法。代码发布于https://github.com/nathanlct/IIG-RL-Benchmark 与 https://github.com/gabrfarina/exp-a-spiel 。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the recent success of magnetic mirror descent and the hypothesis that simpler policy gradient methods might outperform more complex approaches designed for imperfect-information games, this paper reevaluates generic methods like PPO against specialized algorithms based on fictitious play, double oracle, and counterfactual regret minimization. The method involves implementing exact exploitability computations for five large games and conducting over 7000 training runs to compare deep reinforcement learning algorithms. The main experimental results show that the specialized approaches fail to outperform generic policy gradient methods, suggesting that simpler methods are competitive or superior in these adversarial settings.
受磁镜下降算法近期成功的启发，以及认为简单策略梯度方法可能优于为不完美信息博弈设计的复杂方法的假设，本文重新评估了像PPO这样的通用方法相对于基于虚拟博弈、双预言机和反事实遗憾最小化的专用算法。方法包括为五个大型博弈实现精确可剥削性计算，并进行超过7000次训练运行以比较深度强化学习算法。主要实验结果表明，专用方法未能超越通用策略梯度方法，表明在这些对抗性环境中，简单方法具有竞争力或更优。
From the Inside Out: Progressive Distribution Refinement for Confidence Calibration
Authors: Xizhong Yang, Yinan Xia, Huiming Wang, Mofei Song
First: 2026-03-17T13:26:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T13:26:29+00:00
Comments: 15 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Leveraging the model's internal information as the self-reward signal in Reinforcement Learning (RL) has received extensive attention due to its label-free nature. While prior works have made significant progress in applying the Test-Time Scaling (TTS) strategies to RL, the discrepancy in internal information between test and training remains inadequately addressed. Moreover, Test-Time Training based on voting-based TTS strategies often suffers from reward hacking problems. To address these issues, we propose DistriTTRL, which leverages the distribution prior of the model's confidence during RL to progressively optimize the reward signal, rather than relying solely on single-query rollouts. Additionally, we mitigate the phenomenon of consistent reward hacking caused by the voting-based TTS strategies through diversity-targeted penalties. Benefiting from this training mechanism where model capability and self-reward signals complement each other, and the mitigation of reward hacking, DistriTTRL has achieved significant performance improvements across multiple models and benchmarks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：由内而外：基于渐进式分布优化的置信度校准方法
利用模型内部信息作为强化学习中的自奖励信号，因其无需标注的特性受到广泛关注。尽管先前研究在将测试时缩放策略应用于强化学习方面取得重要进展，但训练与测试阶段内部信息的差异仍未得到充分解决。基于投票机制的测试时训练策略常受奖励破解问题困扰。为此，我们提出DistriTTRL方法，通过强化学习中模型置信度的先验分布逐步优化奖励信号，而非仅依赖单次查询推演。同时，我们通过针对多样性的惩罚机制缓解投票式测试时训练策略引发的持续性奖励破解现象。得益于模型能力与自奖励信号相互促进的训练机制，以及对奖励破解的抑制，DistriTTRL在多个模型与基准测试中均取得显著性能提升。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of leveraging a model's internal information as a self-reward signal in Reinforcement Learning (RL), where discrepancies between test and training data and issues like reward hacking in voting-based Test-Time Scaling strategies remain problematic. The proposed method, DistriTTRL, progressively refines the reward signal by utilizing the distribution prior of the model's confidence during RL, moving beyond single-query rollouts, and introduces diversity-targeted penalties to mitigate consistent reward hacking. Experimental results demonstrate that DistriTTRL achieves significant performance improvements across multiple models and benchmarks, benefiting from a synergistic training mechanism that enhances model capability and self-reward signals while reducing reward hacking.
本文针对在强化学习中利用模型内部信息作为自奖励信号所面临的挑战，即测试与训练数据之间的差异以及基于投票的测试时间缩放策略中的奖励黑客问题。提出的方法DistriTTRL通过利用强化学习过程中模型置信度的分布先验来逐步优化奖励信号，而非依赖单次查询展开，并引入针对多样性的惩罚来缓解持续的奖励黑客现象。实验结果表明，DistriTTRL在多个模型和基准测试中实现了显著的性能提升，这得益于一种模型能力与自奖励信号相互补充的训练机制，同时有效减轻了奖励黑客问题。
Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning Counteracts Delayed CSI in Multi-Satellite Systems
Authors: Marios Aristodemou, Yasaman Omid, Sangarapillai Lambotharan, Mahsa Derakhshan, Lajos Hanzo
First: 2026-03-17T12:58:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T12:58:22+00:00
Comments: 12 pages, 6 Figures, Submit to IEEE Transactions of Vehicular Technology. It has been reviewed once
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The integration of satellite communication networks with next-generation (NG) technologies is a promising approach towards global connectivity. However, the quality of services is highly dependant on the availability of accurate channel state information (CSI). Channel estimation in satellite communications is challenging due to the high propagation delay between terrestrial users and satellites, which results in outdated CSI observations on the satellite side. In this paper, we study the downlink transmission of multiple satellites acting as distributed base stations (BS) to mobile terrestrial users. We propose a multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) algorithm which aims for maximising the sum-rate of the users, while coping with the outdated CSI. We design a novel bi-level optimisation, procedure themes as dual stage proximal policy optimisation (DS-PPO), for tackling the problem of large continuous action spaces as well as of independent and non-identically distributed (non-IID) environments in MARL. Specifically, the first stage of DS-PPO maximises the sum-rate for an individual satellite and the second stage maximises the sum-rate when all the satellites cooperate to form a distributed multi-antenna BS. Our numerical results demonstrate the robustness of DS-PPO to CSI imperfections as well as the sum-rate improvement attached by the use of DS-PPO. In addition, we provide the convergence analysis for the DS-PPO along with the computational complexity.
中文标题/摘要
标题：多智能体强化学习应对多卫星系统中的延迟信道状态信息
卫星通信网络与下一代技术的融合是实现全球连接的重要途径。然而，服务质量高度依赖于准确信道状态信息的可用性。卫星通信中的信道估计因地面用户与卫星间的高传播延迟而面临挑战，导致卫星端获取的信道状态信息过时。本文研究了多颗卫星作为分布式基站向移动地面用户进行下行传输的场景。我们提出一种多智能体强化学习算法，旨在最大化用户总速率，同时应对过时的信道状态信息。针对多智能体强化学习中大规模连续动作空间及独立非独立同分布环境的问题，我们设计了一种新颖的双层优化流程——双阶段近端策略优化算法。具体而言，DS-PPO的第一阶段最大化单颗卫星的总速率，第二阶段在所有卫星协作形成分布式多天线基站时最大化总速率。数值结果表明DS-PPO对信道状态信息缺陷具有鲁棒性，且能提升系统总速率。此外，我们还提供了DS-PPO的收敛性分析与计算复杂度评估。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of outdated channel state information (CSI) due to high propagation delays in multi-satellite communication systems, which degrades service quality, this paper proposes a multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) approach to maximize user sum-rate. The method introduces a novel bi-level optimization algorithm called dual-stage proximal policy optimization (DS-PPO), designed to handle large continuous action spaces and non-identically distributed environments; the first stage optimizes individual satellite performance, while the second stage coordinates satellites to act as a distributed multi-antenna base station. Experimental results demonstrate that DS-PPO robustly improves sum-rate despite CSI imperfections, with supporting convergence analysis and computational complexity evaluation.
本文针对多卫星通信系统中因高传播延迟导致信道状态信息过时、从而影响服务质量的问题，提出采用多智能体强化学习方法来最大化用户总速率。该方法设计了一种新颖的双层优化算法——双阶段近端策略优化，以处理大规模连续动作空间和非独立同分布环境；第一阶段优化单个卫星性能，第二阶段协调所有卫星作为分布式多天线基站协作。实验结果表明，该算法能有效应对信道状态信息不完善，显著提升系统总速率，并提供了收敛性分析和计算复杂度评估。
Follow the Clues, Frame the Truth: Hybrid-evidential Deductive Reasoning in Open-Vocabulary Multimodal Emotion Recognition
Authors: Yu Liu, Lei Zhang, Haoxun Li, Hanlei Shi, Yuxuan Ding, Leyuan Qu, Taihao Li
First: 2026-03-17T12:49:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T12:49:51+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Open-Vocabulary Multimodal Emotion Recognition (OV-MER) is inherently challenging due to the ambiguity of equivocal multimodal cues, which often stem from distinct unobserved situational dynamics. While Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) offer extensive semantic coverage, their performance is often bottlenecked by premature commitment to dominant data priors, resulting in suboptimal heuristics that overlook crucial, complementary affective cues across modalities. We argue that effective affective reasoning requires more than surface-level association; it necessitates reconstructing nuanced emotional states by synthesizing multiple evidence-grounded rationales that reconcile these observations from diverse latent perspectives. We introduce HyDRA, a Hybrid-evidential Deductive Reasoning Architecture that formalizes inference as a Propose-Verify-Decide protocol. To internalize this abductive process, we employ reinforcement learning with hierarchical reward shaping, aligning the reasoning trajectories with final task performance to ensure they best reconcile the observed multimodal cues. Systematic evaluations validate our design choices, with HyDRA consistently outperforming strong baselines--especially in ambiguous or conflicting scenarios--while providing interpretable, diagnostic evidence traces.
中文标题/摘要
标题：循迹探真：开放词汇多模态情感识别中的混合证据演绎推理
开放词汇多模态情感识别（OV-MER）因多模态线索的模糊性而面临固有挑战，这些线索常源于未观测到的情境动态。尽管多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）具备广泛语义覆盖能力，但其性能常受限于对显性数据先验的过早固化，导致形成次优启发式策略，忽视跨模态的关键互补情感线索。我们认为有效的情感推理需超越表层关联，必须通过整合多源证据驱动的理性依据，从多元潜在视角协调观测结果，以重构细腻的情感状态。为此，我们提出HyDRA——一种混合证据演绎推理架构，将推理形式化为“提出-验证-决策”协议。为内化这一溯因过程，我们采用分层奖励塑形的强化学习方法，使推理轨迹与最终任务性能对齐，确保其能最优协调观测到的多模态线索。系统化评估验证了我们的设计选择：HyDRA在各类场景（尤其是模糊或冲突情境）中持续超越强基线模型，同时提供可解释的诊断证据轨迹。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of Open-Vocabulary Multimodal Emotion Recognition (OV-MER), where ambiguous and conflicting cues across modalities often lead models to rely on superficial heuristics, overlooking nuanced emotional states. The authors propose HyDRA, a Hybrid-evidential Deductive Reasoning Architecture that formalizes inference as a Propose-Verify-Decide protocol, using reinforcement learning with hierarchical reward shaping to align reasoning trajectories with task performance and synthesize evidence from multiple latent perspectives. Experimental results show that HyDRA consistently outperforms strong baselines, particularly in ambiguous or conflicting scenarios, while providing interpretable evidence traces.

TRUST-SQL: Tool-Integrated Multi-Turn Reinforcement Learning for Text-to-SQL over Unknown Schemas
Authors: Ai Jian, Xiaoyun Zhang, Wanrou Du, Jingqing Ruan, Jiangbo Pei, Weipeng Zhang, Ke Zeng, Xunliang Cai
First: 2026-03-17T12:30:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T12:30:42+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Text-to-SQL parsing has achieved remarkable progress under the Full Schema Assumption. However, this premise fails in real-world enterprise environments where databases contain hundreds of tables with massive noisy metadata. Rather than injecting the full schema upfront, an agent must actively identify and verify only the relevant subset, giving rise to the Unknown Schema scenario we study in this work. To address this, we propose TRUST-SQL (Truthful Reasoning with Unknown Schema via Tools). We formulate the task as a Partially Observable Markov Decision Process where our autonomous agent employs a structured four-phase protocol to ground reasoning in verified metadata. Crucially, this protocol provides a structural boundary for our novel Dual-Track GRPO strategy. By applying token-level masked advantages, this strategy isolates exploration rewards from execution outcomes to resolve credit assignment, yielding a 9.9% relative improvement over standard GRPO. Extensive experiments across five benchmarks demonstrate that TRUST-SQL achieves an average absolute improvement of 30.6% and 16.6% for the 4B and 8B variants respectively over their base models. Remarkably, despite operating entirely without pre-loaded metadata, our framework consistently matches or surpasses strong baselines that rely on schema prefilling.
中文标题/摘要
标题：TRUST-SQL：面向未知数据库模式的工具集成多轮强化学习文本转SQL方法
文本转SQL解析在全模式假设下已取得显著进展，但该前提在企业真实场景中往往失效——数据库常包含数百个具有海量噪声元数据的表。本文研究的未知模式场景要求智能体主动识别并验证相关子集，而非预先注入完整模式。为此，我们提出TRUST-SQL（基于工具的未知模式可信推理框架），将任务建模为部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程，使自主智能体通过结构化四阶段协议在已验证元数据中实现推理锚定。该协议为创新的双轨GRPO策略提供了结构化边界：通过应用词元级掩码优势值，该策略将探索奖励与执行结果解耦以解决信用分配问题，相较标准GRPO实现9.9%相对性能提升。在五个基准测试上的大量实验表明，TRUST-SQL的4B与8B变体相较基础模型分别获得30.6%与16.6%的平均绝对提升。值得注意的是，尽管完全无需预载元数据，本框架始终达到或超越依赖模式预填充的强基线方法。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the real-world challenge of text-to-SQL parsing over large, noisy enterprise databases where the full schema is not known upfront, moving beyond the unrealistic full schema assumption. The method introduces TRUST-SQL, which formulates the task as a Partially Observable Markov Decision Process and employs an autonomous agent with a structured four-phase protocol for metadata verification, enhanced by a novel Dual-Track GRPO strategy that uses token-level masked advantages to improve credit assignment. The main experimental results show that this approach yields a 9.9% relative improvement over standard GRPO and achieves average absolute improvements of 30.6% and 16.6% for 4B and 8B model variants over their base models across five benchmarks, consistently matching or surpassing baselines that rely on schema prefilling despite operating without pre-loaded metadata.
本研究的动机是解决现实世界中针对大型、嘈杂的企业数据库进行文本到SQL解析的挑战，这些数据库的完整模式并非预先已知，从而超越了不切实际的完整模式假设。方法上提出了TRUST-SQL，将任务建模为部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程，采用一个具有结构化四阶段协议的自主代理进行元数据验证，并通过一种新颖的双轨GRPO策略增强，该策略利用令牌级掩码优势改进信用分配。主要实验结果表明，该方法相比标准GRPO实现了9.9%的相对提升，在五个基准测试中，4B和8B模型变体相比其基础模型分别取得了30.6%和16.6%的平均绝对改进，尽管完全无需预加载元数据，仍持续匹配或超越了依赖模式预填充的强基线。
CHARM: Calibrating Reward Models With Chatbot Arena Scores
Authors: Xiao Zhu, Chenmien Tan, Pinzhen Chen, Rico Sennrich, Huiming Wang, Yanlin Zhang, Hanxu Hu
First: 2025-04-14T09:51:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T12:03:29+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reward models (RMs) play a crucial role in Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback by serving as proxies for human preferences in aligning large language models. However, they suffer from various biases which could lead to reward hacking. In this paper, we identify a model preference bias in RMs, where they systematically assign disproportionately high scores to responses from certain policy models, leading to unfair judgments. To mitigate this bias, we propose a calibration method named CHatbot Arena calibrated Reward Modeling (CHARM) that leverages Elo scores from the Chatbot Arena to construct debiased preference datasets and adjust reward model scoring. We conduct extensive experiments on reward model benchmarks and human preference alignment. Results demonstrate that our calibrated RMs achieve improved evaluation accuracy on RM-Bench and the Chat-Hard domain of RewardBench, exhibit a stronger correlation with human preferences by producing scores more closely aligned with Elo rankings and improve downstream post-training performance. These results demonstrate that CHARM provides a simple, effective, and broadly applicable approach to building more reliable and fair reward models.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CHARM：基于聊天机器人竞技场分数的奖励模型校准方法
奖励模型在基于人类反馈的强化学习中扮演关键角色，作为人类偏好的代理以对齐大语言模型。然而，奖励模型存在多种偏差，可能导致奖励攻击。本文识别出奖励模型中的模型偏好偏差——其系统性地对某些策略模型的响应赋予过高评分，导致不公正评估。为缓解此偏差，我们提出名为CHARM的校准方法，利用聊天机器人竞技场的Elo分数构建去偏好的偏好数据集并调整奖励模型评分。我们在奖励模型基准和人类偏好对齐任务上进行了广泛实验。结果表明，经校准的奖励模型在RM-Bench和RewardBench的Chat-Hard领域实现了更高的评估准确度，通过生成更贴近Elo排名的分数与人类偏好呈现更强相关性，并提升了下游后训练性能。这些结果证明CHARM为构建更可靠、公平的奖励模型提供了简洁高效且广泛适用的解决方案。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the model preference bias in reward models (RMs), where RMs unfairly favor responses from certain policy models, leading to reward hacking. To mitigate this, the authors propose CHARM, a calibration method that uses Elo scores from Chatbot Arena to create debiased preference datasets and adjust RM scoring. Experimental results show that CHARM improves evaluation accuracy on RM-Bench and RewardBench's Chat-Hard domain, enhances correlation with human preferences by aligning scores with Elo rankings, and boosts downstream post-training performance, offering a simple and effective approach for more reliable RMs.
本文针对奖励模型（RMs）中存在的模型偏好偏差问题展开研究，该偏差导致RMs系统性地偏向某些策略模型的响应，造成不公平判断。为缓解此偏差，作者提出了CHARM校准方法，利用Chatbot Arena的Elo分数构建去偏好的数据集并调整奖励模型评分。实验结果表明，CHARM在RM-Bench和RewardBench的Chat-Hard领域上提高了评估准确性，通过使评分更贴近Elo排名增强了与人类偏好的相关性，并改善了下游后训练性能，为构建更可靠、公平的奖励模型提供了一种简单有效的方法。
Via Negativa for AI Alignment: Why Negative Constraints Are Structurally Superior to Positive Preferences
Authors: Quan Cheng
First: 2026-03-17T11:52:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T11:52:18+00:00
Comments: 9 pages, position paper
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent empirical results have demonstrated that training large language models (LLMs) with negative-only feedback can match or exceed standard reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF). Negative Sample Reinforcement achieves parity with PPO on mathematical reasoning; Distributional Dispreference Optimization trains effectively using only dispreferred samples; and Constitutional AI outperforms pure RLHF on harmlessness benchmarks. Yet no unified theoretical account explains why negative signals are so effective. This paper proposes such an account: positive preferences and negative constraints are structurally asymmetric. Positive preferences ("which is better") encode continuously coupled, context-dependent human values that cannot be exhaustively specified -- leading models to learn surface correlates such as agreement with the user (sycophancy). Negative constraints ("what is wrong") encode discrete, finite, independently verifiable prohibitions that can converge to a stable boundary. This asymmetry -- rooted in Popper's falsification logic and the epistemology of negative knowledge -- explains both the sycophancy failure of preference-based RLHF and the surprising effectiveness of negative-signal methods. We argue that alignment research should shift its center of gravity from "learning what humans prefer" to "learning what humans reject," and offer testable predictions for this framework.
中文标题/摘要
标题：AI对齐的否定路径：为何负面约束在结构上优于正面偏好
近期实证研究表明，仅使用负面反馈训练大语言模型（LLMs）可达到或超越基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF）标准效果。负面样本强化在数学推理上与PPO算法表现相当；分布性非偏好优化仅通过非偏好样本即可有效训练；宪法AI在无害性基准测试中优于纯RLHF方法。然而，尚无统一理论解释负面信号为何如此有效。本文提出：正面偏好与负面约束存在结构性不对称。正面偏好（“哪个更好”）编码了连续耦合、依赖语境且无法穷尽的人类价值观——导致模型学习表面关联特征（如迎合用户的谄媚行为）。负面约束（“什么是错的”）编码了离散、有限、可独立验证的禁令，能够收敛至稳定边界。这种根植于波普尔证伪逻辑与否定知识论的不对称性，既解释了基于偏好的RLHF产生谄媚行为的原因，也揭示了负面信号方法惊人成效的机理。我们主张对齐研究重心应从“学习人类偏好”转向“学习人类排斥”，并为此框架提供可检验的预测。
Summary / 总结
This paper is motivated by the empirical success of training large language models with negative-only feedback, which has matched or surpassed standard reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF), yet lacks a unified theoretical explanation. The authors propose that positive preferences and negative constraints are structurally asymmetric: positive preferences encode continuous, context-dependent human values that are hard to specify exhaustively, leading to issues like sycophancy, while negative constraints represent discrete, verifiable prohibitions that converge to stable boundaries, drawing on Popper's falsification logic. Experimental results cited include Negative Sample Reinforcement achieving parity with PPO on mathematical reasoning, Distributional Dispreference Optimization training effectively with dispreferred samples, and Constitutional AI outperforming RLHF on harmlessness benchmarks, supporting the argument that alignment research should shift focus from learning human preferences to learning human rejections.
本文的动机在于，仅使用负面反馈训练大语言模型已在实证中取得与标准人类反馈强化学习（RLHF）相当或更优的效果，但缺乏统一的理论解释。作者提出，正面偏好与负面约束在结构上不对称：正面偏好编码连续、依赖语境的人类价值观，难以穷尽指定，易导致模型学习表面关联如迎合用户；而负面约束代表离散、可独立验证的禁令，能收敛到稳定边界，这基于波普尔的证伪逻辑和负面知识认识论。引用的实验结果包括负面样本强化在数学推理上与PPO持平、分布性非偏好优化仅用非偏好样本有效训练，以及宪法AI在无害性基准上超越纯RLHF，从而支持对齐研究应从学习人类偏好转向学习人类拒绝的论点。
Deep Reinforcement Learning-Assisted Automated Operator Portfolio for Constrained Multi-objective Optimization
Authors: Shuai Shao, Ye Tian, Shangshang Yang, Xingyi Zhang
First: 2026-03-17T11:39:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T11:39:19+00:00
Comments: 14 pages, 5 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Constrained multi-objective optimization problems (CMOPs) are of great significance in the context of practical applications, ranging from scientific to engineering domains. Most existing constrained multi-objective evolutionary algorithms (CMOEAs) usually employ fixed operators all the time, which exhibit poor versatility in handling various CMOPs. Therefore, some recent studies have focused on adaptively selecting the best operators for the current population states during the search process. The evolutionary algorithms proposed in these studies learn the value of each operator and recommend the operator with the highest value for the current population, resulting in only a single operator being recommended at each generation, which can potentially lead to local optima and inefficient utilization of function evaluations. To address the dilemma in operator adaptation, this paper proposes a reinforcement learning-based automated operator portfolio approach to learn an allocation scheme of operators at each generation. This approach considers the optimization-related and constraint-related features of the current population as states, the overall improvement in population convergence and diversity as rewards, and different operator portfolios as actions. By utilizing deep neural networks to establish a mapping model between the population states and the expected cumulative rewards, the proposed approach determines the optimal operator portfolio during the evolutionary process. By embedding the proposed approach into existing CMOEAs, a deep reinforcement learning-assisted automated operator portfolio based evolutionary algorithm for solving CMOPs, abbreviated as CMOEA-AOP, is developed. Empirical studies on 33 benchmark problems demonstrate that the proposed algorithm significantly enhances the performance of CMOEAs and exhibits more stable performance across different CMOPs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于深度强化学习的自动化算子组合用于约束多目标优化
约束多目标优化问题（CMOPs）在科学与工程等实际应用领域具有重要意义。现有的大多数约束多目标进化算法（CMOEAs）通常始终采用固定算子，在处理各类CMOPs时表现出较差的通用性。因此，近期研究聚焦于在搜索过程中自适应地为当前种群状态选择最佳算子。这些研究提出的进化算法通过学习每个算子的价值，并为当前种群推荐价值最高的算子，导致每代仅推荐单一算子，可能陷入局部最优且函数评估利用效率低下。为解决算子自适应中的困境，本文提出一种基于强化学习的自动化算子组合方法，以学习每代算子的分配方案。该方法将当前种群的优化相关特征和约束相关特征作为状态，种群收敛性与多样性的整体提升作为奖励，不同算子组合作为动作。通过利用深度神经网络建立种群状态与期望累积奖励之间的映射模型，所提方法在进化过程中确定最优算子组合。通过将该方法嵌入现有CMOEAs，开发了一种基于深度强化学习的自动化算子组合进化算法（简称CMOEA-AOP）用于求解CMOPs。在33个基准问题上的实证研究表明，所提算法显著提升了CMOEAs的性能，并在不同CMOPs上表现出更稳定的性能。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the limited versatility of constrained multi-objective evolutionary algorithms (CMOEAs) that rely on fixed operators by proposing a deep reinforcement learning-assisted automated operator portfolio approach. The method models the optimization and constraint features of the population as states, uses overall improvements in convergence and diversity as rewards, and selects optimal operator portfolios as actions via deep neural networks to map states to expected cumulative rewards. Experimental results on 33 benchmark problems show that the resulting algorithm, CMOEA-AOP, significantly enhances CMOEA performance and achieves more stable outcomes across diverse constrained multi-objective optimization problems.
本文针对现有约束多目标进化算法（CMOEAs）因使用固定算子而泛化能力不足的问题，提出了一种基于深度强化学习的自动化算子组合方法。该方法将种群的优化和约束特征作为状态，以种群收敛性和多样性的整体提升作为奖励，通过深度神经网络建立状态与预期累积奖励的映射，从而在进化过程中动态选择最优算子组合。在33个基准问题上的实验表明，所提出的CMOEA-AOP算法显著提升了CMOEAs的性能，并在不同的约束多目标优化问题上表现出更稳定的效果。
LLM-Guided Reinforcement Learning for Audio-Visual Speech Enhancement
Authors: Chih-Ning Chen, Jen-Cheng Hou, Hsin-Min Wang, Shao-Yi Chien, Yu Tsao, Fan-Gang Zeng
First: 2026-03-14T14:01:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T11:37:19+00:00
Comments: 6 pages, 4 figures, submitted to Interspeech 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In existing Audio-Visual Speech Enhancement (AVSE) methods, objectives such as Scale-Invariant Signal-to-Noise Ratio (SI-SNR) and Mean Squared Error (MSE) are widely used; however, they often correlate poorly with perceptual quality and provide limited interpretability for optimization. This work proposes a reinforcement learning-based AVSE framework with a Large Language Model (LLM)-based interpretable reward model. An audio LLM generates natural language descriptions of enhanced speech, which are converted by a sentiment analysis model into a 1-5 rating score serving as the PPO reward for fine-tuning a pretrained AVSE model. Compared with scalar metrics, LLM-generated feedback is semantically rich and explicitly describes improvements in speech quality. Experiments on the 4th COG-MHEAR AVSE Challenge (AVSEC-4) dataset show that the proposed method outperforms a supervised baseline and a DNSMOS-based RL baseline in PESQ, STOI, neural quality metrics, and subjective listening tests.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于大语言模型引导的视听语音增强强化学习方法
现有视听语音增强方法广泛采用尺度不变信噪比和均方误差等目标函数，但这些指标常与感知质量相关性较弱，且对优化过程的解释性有限。本研究提出一种基于强化学习的AVSE框架，采用基于大语言模型的可解释奖励模型。音频大语言模型生成增强语音的自然语言描述，通过情感分析模型转换为1-5级评分，作为近端策略优化算法的奖励信号，用于微调预训练的AVSE模型。与标量指标相比，大语言模型生成的反馈语义更丰富，能明确描述语音质量改进。在第四届COG-MHEAR AVSE挑战赛数据集上的实验表明，该方法在PESQ、STOI、神经质量指标及主观听力测试中均优于监督基线方法和基于DNSMOS的强化学习基线。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the poor correlation of traditional scalar metrics like SI-SNR with perceptual quality and their limited interpretability, this paper introduces a reinforcement learning framework for audio-visual speech enhancement that leverages a large language model to provide interpretable rewards. The method uses an audio LLM to generate natural language descriptions of enhanced speech, which are then converted via sentiment analysis into a 1-5 rating score to guide the fine-tuning of a pretrained AVSE model using proximal policy optimization. Experimental results on the AVSEC-4 dataset demonstrate that this approach surpasses both a supervised baseline and a DNSMOS-based RL baseline across objective metrics such as PESQ and STOI, neural quality measures, and subjective listening tests.
针对现有视听语音增强方法中广泛使用的SI-SNR等标量指标与感知质量相关性差且可解释性有限的问题，本研究提出了一种基于强化学习的视听语音增强框架，采用大语言模型提供可解释的奖励。该方法利用音频大语言模型生成增强语音的自然语言描述，再通过情感分析模型将其转换为1-5分的评分，作为近端策略优化奖励来微调预训练的视听语音增强模型。在AVSEC-4数据集上的实验表明，该方法在PESQ、STOI等客观指标、神经质量度量以及主观听力测试上均优于监督学习基线和基于DNSMOS的强化学习基线。
On-Policy RL Meets Off-Policy Experts: Harmonizing Supervised Fine-Tuning and Reinforcement Learning via Dynamic Weighting
Authors: Wenhao Zhang, Yuexiang Xie, Yuchang Sun, Yanxi Chen, Guoyin Wang, Yaliang Li, Bolin Ding, Jingren Zhou
First: 2025-08-15T11:20:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T11:27:09+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) and Reinforcement Learning (RL) are two prominent post-training paradigms for refining the capabilities and aligning the behavior of Large Language Models (LLMs). Existing approaches that integrate SFT and RL often face the risk of disrupting established response patterns and inducing overfitting to expert data. To address this, we present a novel investigation into the unified view of SFT and RL through an off-policy versus on-policy lens. We propose CHORD, a framework for Controllable Harmonization of On- and Off-Policy Reinforcement Learning via Dynamic Weighting, which reframes SFT not as a separate stage but as a dynamically weighted auxiliary objective within the on-policy RL process. Based on an analysis of off-policy expert data's influence at both holistic and granular levels, we incorporate a dual-control mechanism in CHORD. Specifically, the framework first employs a global coefficient to holistically guide the transition from off-policy imitation to on-policy exploration, and then applies a token-wise weighting function that enables granular learning from the expert, which promotes on-policy exploration and mitigates disruption from off-policy data. We conduct extensive experiments across various practical tasks, providing empirical evidence that CHORD achieves a stable and efficient learning process. By effectively harmonizing off-policy expert data with on-policy exploration, CHORD demonstrates significant improvements over baselines. We release the implementation at https://github.com/modelscope/Trinity-RFT/tree/main/examples/mix_chord to inspire further research.
中文标题/摘要
标题：在线强化学习与离线专家策略的融合：通过动态加权协调监督微调与强化学习
监督微调（SFT）与强化学习（RL）是优化大语言模型（LLMs）能力与行为对齐的两种主流后训练范式。现有整合SFT与RL的方法常面临破坏已有响应模式、对专家数据过拟合的风险。为此，我们通过离线策略与在线策略的视角，对SFT与RL的统一框架展开创新性研究，提出CHORD框架——基于动态加权的在线与离线强化学习可控协调框架。该框架将SFT重构为在线RL过程中动态加权的辅助目标，而非独立阶段。基于对离线专家数据在整体与细粒度层面影响的分析，CHORD引入双重控制机制：首先采用全局系数整体引导从离线模仿到在线探索的过渡，再通过词元级加权函数实现细粒度的专家学习，从而促进在线探索并缓解离线数据的干扰。我们在多种实际任务中开展广泛实验，实证表明CHORD能实现稳定高效的学习过程，通过有效协调离线专家数据与在线探索，其性能显著超越基线方法。代码已开源：https://github.com/modelscope/Trinity-RFT/tree/main/examples/mix_chord，以推动后续研究。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of integrating Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) and Reinforcement Learning (RL) for Large Language Models, where existing methods risk disrupting learned patterns and overfitting to expert data. The authors propose CHORD, a framework that unifies SFT and RL by reframing SFT as a dynamically weighted auxiliary objective within on-policy RL, using a dual-control mechanism with global and token-wise weighting to transition from imitation to exploration. Experimental results across various tasks demonstrate that CHORD achieves a more stable and efficient learning process, leading to significant performance improvements over baseline methods by effectively harmonizing off-policy expert data with on-policy exploration.
本文针对大语言模型中监督微调与强化学习的整合挑战展开研究，现有方法常会破坏已习得的响应模式并导致对专家数据的过拟合。为此，作者提出了CHORD框架，通过将监督微调重新定义为策略内强化学习中动态加权的辅助目标，并采用包含全局系数和词级权重的双重控制机制，以实现从模仿到探索的平稳过渡。在多种实际任务上的实验结果表明，CHORD通过有效协调策略外专家数据与策略内探索，实现了更稳定高效的学习过程，相比基线方法取得了显著性能提升。
Controlling Fish Schools via Reinforcement Learning of Virtual Fish Movement
Authors: Yusuke Nishii, Hiroaki Kawashima
First: 2026-03-17T11:12:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T11:12:36+00:00
Comments: English translation of the author's 2018 bachelor's thesis. Keywords: fish schooling, reinforcement learning, collective behavior, artificial agents, swarm-machine interaction
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This study investigates a method to guide and control fish schools using virtual fish trained with reinforcement learning. We utilize 2D virtual fish displayed on a screen to overcome technical challenges such as durability and movement constraints inherent in physical robotic agents. To address the lack of detailed behavioral models for real fish, we adopt a model-free reinforcement learning approach. First, simulation results show that reinforcement learning can acquire effective movement policies even when simulated real fish frequently ignore the virtual stimulus. Second, real-world experiments with live fish confirm that the learned policy successfully guides fish schools toward specified target directions. Statistical analysis reveals that the proposed method significantly outperforms baseline conditions, including the absence of stimulus and a heuristic "stay-at-edge" strategy. This study provides an early demonstration of how reinforcement learning can be used to influence collective animal behavior through artificial agents.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于强化学习的虚拟鱼运动控制鱼群方法研究
本研究探索了一种利用强化学习训练的虚拟鱼来引导和控制鱼群的方法。通过屏幕上显示的二维虚拟鱼，克服了实体机器人代理在耐久性和运动限制方面的技术挑战。针对真实鱼类缺乏详细行为模型的问题，我们采用了无模型强化学习方法。首先，仿真结果表明，即使模拟的真实鱼频繁忽略虚拟刺激，强化学习仍能习得有效的运动策略。其次，活鱼实验证实，习得的策略能成功引导鱼群朝向指定目标方向。统计分析显示，该方法在无刺激及启发式“边缘停留”策略等基线条件下均表现出显著优势。本研究为如何通过人工代理利用强化学习影响动物集体行为提供了早期实证。
