Motivated by the challenge of guiding collective animal behavior without detailed biological models, this study proposes using a virtual fish trained via model-free reinforcement learning to control fish schools. The method employs a 2D virtual agent displayed on a screen to circumvent limitations of physical robots, learning effective movement policies in simulation even when real fish often ignore the stimulus. Real-world experiments confirm that the learned policy successfully guides live fish schools toward target directions, with statistical analysis showing it significantly outperforms baseline conditions like no stimulus or a heuristic edge-following strategy, demonstrating early potential for reinforcement learning in swarm-machine interaction.
本研究针对缺乏详细鱼类行为模型下引导群体行为的挑战，提出使用通过无模型强化学习训练的虚拟鱼来控制鱼群。该方法采用屏幕上显示的二维虚拟代理，以规避物理机器人的耐久性和运动限制，在模拟中学习有效的游动策略，即使真实鱼类常忽略刺激。真实实验证实，习得的策略能成功将活鱼群引导至指定目标方向，统计分析表明该方法显著优于无刺激或启发式“边缘停留”策略等基线条件，为强化学习在群体-机器交互中的应用提供了早期验证。
Masked Auto-Regressive Variational Acceleration: Fast Inference Makes Practical Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Yuxuan Gu, Weimin Bai, Yifei Wang, Weijian Luo, He Sun
First: 2025-11-19T07:24:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T10:51:27+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Masked auto-regressive diffusion models (MAR) benefit from the expressive modeling ability of diffusion models and the flexibility of masked auto-regressive ordering. However, vanilla MAR suffers from slow inference due to its hierarchical inference mechanism: an outer AR unmasking loop and an inner diffusion denoising chain. Such decoupled structure not only harm the generation efficiency but also hinder the practical use of MAR for reinforcement learning (RL), an increasingly critical paradigm for generative model post-training.To address this fundamental issue, we introduce MARVAL (Masked Auto-regressive Variational Acceleration), a distillation-based framework that compresses the diffusion chain into a single AR generation step while preserving the flexible auto-regressive unmasking order. Such a distillation with MARVAL not only yields substantial inference acceleration but, crucially, makes RL post-training with verifiable rewards practical, resulting in scalable yet human-preferred fast generative models. Our contributions are twofold: (1) a novel score-based variational objective for distilling masked auto-regressive diffusion models into a single generation step without sacrificing sample quality; and (2) an efficient RL framework for masked auto-regressive models via MARVAL-RL. On ImageNet 256*256, MARVAL-Huge achieves an FID of 2.00 with more than 30 times speedup compared with MAR-diffusion, and MARVAL-RL yields consistent improvements in CLIP and image-reward scores on ImageNet datasets with entity names. In conclusion, MARVAL demonstrates the first practical path to distillation and RL of masked auto-regressive diffusion models, enabling fast sampling and better preference alignments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：掩码自回归变分加速：快速推理实现实用强化学习
掩码自回归扩散模型（MAR）结合了扩散模型的强大建模能力与掩码自回归排序的灵活性，但其分层推理机制（外层自回归解掩循环与内层扩散去噪链）导致推理速度缓慢。这种解耦结构不仅影响生成效率，也阻碍了MAR在强化学习（RL）中的实际应用。为解决这一问题，我们提出MARVAL（掩码自回归变分加速），这是一个基于蒸馏的框架，可将扩散链压缩为单步自回归生成，同时保留灵活的解掩顺序。MARVAL蒸馏不仅实现了显著的推理加速，更关键的是使基于可验证奖励的RL后训练变得实用，从而构建出可扩展且符合人类偏好的快速生成模型。我们的贡献包括：（1）提出基于分数的变分目标，将掩码自回归扩散模型蒸馏为单步生成且不损失样本质量；（2）通过MARVAL-RL为掩码自回归模型构建高效RL框架。在ImageNet 256*256数据集上，MARVAL-Huge以2.00的FID指标实现超过MAR扩散模型30倍的加速，MARVAL-RL在包含实体名称的ImageNet数据集中持续提升CLIP与图像奖励分数。综上，MARVAL首次为掩码自回归扩散模型提供了实用的蒸馏与RL路径，实现了快速采样与更好的偏好对齐。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the slow inference problem of masked auto-regressive diffusion models (MAR), which limits their practical use in reinforcement learning (RL) due to a hierarchical structure involving an outer auto-regressive loop and an inner diffusion chain. To solve this, the authors propose MARVAL, a distillation framework that compresses the diffusion process into a single auto-regressive step while maintaining flexible unmasking order, enabling fast inference and making RL post-training feasible. Experimental results on ImageNet 256*256 show that MARVAL-Huge achieves an FID of 2.00 with over 30x speedup compared to MAR-diffusion, and MARVAL-RL improves CLIP and image-reward scores, demonstrating effective preference alignment and scalable generative modeling.
本文针对掩码自回归扩散模型（MAR）推理速度慢的问题展开研究，该问题因其外层自回归循环和内层扩散链的层次化结构而限制了在强化学习（RL）中的实际应用。为此，作者提出了MARVAL，一个蒸馏框架，将扩散过程压缩为单步自回归生成，同时保持灵活的掩码解除顺序，从而实现快速推理并使RL后训练变得可行。在ImageNet 256*256数据集上的实验结果表明，MARVAL-Huge实现了2.00的FID分数，相比MAR-diffusion加速超过30倍，且MARVAL-RL在CLIP和图像奖励分数上均有提升，证明了其在偏好对齐和可扩展生成建模方面的有效性。
A Novel Evolutionary Method for Automated Skull-Face Overlay in Computer-Aided Craniofacial Superimposition
Authors: Práxedes Martínez-Moreno, Andrea Valsecchi, Pablo Mesejo, Pilar Navarro-Ramírez, Valentino Lugli, Sergio Damas
First: 2026-02-26T13:55:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T10:19:20+00:00
Comments: 11 pages, 6 figures, 3 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Craniofacial Superimposition is a forensic technique for identifying skeletal remains by comparing a post-mortem skull with ante-mortem facial photographs. A critical step in this process is Skull-Face Overlay (SFO). This stage involves aligning a 3D skull model with a 2D facial image, typically guided by cranial and facial landmarks' correspondence. However, its accuracy is undermined by individual variability in soft-tissue thickness, introducing significant uncertainty into the overlay. This paper introduces Lilium, an automated evolutionary method to enhance the accuracy and robustness of SFO. Lilium explicitly models soft-tissue variability using a 3D cone-based representation whose parameters are optimized via a Differential Evolution algorithm. The method enforces anatomical, morphological, and photographic plausibility through a combination of constraints: landmark matching, camera parameter consistency, head pose alignment, skull containment within facial boundaries, and region parallelism. This emulation of the usual forensic practitioners' approach leads Lilium to outperform the state-of-the-art method in terms of both accuracy and robustness.
中文标题/摘要
标题：一种用于计算机辅助颅面叠加中自动颅骨-面部覆盖的新型进化方法
颅面叠加是一种法医学技术，通过比对死后颅骨与生前面部照片来识别骨骼遗骸。该过程中的关键步骤是颅骨-面部覆盖（SFO），涉及将三维颅骨模型与二维面部图像对齐，通常依据颅骨与面部标志点的对应关系进行。然而，软组织厚度的个体差异会降低其准确性，为覆盖过程引入显著不确定性。本文提出Lilium，一种自动进化方法，旨在提升SFO的准确性与鲁棒性。Lilium采用基于三维锥体的表示法明确建模软组织变异性，其参数通过差分进化算法优化。该方法结合多种约束条件确保解剖、形态及摄影合理性：标志点匹配、相机参数一致性、头部姿态对齐、颅骨包含于面部边界内以及区域平行性。通过模拟法医从业者的常规操作流程，Lilium在准确性和鲁棒性上均优于当前最优方法。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to improve the accuracy of skull-face overlay in forensic craniofacial superimposition, which is challenged by individual soft-tissue thickness variability, this paper introduces Lilium, an automated evolutionary method. The method employs a Differential Evolution algorithm to optimize a 3D cone-based model that explicitly represents soft-tissue variability, incorporating anatomical, morphological, and photographic constraints such as landmark matching and skull containment within facial boundaries. Experimental results demonstrate that Lilium outperforms the state-of-the-art method in both accuracy and robustness, effectively emulating and enhancing the forensic practitioner's approach.
本研究旨在改进法医颅面重合技术中因个体软组织厚度差异而影响准确性的颅骨-面部叠加步骤，提出了一种名为Lilium的自动化进化方法。该方法采用差分进化算法优化一个明确模拟软组织变异性的三维锥体模型，并通过结合标志点匹配、颅骨包含于面部轮廓等解剖学、形态学和摄影学约束来确保合理性。实验结果表明，Lilium在准确性和鲁棒性上均优于现有最先进方法，有效模拟并提升了法医实践中的叠加流程。
ERGO: Efficient High-Resolution Visual Understanding for Vision-Language Models
Authors: Jewon Lee, Wooksu Shin, Seungmin Yang, Ki-Ung Song, DongUk Lim, Jaeyeon Kim, Tae-Ho Kim, Bo-Kyeong Kim
First: 2025-09-26T07:15:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T09:34:26+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Efficient processing of high-resolution images is crucial for real-world vision-language applications. However, existing Large Vision-Language Models (LVLMs) incur substantial computational overhead due to the large number of vision tokens. With the advent of "thinking with images" models, reasoning now extends beyond text to the visual domain. This capability motivates our two-stage "coarse-to-fine" reasoning pipeline: first, a downsampled image is analyzed to identify task-relevant regions; then, only these regions are cropped at full resolution and processed in a subsequent reasoning stage. This approach reduces computational cost while preserving fine-grained visual details where necessary. A major challenge lies in inferring which regions are truly relevant to a given query. Recent related methods often fail in the first stage after input-image downsampling, due to perception-driven reasoning, where clear visual information is required for effective reasoning. To address this issue, we propose ERGO (Efficient Reasoning & Guided Observation) that performs reasoning-driven perception-leveraging multimodal context to determine where to focus. Our model can account for perceptual uncertainty, expanding the cropped region to cover visually ambiguous areas for answering questions. To this end, we develop simple yet effective reward components in a reinforcement learning framework for coarse-to-fine perception. Across multiple datasets, our approach delivers higher accuracy than the original model and competitive methods, with greater efficiency. For instance, ERGO surpasses Qwen2.5-VL-7B on the V* benchmark by 4.7 points while using only 23% of the vision tokens, achieving a 3x inference speedup. The code and models can be found at: https://github.com/nota-github/ERGO.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ERGO：面向视觉语言模型的高效高分辨率视觉理解
高效处理高分辨率图像对现实世界的视觉语言应用至关重要。然而，现有的大型视觉语言模型因视觉标记数量庞大而产生大量计算开销。随着“图像思维”模型的出现，推理能力已从文本扩展至视觉领域。这一能力促使我们提出两阶段“由粗到精”的推理流程：首先分析下采样图像以识别任务相关区域；随后仅对这些区域进行全分辨率裁剪，并在后续推理阶段处理。该方法在降低计算成本的同时，在必要时保留了细粒度视觉细节。核心挑战在于推断哪些区域真正与给定查询相关。近期相关方法常因感知驱动推理的局限，在下采样后的第一阶段失效——有效推理需要清晰的视觉信息。为解决此问题，我们提出ERGO（高效推理与引导观察），通过推理驱动的感知机制，利用多模态上下文确定关注区域。该模型能处理感知不确定性，扩展裁剪区域以覆盖视觉模糊区域来回答问题。为此，我们在强化学习框架中设计了简洁高效的奖励组件，用于实现由粗到精的感知。在多个数据集上，本方法以更高效率实现了优于原模型及竞争方法的准确率。例如，ERGO在V*基准测试中超越Qwen2.5-VL-7B模型4.7分，仅使用23%的视觉标记，推理速度提升3倍。代码与模型已开源：https://github.com/nota-github/ERGO。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the high computational cost of processing high-resolution images in large vision-language models (LVLMs) by introducing ERGO, a two-stage coarse-to-fine reasoning pipeline. The motivation is to reduce the number of vision tokens needed while preserving fine details, overcoming limitations of prior methods that often fail at the initial downsampling stage due to reliance on clear visual cues. ERGO employs reasoning-driven perception, using multimodal context to identify and crop task-relevant regions at full resolution, and incorporates reinforcement learning with reward components to handle perceptual uncertainty by expanding cropped areas when needed. Experimental results show that ERGO achieves higher accuracy than baseline models like Qwen2.5-VL-7B, with a 4.7-point improvement on the V* benchmark while using only 23% of vision tokens and achieving a 3x inference speedup.

A Survey of Reinforcement Learning For Economics
Authors: Pranjal Rawat
First: 2026-03-09T21:43:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T08:31:37+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This survey (re)introduces reinforcement learning methods to economists. The curse of dimensionality limits how far exact dynamic programming can be effectively applied, forcing us to rely on suitably "small" problems or our ability to convert "big" problems into smaller ones. While this reduction has been sufficient for many classical applications, a growing class of economic models resists such reduction. Reinforcement learning algorithms offer a natural, sample-based extension of dynamic programming, extending tractability to problems with high-dimensional states, continuous actions, and strategic interactions. I review the theory connecting classical planning to modern learning algorithms and demonstrate their mechanics through simulated examples in pricing, inventory control, strategic games, and preference elicitation. I also examine the practical vulnerabilities of these algorithms, noting their brittleness, sample inefficiency, sensitivity to hyperparameters, and the absence of global convergence guarantees outside of tabular settings. The successes of reinforcement learning remain strictly bounded by these constraints, as well as a reliance on accurate simulators. When guided by economic structure, reinforcement learning provides a remarkably flexible framework. It stands as an imperfect, but promising, addition to the computational economist's toolkit. A companion survey (Rust and Rawat, 2026b) covers the inverse problem of inferring preferences from observed behavior. All simulation code is publicly available.
中文标题/摘要
标题：强化学习在经济学中的应用综述
本文向经济学家（重新）介绍了强化学习方法。维度灾难限制了精确动态规划的有效应用范围，迫使我们依赖适当的“小”问题或将“大”问题转化为较小问题的能力。尽管这种简化对许多经典应用已足够，但越来越多的经济模型难以进行此类简化。强化学习算法提供了一种基于样本的动态规划自然扩展，将可处理性延伸至高维状态、连续动作和策略交互的问题。本文回顾了连接经典规划与现代学习算法的理论，并通过定价、库存控制、策略博弈和偏好诱导的模拟示例展示其机制。同时，文章分析了这些算法的实际脆弱性，包括其脆弱性、样本效率低下、对超参数的敏感性，以及在非表格化场景中缺乏全局收敛保证。强化学习的成功仍严格受限于这些约束以及对精确模拟器的依赖。当结合经济结构指导时，强化学习提供了一个极为灵活的框架，虽不完美但前景可期，是计算经济学家工具箱的有力补充。配套综述（Rust and Rawat, 2026b）涵盖了从观测行为推断偏好的逆问题。所有模拟代码均已公开。
Summary / 总结
This survey aims to introduce reinforcement learning (RL) to economists as a method to overcome the curse of dimensionality in dynamic programming, which restricts classical approaches to small or reducible problems. The method involves using sample-based RL algorithms to extend tractability to economic models with high-dimensional states, continuous actions, and strategic interactions. Experimental results from simulated examples in pricing, inventory control, games, and preference elicitation demonstrate RL's flexibility, but also reveal practical vulnerabilities such as brittleness, sample inefficiency, hyperparameter sensitivity, and lack of global convergence guarantees, limiting its success to contexts with accurate simulators and guided economic structure.
本综述旨在向经济学家介绍强化学习方法，以解决动态规划中维度灾难的限制，该限制迫使经典方法仅适用于小型或可简化的问题。该方法利用基于样本的强化学习算法，将可处理性扩展到具有高维状态、连续动作和策略互动的经济模型中。在定价、库存控制、策略博弈和偏好诱导等模拟实验结果表明，强化学习具有灵活性，但也揭示了实际脆弱性，如脆弱性、样本效率低下、超参数敏感性以及缺乏全局收敛保证，这些约束将其成功限制在需要精确模拟器和经济结构指导的背景下。
Amnesia: Adversarial Semantic Layer Specific Activation Steering in Large Language Models
Authors: Ali Raza, Gurang Gupta, Nikolay Matyunin, Jibesh Patra
First: 2026-03-10T09:41:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T08:26:11+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Warning: This article includes red-teaming experiments, which contain examples of compromised LLM responses that may be offensive or upsetting. Large Language Models (LLMs) have the potential to create harmful content, such as generating sophisticated phishing emails and assisting in writing code of harmful computer viruses. Thus, it is crucial to ensure their safe and responsible response generation. To reduce the risk of generating harmful or irresponsible content, researchers have developed techniques such as reinforcement learning with human feedback to align LLM's outputs with human values and preferences. However, it is still undetermined whether such measures are sufficient to prevent LLMs from generating interesting responses. In this study, we propose Amnesia, a lightweight activation-space adversarial attack that manipulates internal transformer states to bypass existing safety mechanisms in open-weight LLMs. Through experimental analysis on state-of-the-art, open-weight LLMs, we demonstrate that our attack effectively circumvents existing safeguards, enabling the generation of harmful content without the need for any fine-tuning or additional training. Our experiments on benchmark datasets show that the proposed attack can induce various antisocial behaviors in LLMs. These findings highlight the urgent need for more robust security measures in open-weight LLMs and underscore the importance of continued research to prevent their potential misuse.

A Survey of Frontiers in LLM Reasoning: Inference Scaling, Learning to Reason, and Agentic Systems
Authors: Zixuan Ke, Fangkai Jiao, Yifei Ming, Xuan-Phi Nguyen, Austin Xu, Do Xuan Long, Minzhi Li, Chengwei Qin, Peifeng Wang, Silvio Savarese, Caiming Xiong, Shafiq Joty
First: 2025-04-12T01:27:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T08:09:31+00:00
Comments: 72 pages, 6 figures. Accepted to TMLR, with Survey Certification award
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reasoning is a fundamental cognitive process that enables logical inference, problem-solving, and decision-making. With the rapid advancement of large language models (LLMs), reasoning has emerged as a key capability that distinguishes advanced AI systems from conventional models that empower chatbots. In this survey, we categorize existing methods along two orthogonal dimensions: (1) Regimes, which define the stage at which reasoning is achieved (either at inference time or through dedicated training); and (2) Architectures, which determine the components involved in the reasoning process, distinguishing between standalone LLMs and agentic compound systems that incorporate external tools, and multi-agent collaborations. Within each dimension, we analyze two key perspectives: (1) Input level, which focuses on techniques that construct high-quality prompts that the LLM condition on; and (2) Output level, which methods that refine multiple sampled candidates to enhance reasoning quality. This categorization provides a systematic understanding of the evolving landscape of LLM reasoning, highlighting emerging trends such as the shift from inference-scaling to learning-to-reason (e.g., DeepSeek-R1), and the transition to agentic workflows (e.g., OpenAI Deep Research, Manus Agent). Additionally, we cover a broad spectrum of learning algorithms, from supervised fine-tuning to reinforcement learning such as PPO and GRPO, and the training of reasoners and verifiers. We also examine key designs of agentic workflows, from established patterns like generator-evaluator and LLM debate to recent innovations. ...

Summary / 总结
This survey paper is motivated by the growing importance of reasoning as a key capability distinguishing advanced large language models (LLMs) from simpler chatbots. The method involves categorizing existing approaches along two dimensions: regimes (inference-time vs. training-time reasoning) and architectures (standalone LLMs vs. agentic systems with tools or multi-agent collaboration), further analyzed through input-level prompting and output-level candidate refinement techniques. The main experimental results and analysis highlight emerging trends, such as the shift from inference-scaling to learning-to-reason paradigms (e.g., DeepSeek-R1) and the rise of agentic workflows (e.g., OpenAI Deep Research), while covering a broad spectrum of training algorithms and system designs.
本综述论文的动机在于，推理能力作为区分先进大语言模型与简单聊天机器人的关键特性，其重要性日益增长。其方法沿两个维度对现有技术进行分类：范式（推理时实现与训练时学习）和架构（独立大模型与整合外部工具或多智能体协作的智能体复合系统），并进一步从输入级提示构建和输出级候选答案精炼的角度进行分析。主要的实验成果与分析强调了新兴趋势，例如从推理缩放向学习推理（如DeepSeek-R1）的范式转变，以及智能体工作流（如OpenAI深度研究）的兴起，同时涵盖了从监督微调到强化学习等多种训练算法及系统设计。
Dual Consensus: Escaping from Spurious Majority in Unsupervised RLVR via Two-Stage Vote Mechanism
Authors: Kaixuan Du, Meng Cao, Hang Zhang, Yukun Wang, Xiangzhou Huang, Ni Li
First: 2026-03-17T07:57:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T07:57:23+00:00
Comments: 10 pages, 5 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Current label-free RLVR approaches for large language models (LLMs), such as TTRL and Self-reward, have demonstrated effectiveness in improving the performance of LLMs on complex reasoning tasks. However, these methods rely heavily on accurate pseudo-label estimation and converge on spurious yet popular answers, thereby trapping in a dominant mode and limiting further improvements. Building on this, we propose Dual Consensus Reinforcement Learning (DCRL), a novel self-supervised training method which is capable of generating more reliable learning signals through a two-stage consensus mechanism. The model initially acts as an anchor, producing dominant responses; then it serves as an explorer, generating diverse auxiliary signals via a temporary unlearning process. The final training target is derived from the harmonic mean of these two signal sets. Notably, the process operates entirely without external models or supervision. Across eight benchmarks and diverse domains, DCRL consistently improves Pass@1 over majority vote while yielding more stable training dynamics. These results demonstrate that DCRL establishes a scalable path toward stronger reasoning without labels.
中文标题/摘要
标题：双重共识：通过两阶段投票机制在无监督RLVR中摆脱伪多数陷阱
当前面向大语言模型的无标注RLVR方法（如TTRL和Self-reward）已证明能有效提升LLM在复杂推理任务上的性能。然而，这些方法严重依赖准确的伪标签估计，且易收敛于虚假但流行的答案，从而陷入主导模式并限制进一步改进。基于此，我们提出双重共识强化学习，这是一种新颖的自监督训练方法，通过两阶段共识机制生成更可靠的学习信号。模型首先作为锚点生成主导响应，随后作为探索者通过临时遗忘过程生成多样化的辅助信号。最终训练目标源自这两组信号的调和平均值。值得注意的是，该过程完全无需外部模型或监督。在八个基准测试和多个领域中，DCRL始终在多数投票基础上提升Pass@1指标，同时产生更稳定的训练动态。这些结果表明，DCRL为无需标注的更强推理能力建立了可扩展的路径。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of existing unsupervised RLVR methods, which often converge on spurious popular answers due to reliance on pseudo-label estimation, this paper introduces Dual Consensus Reinforcement Learning (DCRL). The method employs a two-stage consensus mechanism where the model first acts as an anchor to produce dominant responses and then as an explorer to generate diverse auxiliary signals via temporary unlearning, with the final training target derived from the harmonic mean of these signals. Experimental results across eight benchmarks show that DCRL consistently improves Pass@1 over majority vote and yields more stable training dynamics, demonstrating a scalable path toward stronger reasoning without external supervision.
针对现有无监督RLVR方法因依赖伪标签估计而常收敛于虚假流行答案的局限，本文提出了双重共识强化学习（DCRL）。该方法采用两阶段共识机制：模型首先作为锚点生成主导响应，随后作为探索者通过临时遗忘过程产生多样辅助信号，最终训练目标源自这些信号的调和平均。在八个基准测试上的实验结果表明，DCRL持续优于多数投票的Pass@1指标，并带来更稳定的训练动态，证明了无需外部监督即可实现更强推理的可扩展路径。
Stepwise Think-Critique: A Unified Framework for Robust and Interpretable LLM Reasoning
Authors: Jiaqi Xu, Cuiling Lan, Xuejin Chen, Yan LU
First: 2025-12-17T18:15:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T07:50:35+00:00
Comments: Under Review
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Human beings solve complex problems through critical thinking, where reasoning and evaluation are intertwined to converge toward correct solutions. However, most existing large language models (LLMs) treat the reasoning and verification as separate processes: they either generate reasoning without explicit self-checking or rely on external verifiers to detect errors post hoc. The former lacks immediate feedback, while the latter increases system complexity and hinders synchronized learning. Motivated by human critical thinking, we propose Stepwise Think-Critique (STC), a unified and end-to-end trainable framework that interleaves reasoning and self-critique at every intermediate step within a single model. STC is trained with a hybrid reinforcement learning objective that integrates reasoning rewards and critique-consistency rewards, thereby jointly optimizing solution correctness and reliability of self-evaluation. Experiments on mathematical reasoning benchmarks show that STC demonstrates strong critical-thinking capabilities and produces more interpretable reasoning traces, representing a step toward LLMs with built-in critical thinking.
中文标题/摘要
标题：逐步思考-批判：面向鲁棒可解释大语言模型推理的统一框架
人类通过批判性思维解决复杂问题，其推理与评估过程相互交织以趋近正确解。然而现有大语言模型大多将推理与验证分离：要么生成缺乏显式自检的推理过程，要么依赖外部验证器进行事后纠错。前者缺乏即时反馈，后者则增加系统复杂度并阻碍协同学习。受人类批判性思维启发，我们提出逐步思考-批判框架——一种统一且端到端可训练的框架，在单一模型内部实现每个中间步骤的推理与自批判交错执行。该框架通过融合推理奖励与批判一致性奖励的混合强化学习目标进行训练，从而协同优化解的正确性与自评估可靠性。数学推理基准实验表明，该框架展现出强大的批判性思维能力，生成更具可解释性的推理轨迹，标志着向具备内置批判性思维的大语言模型迈进了一步。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to emulate human critical thinking where reasoning and evaluation are intertwined, this paper proposes Stepwise Think-Critique (STC), a unified framework that interleaves reasoning and self-critique at each step within a single large language model. The method employs a hybrid reinforcement learning objective combining reasoning and critique-consistency rewards to jointly optimize solution correctness and self-evaluation reliability. Experimental results on mathematical reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that STC enhances critical-thinking capabilities and yields more interpretable reasoning traces compared to approaches that separate reasoning and verification.
受人类批判性思维中推理与评估交织的启发，本文提出了逐步思考-批判框架，该统一框架在单个大语言模型内于每个中间步骤交织进行推理与自我批判。该方法采用结合了推理奖励和批判一致性奖励的混合强化学习目标，以共同优化解答的正确性和自我评估的可靠性。在数学推理基准测试上的实验结果表明，该框架展现出更强的批判性思维能力，并产生了比将推理与验证分离的方法更具可解释性的推理轨迹。
Offline Exploration-Aware Fine-Tuning for Long-Chain Mathematical Reasoning
Authors: Yongyu Mu, Jiali Zeng, Fandong Meng, JingBo Zhu, Tong Xiao
First: 2026-03-17T07:36:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T07:36:29+00:00
Comments: Working in process
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Through encouraging self-exploration, reinforcement learning from verifiable rewards (RLVR) has significantly advanced the mathematical reasoning capabilities of large language models. As the starting point for RLVR, the capacity of supervised fine-tuning (SFT) to memorize new chain-of-thought trajectories provides a crucial initialization that shapes the subsequent exploration landscape. However, existing research primarily focuses on facilitating exploration during RLVR training, leaving exploration-aware SFT under-explored. To bridge this gap, we propose Offline eXploration-Aware (OXA) fine-tuning. Specifically, OXA optimizes two objectives: promoting low-confidence verified teacher-distillation data to internalize previously uncaptured reasoning patterns, and suppressing high-confidence incorrect self-distillation data to redistribute probability mass of incorrect patterns toward potentially correct candidates. Experimental results across 6 benchmarks show that OXA consistently improves mathematical reasoning performance, especially achieving an average gain of $+6$ Pass@1 and $+5$ Pass@$k$ points compared to conventional SFT on the Qwen2.5-1.5B-Math. Crucially, OXA elevates initial policy entropy, and performance gains persist throughout extensive RLVR training, demonstrating the long-term value of OXA.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向长链数学推理的离线探索感知微调
通过鼓励自我探索，基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）显著提升了大型语言模型的数学推理能力。作为RLVR的起点，监督微调（SFT）记忆新思维链轨迹的能力提供了关键初始化，塑造了后续的探索空间。然而，现有研究主要集中于促进RLVR训练期间的探索，对探索感知的SFT关注不足。为填补这一空白，我们提出了离线探索感知（OXA）微调。具体而言，OXA优化两个目标：促进低置信度已验证教师蒸馏数据以内化先前未捕获的推理模式，并抑制高置信度错误自蒸馏数据以将错误模式的概率质量重新分配给潜在正确候选。在6个基准测试上的实验结果表明，OXA持续提升数学推理性能，尤其在Qwen2.5-1.5B-Math模型上，相比传统SFT平均获得+6 Pass@1和+5 Pass@k的提升。关键的是，OXA提高了初始策略熵，且性能增益在广泛的RLVR训练中持续存在，证明了OXA的长期价值。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the under-explored role of supervised fine-tuning (SFT) in preparing large language models for subsequent reinforcement learning from verifiable rewards (RLVR) in mathematical reasoning. The authors propose Offline eXploration-Aware (OXA) fine-tuning, a method that optimizes two objectives: promoting low-confidence verified data to internalize new reasoning patterns and suppressing high-confidence incorrect data to redistribute probability toward correct candidates. Experimental results on six benchmarks demonstrate that OXA consistently enhances performance, notably achieving average gains of +6 Pass@1 and +5 Pass@k points over conventional SFT on the Qwen2.5-1.5B-Math model, while increasing initial policy entropy and sustaining improvements throughout extended RLVR training.
本文针对在数学推理中，监督微调为后续可验证奖励的强化学习做准备这一未被充分探索的角色进行研究。作者提出了离线探索感知微调方法，该方法优化两个目标：促进低置信度的已验证数据以内化新的推理模式，并抑制高置信度的错误数据以将概率质量重新分配给正确的候选答案。在六个基准测试上的实验结果表明，该方法持续提升了性能，特别是在Qwen2.5-1.5B-Math模型上，相比传统监督微调平均获得了+6 Pass@1和+5 Pass@k分的增益，同时提高了初始策略熵，并在长期的强化学习训练中保持了性能提升。
SAGE: Multi-Agent Self-Evolution for LLM Reasoning
Authors: Yulin Peng, Xinxin Zhu, Chenxing Wei, Nianbo Zeng, Leilei Wang, Ying Tiffany He, F. Richard Yu
First: 2026-03-16T13:24:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T07:31:05+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards improves reasoning in large language models (LLMs), but many methods still rely on large human-labeled datasets. While self-play reduces this dependency, it often lacks explicit planning and strong quality control, limiting stability in long-horizon multi-step reasoning. We present SAGE (Self-evolving Agents for Generalized reasoning Evolution), a closed-loop framework where four agents: Challenger, Planner, Solver, and Critic, co-evolve from a shared LLM backbone using only a small seed set. The Challenger continuously generates increasingly difficult tasks; the Planner converts each task into a structured multi-step plan; and the Solver follows the plan to produce an answer, whose correctness is determined by external verifiers. The Critic scores and filters both generated questions and plans to prevent curriculum drift and maintain training signal quality, enabling stable self-training. Across mathematics and code-generation benchmarks, SAGE delivers consistent gains across model scales, improving the Qwen-2.5-7B model by 8.9% on LiveCodeBench and 10.7% on OlympiadBench.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SAGE：面向大语言模型推理的多智能体自进化框架
基于可验证奖励的强化学习能提升大语言模型（LLMs）的推理能力，但现有方法仍依赖大规模人工标注数据集。尽管自博弈机制可降低这种依赖，但其常缺乏显式规划和严格的质量控制，限制了长跨度多步推理的稳定性。本文提出SAGE（面向泛化推理进化的自进化智能体框架），这是一个闭环系统：挑战者、规划者、求解者、评判者四个智能体仅基于少量种子数据，从共享的LLM主干网络协同进化。挑战者持续生成难度递增的任务；规划者将任务转化为结构化多步方案；求解者依据方案生成答案，其正确性由外部验证器判定。评判者对生成的问题和方案进行评分筛选，防止课程漂移并维持训练信号质量，从而实现稳定的自训练。在数学与代码生成基准测试中，SAGE在不同规模模型上均取得稳定提升，将Qwen-2.5-7B模型在LiveCodeBench和OlympiadBench上的性能分别提升8.9%和10.7%。
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind SAGE is to enhance LLM reasoning without heavy reliance on large human-labeled datasets by addressing the limitations of self-play methods, which often lack explicit planning and quality control in multi-step reasoning. The method introduces a closed-loop framework with four co-evolving agents—Challenger, Planner, Solver, and Critic—all derived from a shared LLM backbone using only a small seed set; the Challenger generates progressively harder tasks, the Planner creates structured multi-step plans, the Solver executes these plans to produce answers verified externally, and the Critic filters questions and plans to prevent curriculum drift and ensure training stability. Experimental results show consistent improvements across model scales, with the Qwen-2.5-7B model achieving gains of 8.9% on LiveCodeBench and 10.7% on OlympiadBench in mathematics and code-generation benchmarks.
SAGE的动机是在减少对大规模人工标注数据依赖的同时，提升大语言模型的推理能力，解决现有自博弈方法在长程多步推理中缺乏显式规划和质量控制的问题。该方法提出一个闭环框架，包含四个从共享LLM主干协同进化的智能体——挑战者、规划者、求解者和评判者，仅使用少量种子数据；挑战者持续生成难度递增的任务，规划者将任务转化为结构化多步计划，求解者按计划生成答案并由外部验证器检验正确性，评判者则对生成的问题和计划进行评分过滤，以防止课程漂移并保持训练信号质量。实验结果表明，该方法在不同规模模型上均取得稳定提升，其中Qwen-2.5-7B模型在数学和代码生成基准测试中，于LiveCodeBench和OlympiadBench分别提高了8.9%和10.7%。
APEX-Searcher: Augmenting LLMs' Search Capabilities through Agentic Planning and Execution
Authors: Kun Chen, Qingchao Kong, Zhao Feifei, Wenji Mao
First: 2026-03-14T09:17:12+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T07:07:31+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Retrieval-augmented generation (RAG), based on large language models (LLMs), serves as a vital approach to retrieving and leveraging external knowledge in various domain applications. When confronted with complex multi-hop questions, single-round retrieval is often insufficient for accurate reasoning and problem solving. To enhance search capabilities for complex tasks, most existing works integrate multi-round iterative retrieval with reasoning processes via end-to-end training. While these approaches significantly improve problem-solving performance, they are still faced with challenges in task reasoning and model training, especially ambiguous retrieval execution paths and sparse rewards in end-to-end reinforcement learning (RL) process, leading to inaccurate retrieval results and performance degradation. To address these issues, in this paper, we proposes APEX-Searcher, a novel Agentic Planning and Execution framework to augment LLM search capabilities. Specifically, we introduce a two-stage agentic framework that decouples the retrieval process into planning and execution: It first employs RL with decomposition-specific rewards to optimize strategic planning; Built on the sub-task decomposition, it then applies supervised fine-tuning on high-quality multi-hop trajectories to equip the model with robust iterative sub-task execution capabilities. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our proposed framework achieves significant improvements in both multi-hop RAG and task planning performances across multiple benchmarks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：APEX-Searcher：通过智能体规划与执行增强大语言模型的搜索能力
基于大语言模型的检索增强生成技术是各领域应用中获取并利用外部知识的重要方法。面对复杂的多跳问题时，单轮检索往往难以支撑精准的推理与求解。为提升复杂任务的搜索能力，现有研究多通过端到端训练将多轮迭代检索与推理过程相结合。这些方法虽显著提升了问题解决性能，但在任务推理与模型训练方面仍面临挑战，特别是检索执行路径的模糊性以及端到端强化学习过程中的稀疏奖励问题，导致检索结果不准确与性能下降。为此，本文提出APEX-Searcher——一种增强大语言模型搜索能力的新型智能体规划与执行框架。具体而言，我们引入两阶段智能体框架，将检索过程解耦为规划与执行：首先采用具有分解专项奖励的强化学习优化策略规划；基于子任务分解，随后对高质量多跳轨迹进行监督微调，使模型具备稳健的迭代子任务执行能力。大量实验表明，该框架在多个基准测试的多跳检索增强生成与任务规划性能上均取得显著提升。

To enhance search capabilities, the authors propose APEX-Searcher, a two-stage agentic framework that decouples retrieval into planning and execution: it first uses reinforcement learning with decomposition-specific rewards to optimize strategic planning, then applies supervised fine-tuning on high-quality trajectories to improve iterative sub-task execution. Experimental results show that this approach significantly boosts performance in multi-hop RAG and task planning across multiple benchmarks.
本文针对检索增强生成（RAG）在处理复杂多跳问题时单轮检索的不足，现有端到端训练方法因检索路径模糊和强化学习中奖励稀疏而导致结果不准确。为增强搜索能力，作者提出APEX-Searcher，一个两阶段的智能体框架，将检索解耦为规划与执行：首先利用强化学习和分解特定奖励优化策略规划，然后基于高质量轨迹进行监督微调以提升迭代子任务执行能力。实验结果表明，该方法在多个基准测试中显著提高了多跳RAG和任务规划的性能。
SQL-ASTRA: Alleviating Sparse Feedback in Agentic SQL via Column-Set Matching and Trajectory Aggregation
Authors: Long Li, Zhijian Zhou, Jiangxuan Long, Peiyang Liu, Weidi Xu, Zhe Wang, Shirui Pan, Chao Qu
First: 2026-03-17T06:26:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T06:26:36+00:00
Comments: 17 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Agentic Reinforcement Learning (RL) shows promise for complex tasks, but Text-to-SQL remains mostly restricted to single-turn paradigms. A primary bottleneck is the credit assignment problem. In traditional paradigms, rewards are determined solely by the final-turn feedback, which ignores the intermediate process and leads to ambiguous credit evaluation. To address this, we propose Agentic SQL, a framework featuring a universal two-tiered reward mechanism designed to provide effective trajectory-level evaluation and dense step-level signals. First, we introduce Aggregated Trajectory Reward (ATR) to resolve multi-turn credit assignment. Using an asymmetric transition matrix, ATR aggregates process-oriented scores to incentivize continuous improvement. Leveraging Lyapunov stability theory, we prove ATR acts as an energy dissipation operator, guaranteeing a cycle-free policy and monotonic convergence. Second, Column-Set Matching Reward (CSMR) provides immediate step-level rewards to mitigate sparsity. By executing queries at each turn, CSMR converts binary (0/1) feedback into dense [0, 1] signals based on partial correctness. Evaluations on BIRD show a 5% gain over binary-reward GRPO. Notably, our approach outperforms SOTA Arctic-Text2SQL-R1-7B on BIRD and Spider 2.0 using identical models, propelling Text-to-SQL toward a robust multi-turn agent paradigm.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SQL-ASTRA：通过列集匹配与轨迹聚合缓解智能体SQL中的稀疏反馈问题
智能体强化学习在复杂任务中展现出潜力，但文本到SQL领域仍主要局限于单轮范式。核心瓶颈在于信用分配问题：传统范式仅依据最终轮次反馈确定奖励，忽略了中间过程，导致信用评估模糊。为此，我们提出智能体SQL框架，采用通用双层奖励机制，提供有效的轨迹级评估与密集的步骤级信号。首先，引入聚合轨迹奖励（ATR）以解决多轮信用分配问题。通过非对称转移矩阵聚合过程导向的评分，激励持续改进。基于李雅普诺夫稳定性理论，我们证明ATR可作为能量耗散算子，确保策略无循环且单调收敛。其次，列集匹配奖励（CSMR）提供即时步骤级奖励以缓解稀疏性。通过在每轮执行查询，CSMR将二元（0/1）反馈转换为基于部分正确性的密集[0,1]信号。在BIRD数据集上的评估显示，本方法比二元奖励GRPO提升5%。值得注意的是，使用相同模型时，我们的方法在BIRD和Spider 2.0上均优于SOTA Arctic-Text2SQL-R1-7B，推动文本到SQL向鲁棒的多轮智能体范式演进。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the credit assignment problem in agentic reinforcement learning for multi-turn Text-to-SQL, where sparse binary feedback from final-turn execution fails to guide intermediate steps effectively. To alleviate this, the authors propose SQL-ASTRA, a framework with a two-tiered reward mechanism: an Aggregated Trajectory Reward (ATR) that uses an asymmetric transition matrix to provide trajectory-level evaluation and ensure monotonic convergence via Lyapunov stability theory, and a Column-Set Matching Reward (CSMR) that offers dense step-level rewards by assessing partial correctness of queries at each turn. Experimental results on the BIRD benchmark show a 5% improvement over binary-reward GRPO, and the approach outperforms the state-of-the-art Arctic-Text2SQL-R1-7B model on both BIRD and Spider 2.0, advancing Text-to-SQL toward a robust multi-turn agent paradigm.
本文针对多轮Text-to-SQL中智能体强化学习的信用分配问题，其中仅依赖最终轮执行的稀疏二元反馈无法有效指导中间步骤。为缓解此问题，作者提出了SQL-ASTRA框架，采用双层奖励机制：聚合轨迹奖励（ATR）通过非对称转移矩阵提供轨迹级评估，并基于李雅普诺夫稳定性理论确保单调收敛；列集匹配奖励（CSMR）则通过每轮查询的部分正确性评估，提供密集的步骤级奖励。在BIRD基准测试上的实验结果显示，该方法比二元奖励的GRPO提升了5%，并在BIRD和Spider 2.0上超越了最先进的Arctic-Text2SQL-R1-7B模型，推动了Text-to-SQL向鲁棒的多轮智能体范式发展。
Execution-Grounded Credit Assignment for GRPO in Code Generation
Authors: Abhijit Kumar, Natalya Kumar, Shikhar Gupta
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-03-17T06:22:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T06:22:44+00:00
Comments: Accepted at SPOT ICLR 2026 (https://openreview.net/forum?id=nqkVB5EVXJ)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Critic-free reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) improves code generation by optimizing unit-test pass rates, but GRPO-style updates suffer from coarse credit assignment: a single outcome signal is spread uniformly across long programs even when failure stems from a localized semantic error. We propose Execution-Grounded Credit Assignment (EGCA), which localizes GRPO updates using execution traces. For programs that satisfy algorithmic constraints but fail tests, EGCA executes the candidate and a canonical reference solution (curated once offline; used for analysis, not supervision) under identical instrumentation, identifies the earliest semantic divergence, and assigns advantage only to the corresponding token span while masking downstream tokens. EGCA is a drop-in modification requiring no critic, auxiliary loss, or learned verifier, yielding 82.1% pass@1 on HumanEval (+3.1 over GRPO) and 68.9% on MBPP (+1.5) with 18% wall-clock overhead.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向代码生成中GRPO的执行溯源信用分配方法
基于可验证奖励的无评论家强化学习通过优化单元测试通过率改进代码生成，但GRPO式更新存在信用分配粗糙的问题：即使失败源于局部语义错误，单一结果信号仍均匀分配至长程序中。我们提出执行溯源信用分配方法，利用执行轨迹定位GRPO更新。对于满足算法约束但测试失败的程序，EGCA在相同插桩环境下执行候选程序与规范参考解（离线一次性构建，仅用于分析而非监督），识别最早的语义分歧点，仅对相应词元区间分配优势值并屏蔽下游词元。EGCA作为即插即用改进方案，无需评论家网络、辅助损失或学习型验证器，在HumanEval上实现82.1%的pass@1（较GRPO提升3.1），在MBPP上达68.9%（提升1.5），仅增加18%的实时计算开销。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the coarse credit assignment problem in critic-free reinforcement learning for code generation, where uniform reward distribution across long programs fails to localize semantic errors. The proposed Execution-Grounded Credit Assignment (EGCA) method refines GRPO updates by executing both candidate and reference solutions, identifying the earliest point of semantic divergence via execution traces, and assigning advantage only to the relevant token span while masking later tokens. Experimental results show that EGCA improves pass@1 performance to 82.1% on HumanEval and 68.9% on MBPP, outperforming GRPO with minimal computational overhead, without requiring additional critics or learned components.
本文针对代码生成中无评论家强化学习的粗粒度信用分配问题，即奖励在长程序中均匀分布而无法定位语义错误，提出了执行基础的信用分配方法。该方法通过执行候选程序和参考解决方案，利用执行轨迹识别最早的语义分歧点，仅将优势分配给对应标记片段并屏蔽后续标记，从而精细化GRPO更新。实验结果表明，该方法在HumanEval上达到82.1%的pass@1性能，在MBPP上达到68.9%，优于GRPO且计算开销较小，无需额外评论家或学习组件。
DyJR: Preserving Diversity in Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards via Dynamic Jensen-Shannon Replay
Authors: Long Li, Zhijian Zhou, Tianyi Wang, Weidi Xu, Zuming Huang, Wei Chu, Zhe Wang, Shirui Pan, Chao Qu, Yuan Qi
First: 2026-03-17T06:20:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T06:20:56+00:00
Comments: 14 pages, 3 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
While Reinforcement Learning (RL) enhances Large Language Model reasoning, on-policy algorithms like GRPO are sample-inefficient as they discard past rollouts. Existing experience replay methods address this by reusing accurate samples for direct policy updates, but this often incurs high computational costs and causes mode collapse via overfitting. We argue that historical data should prioritize sustaining diversity rather than simply reinforcing accuracy. To this end, we propose Dynamic Jensen-Shannon Replay (DyJR), a simple yet effective regularization framework using a dynamic reference distribution from recent trajectories. DyJR introduces two innovations: (1) A Time-Sensitive Dynamic Buffer that uses FIFO and adaptive sizing to retain only temporally proximal samples, synchronizing with model evolution; and (2) Jensen-Shannon Divergence Regularization, which replaces direct gradient updates with a distributional constraint to prevent diversity collapse. Experiments on mathematical reasoning and Text-to-SQL benchmarks demonstrate that DyJR significantly outperforms GRPO as well as baselines such as RLEP and Ex-GRPO, while maintaining training efficiency comparable to the original GRPO. Furthermore, from the perspective of Rank-$k$ token probability evolution, we show that DyJR enhances diversity and mitigates over-reliance on Rank-1 tokens, elucidating how specific sub-modules of DyJR influence the training dynamics.
中文标题/摘要
标题：DyJR：通过动态Jensen-Shannon回放与可验证奖励保持强化学习中的多样性
尽管强化学习（RL）能提升大语言模型的推理能力，但如GRPO等在线策略算法因丢弃历史轨迹而样本效率低下。现有经验回放方法通过重用准确样本直接更新策略来解决此问题，但这通常带来高计算成本，并因过拟合导致模式崩溃。我们认为历史数据应优先维持多样性而非单纯强化准确性。为此，我们提出动态Jensen-Shannon回放（DyJR），这是一个简单而有效的正则化框架，利用近期轨迹的动态参考分布。DyJR引入两项创新：（1）时间敏感动态缓冲区，采用FIFO和自适应大小机制，仅保留时间邻近样本以同步模型演化；（2）Jensen-Shannon散度正则化，用分布约束替代直接梯度更新以防止多样性崩溃。在数学推理和Text-to-SQL基准测试上的实验表明，DyJR显著优于GRPO及RLEP、Ex-GRPO等基线方法，同时保持与原始GRPO相当的训练效率。此外，从Rank-$k$词元概率演化视角，我们证明DyJR能增强多样性并缓解对Rank-1词元的过度依赖，阐明了DyJR特定子模块如何影响训练动态。

The paper addresses the sample inefficiency and mode collapse issues in on-policy reinforcement learning for large language models, where existing experience replay methods often overfit to accurate samples. It proposes DyJR, a regularization framework that preserves diversity through a dynamic reference distribution from recent trajectories, featuring a time-sensitive dynamic buffer and Jensen-Shannon divergence regularization to constrain policy updates. Experimental results on mathematical reasoning and Text-to-SQL benchmarks show that DyJR outperforms GRPO and other baselines while maintaining training efficiency, with analysis indicating enhanced token diversity and reduced over-reliance on top-ranked tokens.
本文针对大型语言模型在策略强化学习中的样本效率低下和模式崩溃问题，现有经验回放方法常因过度拟合准确样本而产生高计算成本。作者提出DyJR，一种通过近期轨迹动态参考分布来保持多样性的正则化框架，包含时间敏感动态缓冲区和Jensen-Shannon散度正则化以约束策略更新。在数学推理和Text-to-SQL基准测试中，DyJR显著优于GRPO及其他基线方法，同时保持与原始GRPO相当的训练效率，分析表明其增强了令牌多样性并降低了对排名第一令牌的过度依赖。
HIPO: Instruction Hierarchy via Constrained Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Keru Chen, Jun Luo, Sen Lin, Yingbin Liang, Alvaro Velasquez, Nathaniel Bastian, Shaofeng Zou
First: 2026-03-17T06:12:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T06:12:41+00:00
Comments: 9 pages + appendix. Under review
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Hierarchical Instruction Following (HIF) refers to the problem of prompting large language models with a priority-ordered stack of instructions. Standard methods like RLHF and DPO typically fail in this problem since they mainly optimize for a single objective, failing to explicitly enforce system prompt compliance. Meanwhile, supervised fine-tuning relies on mimicking filtered, compliant data, which fails to establish the priority asymmetry at the algorithmic level. In this paper, we introduce \textsc{HIPO}, a novel alignment framework that formulates HIF as a Constrained Markov Decision Process. \textsc{HIPO} elevates system prompts from mere input context to strict algorithmic boundaries. Using a primal-dual safe reinforcement learning approach, the algorithm dynamically enforces system prompt compliance as an explicit constraint, maximizing user utility strictly within this feasible region. Extensive evaluations across diverse model architectures (e.g., Qwen, Phi, Llama) demonstrate that \textsc{HIPO} significantly improves both system compliance and user utility. Furthermore, mechanistic analysis reveals that this constrained optimization autonomously drives the model to shift its attention toward long-range system tokens, providing a principled foundation for reliable LLM deployment in complex workflows.
中文标题/摘要
标题：HIPO：基于约束强化学习的指令层次化方法

本文提出了HIPO这一新颖的对齐框架，其动机是解决分层指令跟随问题，现有方法如RLHF和DPO难以确保对优先级系统指令的遵从。该方法将问题建模为约束马尔可夫决策过程，并采用原始对偶安全强化学习来动态地将系统指令遵从作为显式约束，同时在该可行区域内最大化用户效用。在Qwen、Phi、Llama等多种模型上的广泛评估表明，HIPO显著提升了系统遵从性和用户效用，机制分析进一步揭示该方法能自主驱动模型将注意力转向长距离的系统标记。
Communication-Aware Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning for Decentralized Cooperative UAV Deployment
Authors: Enguang Fan, Yifan Chen, Zihan Shan, Matthew Caesar, Jae Kim
First: 2026-03-17T05:48:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T05:48:51+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Autonomous Unmanned Aerial Vehicle (UAV) swarms are increasingly used as rapidly deployable aerial relays and sensing platforms, yet practical deployments must operate under partial observability and intermittent peer-to-peer links. We present a graph-based multi-agent reinforcement learning framework trained under centralized training with decentralized execution (CTDE): a centralized critic and global state are available only during training, while each UAV executes a shared policy using local observations and messages from nearby neighbors. Our architecture encodes local agent state and nearby entities with an agent-entity attention module, and aggregates inter-UAV messages with neighbor self-attention over a distance-limited communication graph. We evaluate primarily on a cooperative relay deployment task (DroneConnect) and secondarily on an adversarial engagement task (DroneCombat). In DroneConnect, the proposed method achieves high coverage under restricted communication and partial observation (e.g. 74% coverage with M = 5 UAVs and N = 10 nodes) while remaining competitive with a mixed-integer linear programming (MILP) optimization-based offline upper bound, and it generalizes to unseen team sizes without fine-tuning. In the adversarial setting, the same framework transfers without architectural changes and improves win rate over non-communicating baselines.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向去中心化协同无人机部署的通信感知多智能体强化学习

Experimental results on a cooperative relay task show high coverage under restricted conditions, competitive performance with an offline optimization upper bound, and generalization to unseen team sizes, while the same framework also improves win rates in an adversarial setting without architectural modifications.
本文针对自主无人机群在部分可观测和间歇性通信的现实约束下部署的挑战，旨在实现有效的分散式协作。方法提出了一种基于图的多智能体强化学习框架，采用集中训练与分散执行，每个无人机基于本地观测和邻居消息执行共享策略，并通过注意力机制增强本地状态编码和无人机间通信聚合。在协作中继任务上的实验结果表明，该方法在受限条件下实现了高覆盖率，与离线优化上限性能相当，并能泛化到未见过的团队规模；同时，同一框架在对抗性任务中无需架构修改即可提升胜率。
Noisy Data is Destructive to Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards
Authors: Yuxuan Zhu, Daniel Kang
First: 2026-03-17T05:48:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T05:48:32+00:00
Comments: 16 pages, 17 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has driven recent capability advances of large language models across various domains. Recent studies suggest that improved RLVR algorithms allow models to learn effectively from incorrect annotations, achieving performance comparable to learning from clean data. In this work, we show that these findings are invalid because the claimed 100% noisy training data is "contaminated" with clean data. After rectifying the dataset with a rigorous re-verification pipeline, we demonstrate that noise is destructive to RLVR. We show that existing RLVR algorithm improvements fail to mitigate the impact of noise, achieving similar performance to that of the basic GRPO. Furthermore, we find that the model trained on truly incorrect annotations performs 8-10% worse than the model trained on clean data across mathematical reasoning benchmarks. Finally, we show that these findings hold for real-world noise in Text2SQL tasks, where training on real-world, human annotation errors cause 5-12% lower accuracy than clean data. Our results show that current RLVR methods cannot yet compensate for poor data quality. High-quality data remains essential.
中文标题/摘要
标题：噪声数据对可验证奖励强化学习具有破坏性
可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）推动了大型语言模型在各领域的能力进展。近期研究表明，改进的RLVR算法可使模型从错误标注中有效学习，达到与干净数据相当的性能。本研究发现这些结论不成立，因为其所称的100%噪声训练数据实际'掺杂'了干净数据。通过严格的再验证流程修正数据集后，我们证明噪声对RLVR具有破坏性：现有RLVR算法改进未能缓解噪声影响，其性能与基础GRPO算法相当；在数学推理基准测试中，使用真实错误标注训练的模型比使用干净数据训练的模型性能低8-10%；在Text2SQL任务中，使用现实世界人工标注错误训练导致的准确率比干净数据低5-12%。结果表明当前RLVR方法尚无法弥补数据质量缺陷，高质量数据仍不可或缺。

本文挑战了先前关于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）能从噪声数据中有效学习的观点，指出早期研究使用的数据集无意中混杂了干净样本。作者引入了一个严格的重验证流程来创建真正的噪声数据集，并证明噪声对RLVR性能具有高度破坏性。实验表明，现有的算法改进无法缓解这种影响，其表现与GRPO等基础方法相似；在数学推理基准上，使用已验证噪声数据训练的模型比使用干净数据训练的模型性能差8-10%，在真实世界的Text2SQL任务中则差5-12%。研究最终强调，高质量数据依然至关重要，因为当前的RLVR方法尚无法弥补数据质量的不足。
SWE-QA-Pro: A Representative Benchmark and Scalable Training Recipe for Repository-Level Code Understanding
Authors: Songcheng Cai, Zhiheng Lyu, Yuansheng Ni, Xiangchao Chen, Baichuan Zhou, Shenzhe Zhu, Yi Lu, Haozhe Wang, Chi Ruan, Benjamin Schneider, Weixu Zhang, Xiang Li, Andy Zheng, Yuyu Zhang, Ping Nie, Wenhu Chen
First: 2026-03-17T05:12:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T05:12:48+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Agentic repository-level code understanding is essential for automating complex software engineering tasks, yet the field lacks reliable benchmarks. Existing evaluations often overlook the long tail topics and rely on popular repositories where Large Language Models (LLMs) can cheat via memorized knowledge. To address this, we introduce SWE-QA-Pro, a benchmark constructed from diverse, long-tail repositories with executable environments. We enforce topical balance via issue-driven clustering to cover under-represented task types and apply a rigorous difficulty calibration process: questions solvable by direct-answer baselines are filtered out. This results in a dataset where agentic workflows significantly outperform direct answering (e.g., a ~13-point gap for Claude Sonnet 4.5), confirming the necessity of agentic codebase exploration. Furthermore, to tackle the scarcity of training data for such complex behaviors, we propose a scalable synthetic data pipeline that powers a two-stage training recipe: Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) followed by Reinforcement Learning from AI Feedback (RLAIF). This approach allows small open models to learn efficient tool usage and reasoning. Empirically, a Qwen3-8B model trained with our recipe surpasses GPT-4o by 2.3 points on SWE-QA-Pro and substantially narrows the gap to state-of-the-art proprietary models, demonstrating both the validity of our evaluation and the effectiveness of our agentic training workflow.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SWE-QA-Pro：面向仓库级代码理解的代表性基准与可扩展训练方案
智能体驱动的仓库级代码理解对自动化复杂软件工程任务至关重要，但该领域缺乏可靠基准。现有评估常忽略长尾主题，并依赖大型语言模型可通过记忆知识作弊的热门仓库。为此，我们推出SWE-QA-Pro——一个基于多样化长尾仓库与可执行环境构建的基准。我们通过议题驱动聚类确保主题平衡以覆盖低代表性任务类型，并采用严格难度校准流程：过滤可直接回答基线解决的问题。由此产生的数据集中，智能体工作流显著优于直接回答（如Claude Sonnet 4.5存在约13分差距），证实了智能体代码库探索的必要性。此外，针对此类复杂行为训练数据稀缺的问题，我们提出可扩展的合成数据流水线，支持两阶段训练方案：监督微调后接基于AI反馈的强化学习。该方法使小型开源模型能学习高效工具使用与推理。实证表明，采用本方案训练的Qwen3-8B模型在SWE-QA-Pro上超越GPT-4o达2.3分，大幅缩小与顶尖专有模型的差距，既验证了评估有效性，也证明了智能体训练工作流的效能。

The paper addresses the lack of reliable benchmarks for agentic repository-level code understanding, where existing evaluations often miss long-tail topics and allow LLMs to cheat via memorization. To solve this, the authors introduce SWE-QA-Pro, a benchmark built from diverse, long-tail repositories with executable environments, using issue-driven clustering for topical balance and a difficulty calibration process to filter out questions solvable by direct-answer baselines. Experimental results show that agentic workflows significantly outperform direct answering, with a ~13-point gap for Claude Sonnet 4.5, confirming the necessity of agentic exploration. Additionally, the authors propose a scalable synthetic data pipeline for two-stage training (SFT followed by RLAIF), enabling small open models like Qwen3-8B to learn efficient tool usage and reasoning; this model surpasses GPT-4o by 2.3 points on SWE-QA-Pro, narrowing the gap to state-of-the-art proprietary models and validating both the benchmark and training approach.
本文针对代理式仓库级代码理解领域缺乏可靠基准的问题，现有评估常忽略长尾主题且允许大语言模型通过记忆知识作弊。为解决此问题，作者提出了SWE-QA-Pro基准，该基准基于多样化的长尾仓库构建，具备可执行环境，通过问题驱动的聚类确保主题平衡，并采用严格的难度校准过程过滤可直接回答的问题。实验结果表明，代理式工作流显著优于直接回答，例如Claude Sonnet 4.5有约13分的差距，证实了代理式代码库探索的必要性。此外，作者提出了一种可扩展的合成数据管道，支持两阶段训练（监督微调后接AI反馈的强化学习），使小型开源模型如Qwen3-8B能学习高效工具使用和推理；该模型在SWE-QA-Pro上超越GPT-4o达2.3分，缩小了与顶尖专有模型的差距，验证了基准和训练方法的有效性。
Urban Socio-Semantic Segmentation with Vision-Language Reasoning
Authors: Yu Wang, Yi Wang, Rui Dai, Yujie Wang, Kaikui Liu, Xiangxiang Chu, Yansheng Li
First: 2026-01-15T15:00:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T04:11:37+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
As hubs of human activity, urban surfaces consist of a wealth of semantic entities. Segmenting these various entities from satellite imagery is crucial for a range of downstream applications. Current advanced segmentation models can reliably segment entities defined by physical attributes (e.g., buildings, water bodies) but still struggle with socially defined categories (e.g., schools, parks). In this work, we achieve socio-semantic segmentation by vision-language model reasoning. To facilitate this, we introduce the Urban Socio-Semantic Segmentation dataset named SocioSeg, a new resource comprising satellite imagery, digital maps, and pixel-level labels of social semantic entities organized in a hierarchical structure. Additionally, we propose a novel vision-language reasoning framework called SocioReasoner that simulates the human process of identifying and annotating social semantic entities via cross-modal recognition and multi-stage reasoning. We employ reinforcement learning to optimize this non-differentiable process and elicit the reasoning capabilities of the vision-language model. Experiments demonstrate our approach's gains over state-of-the-art models and strong zero-shot generalization. The dataset and code are open-sourced under the Apache License 2.0 at https://github.com/AMAP-ML/SocioReasoner.
中文标题/摘要

DRL-Based Beam Positioning for LEO Satellite Constellations with Weighted Least Squares
Authors: Po-Heng Chou, Chiapin Wang, Kuan-Hao Chen, Wei-Chen Hsiao
First: 2025-11-12T00:14:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T04:06:51+00:00
Comments: 6 pages, 3 figures, 1 table, accepted by 2026 IEEE ICC Workshops
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper investigates a lightweight deep reinforcement learning (DRL)-assisted weighting framework for CSI-free multi-satellite positioning in LEO constellations, where each visible satellite provides one serving beam (one pilot response) per epoch. A discrete-action Deep Q-Network (DQN) learns satellite weights directly from received pilot measurements and geometric features, while an augmented weighted least squares (WLS) estimator provides physics-consistent localization and jointly estimates the receiver clock bias. The proposed hybrid design targets an accuracy-runtime trade-off rather than absolute supervised optimality. In a representative 2-D setting with 10 visible satellites, the proposed approach achieves sub-meter accuracy (0.395m RMSE) with low computational overhead, supporting practical deployment for resource-constrained LEO payloads.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于深度强化学习的加权最小二乘低轨卫星星座波束定位
本文研究了一种轻量级深度强化学习辅助的加权框架，用于低轨星座中无需信道状态信息的多卫星定位，其中每颗可见卫星每周期提供一个服务波束（一个导频响应）。离散动作深度Q网络直接从接收的导频测量值和几何特征中学习卫星权重，而增强的加权最小二乘估计器提供物理一致的位置估计，并联合估计接收机时钟偏差。所提出的混合设计旨在权衡精度与运行时间，而非追求绝对监督最优性。在具有10颗可见卫星的代表性二维场景中，该方法以较低计算开销实现了亚米级精度（0.395米均方根误差），支持资源受限低轨载荷的实际部署。

This paper is motivated by the need for efficient and accurate beam positioning in LEO satellite constellations, particularly for resource-constrained payloads. The method proposes a hybrid framework combining a Deep Q-Network (DQN) with a weighted least squares (WLS) estimator; the DQN learns to assign weights to satellites from pilot measurements and geometric features, and the WLS uses these weights for physics-consistent localization and clock bias estimation, targeting a favorable accuracy-runtime trade-off. Experimental results in a 2-D scenario with 10 visible satellites demonstrate that the approach achieves sub-meter positioning accuracy (0.395m RMSE) with low computational overhead, making it suitable for practical deployment.
本文的动机是低地球轨道卫星星座需要高效、精确的波束定位，尤其适用于资源受限的载荷。方法上提出了一种结合深度Q网络与加权最小二乘估计器的混合框架：深度Q网络从接收的导频测量和几何特征中学习卫星权重，加权最小二乘则利用这些权重进行物理一致的定位和时钟偏差估计，旨在优化精度与运行时间的平衡。在10颗可见卫星的二维场景实验中，该方法实现了亚米级定位精度（均方根误差0.395米）且计算开销低，支持在实际系统中部署。
Large Reward Models: Generalizable Online Robot Reward Generation with Vision-Language Models
Authors: Yanru Wu, Weiduo Yuan, Ang Qi, Vitor Guizilini, Jiageng Mao, Yue Wang
First: 2026-03-17T02:22:16+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T02:22:16+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning (RL) has shown great potential in refining robotic manipulation policies, yet its efficacy remains strongly bottlenecked by the difficulty of designing generalizable reward functions. In this paper, we propose a framework for online policy refinement by adapting foundation VLMs into online reward generators. We develop a robust, scalable reward model based on a state-of-the-art VLM, trained on a large-scale, multi-source dataset encompassing real-world robot trajectories, human-object interactions, and diverse simulated environments. Unlike prior approaches that evaluate entire trajectories post-hoc, our method leverages the VLM to formulate a multifaceted reward signal comprising process, completion, and temporal contrastive rewards based on current visual observations. Initializing with a base policy trained via Imitation Learning (IL), we employ these VLM rewards to guide the model to correct sub-optimal behaviors in a closed-loop manner. We evaluate our framework on challenging long-horizon manipulation benchmarks requiring sequential execution and precise control. Crucially, our reward model operates in a purely zero-shot manner within these test environments. Experimental results demonstrate that our method significantly improves the success rate of the initial IL policy within just 30 RL iterations, demonstrating remarkable sample efficiency. This empirical evidence highlights that VLM-generated signals can provide reliable feedback to resolve execution errors, effectively eliminating the need for manual reward engineering and facilitating efficient online refinement for robot learning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：大型奖励模型：基于视觉语言模型的可泛化在线机器人奖励生成
强化学习（RL）在优化机器人操作策略方面展现出巨大潜力，但其效果仍受限于设计可泛化奖励函数的困难。本文提出一种在线策略优化框架，将基础视觉语言模型（VLM）适配为在线奖励生成器。我们基于先进VLM构建了一个鲁棒、可扩展的奖励模型，该模型通过涵盖真实机器人轨迹、人机交互及多样化模拟环境的大规模多源数据集训练而成。与先前事后评估完整轨迹的方法不同，我们的方法利用VLM基于当前视觉观测构建包含过程奖励、完成奖励和时间对比奖励的多维度奖励信号。通过从模仿学习（IL）训练的基础策略初始化，我们运用这些VLM奖励以闭环方式引导模型修正次优行为。我们在需要顺序执行与精确控制的复杂长程操作基准测试中评估该框架。关键的是，我们的奖励模型在这些测试环境中完全以零样本方式运行。实验结果表明，仅需30次RL迭代，我们的方法就能显著提升初始IL策略的成功率，展现出卓越的样本效率。这一实证证明VLM生成的信号能提供可靠反馈以纠正执行错误，有效避免了人工奖励工程的需求，为机器人学习实现了高效的在线优化。

本研究的动机是解决机器人操作任务中强化学习因难以设计通用奖励函数而受限的瓶颈。其方法是将基础视觉语言模型适配为在线奖励生成器，利用大规模多源数据集进行训练，根据当前视觉观察生成包含过程、完成和时间对比奖励的多方面信号，用于优化初始模仿学习策略。主要实验结果表明，该框架在具有挑战性的长周期操作基准测试中以零样本方式运行，仅需30次强化学习迭代即可显著提升基础策略的成功率，展现了卓越的样本效率，并避免了手动设计奖励函数的需求。
ARISE: Agent Reasoning with Intrinsic Skill Evolution in Hierarchical Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Yu Li, Rui Miao, Zhengling Qi, Tian Lan
First: 2026-03-17T02:03:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T02:03:17+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
The dominant paradigm for improving mathematical reasoning in language models relies on Reinforcement Learning with verifiable rewards. Yet existing methods treat each problem instance in isolation without leveraging the reusable strategies that emerge and accumulate during training. To this end, we introduce ARISE (Agent Reasoning via Intrinsic Skill Evolution), a hierarchical reinforcement learning framework, in which a shared policy operates both to manage skills at high-level and to generate responses at low-level (denoted as a Skills Manager and a Worker, respectively). The Manager maintains a tiered skill library through a dedicated skill generation rollout that performs structured summarization of successful solution traces (after execution), while employing a policy-driven selection mechanism to retrieve relevant skills to condition future rollouts (before execution). A hierarchical reward design guides the co-evolution of reasoning ability and library quality. Experiments on two base models and seven benchmarks spanning both competition mathematics and Omni-MATH show that ARISE consistently outperforms GRPO-family algorithms and memory-augmented baselines, with particularly notable gains on out-of-distribution tasks. Ablation studies confirm that each component contributes to the observed improvements and that library quality and reasoning performance improve in tandem throughout training. Code is available at \href{https://github.com/Skylanding/ARISE}{https://github.com/Skylanding/ARISE}.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ARISE：分层强化学习中基于内在技能演化的智能体推理
当前提升语言模型数学推理能力的主流范式依赖于可验证奖励的强化学习。然而，现有方法孤立处理每个问题实例，未能充分利用训练过程中涌现和积累的可复用策略。为此，我们提出ARISE（基于内在技能演化的智能体推理），一种分层强化学习框架，其中共享策略同时执行高层技能管理与低层响应生成（分别称为技能管理器与执行器）。管理器通过专用技能生成推演维护分层技能库，对成功解题轨迹进行结构化总结（执行后），并采用策略驱动的选择机制检索相关技能以指导后续推演（执行前）。分层奖励设计引导推理能力与技能库质量的协同演化。在两个基础模型和涵盖竞赛数学与Omni-MATH的七个基准测试中，ARISE始终优于GRPO系列算法及记忆增强基线方法，在分布外任务上提升尤为显著。消融实验证实各组件均对性能提升有贡献，且训练过程中技能库质量与推理性能同步提升。代码发布于\href{https://github.com/Skylanding/ARISE}{https://github.com/Skylanding/ARISE}。

Motivated by the need to leverage reusable reasoning strategies beyond isolated problem-solving in mathematical reasoning, this paper introduces ARISE, a hierarchical reinforcement learning framework where a shared policy acts as both a high-level Skills Manager and a low-level Worker. The method involves the Manager building a tiered skill library by summarizing successful solution traces and selecting relevant skills to condition rollouts, guided by a hierarchical reward design that co-evolves reasoning ability and library quality. Experimental results on seven benchmarks with two base models show ARISE consistently outperforms GRPO-family algorithms and memory-augmented baselines, especially on out-of-distribution tasks, with ablations confirming each component's contribution and the tandem improvement of library quality and reasoning performance.

Generalizable End-to-End Tool-Use RL with Synthetic CodeGym
Authors: Weihua Du, Hailei Gong, Zhan Ling, Kang Liu, Lingfeng Shen, Xuesong Yao, Yufei Xu, Dingyuan Shi, Yiming Yang, Jiecao Chen
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-09-22T03:03:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T01:17:09+00:00
Comments: 24 pages. Accepted to ICLR 2026. Project repository: https://github.com/StigLidu/CodeGym
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Tool-augmented large language models (LLMs), hereafter LLM agents, leverage external tools to solve diverse tasks and interface with the real world. However, current training practices largely rely on supervised fine-tuning (SFT) over static trajectories or reinforcement learning (RL) on narrow tasks, which generalize poorly beyond development settings and lead to brittleness with new tools and unseen workflows. Because code execution reflects many structural patterns of real-world workflows, we use coding problems as a structured substrate to build tool-use agent training environments with diverse task configurations. To this end, we introduce CodeGym, a scalable framework that synthesizes diverse, verifiable, and controllable multi-turn tool-use environments for agent RL, enabling LLM agents to explore and master various workflows actively. CodeGym converts static coding problems into interactive environments by extracting atomic functions or logic into callable tools, yielding verifiable tasks that span various tool-execution workflows. Models of varying sizes and chain-of-thought configurations trained in CodeGym exhibit consistent out-of-distribution generalizability; for example, Qwen2.5-32B-Instruct achieves an absolute accuracy gain of 8.7 points on the OOD benchmark $τ$-Bench. These results highlight CodeGym as a step toward scalable general-purpose RL environments for training tool-use behaviors that align with real-world agent workflows.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于合成CodeGym的可泛化端到端工具使用强化学习
工具增强型大语言模型（LLM智能体）通过调用外部工具解决多样化任务并与现实世界交互。然而，当前训练方法主要依赖静态轨迹的监督微调（SFT）或狭窄任务的强化学习（RL），导致其在开发环境外泛化能力弱，面对新工具与未知工作流时表现脆弱。鉴于代码执行能反映现实工作流的多种结构模式，我们以编程问题作为结构化载体，构建具有多样化任务配置的工具使用智能体训练环境。为此，我们提出CodeGym——一个可扩展的框架，通过合成多样化、可验证、可控的多轮次工具使用环境来支持智能体强化学习，使LLM智能体能主动探索并掌握各类工作流。CodeGym通过将原子函数或逻辑封装为可调用工具，将静态编程问题转化为交互式环境，生成涵盖多种工具执行流程的可验证任务。在CodeGym中训练的不同规模模型与思维链配置均展现出稳定的分布外泛化能力：例如Qwen2.5-32B-Instruct在OOD基准测试τ-Bench上实现了8.7个百分点的绝对准确率提升。这些成果标志着CodeGym向构建可扩展的通用强化学习环境迈出重要一步，其训练的工具使用行为能与现实智能体工作流有效对齐。

To overcome this, the authors introduce CodeGym, a framework that synthesizes diverse, verifiable multi-turn tool-use environments from coding problems, converting atomic functions into callable tools to enable active exploration through RL. Experimental results show that models trained in CodeGym achieve strong out-of-distribution generalization, with Qwen2.5-32B-Instruct gaining 8.7 accuracy points on the τ-Bench benchmark, demonstrating the framework's potential for scalable training of general-purpose tool-use agents.
本文针对当前基于监督微调或狭窄强化学习训练的工具增强大语言模型智能体泛化能力有限、难以适应新工具和工作流程的问题，提出CodeGym框架。该方法将静态编程问题转化为交互式环境，通过提取原子函数为可调用工具，构建多样化、可验证的多轮工具使用环境，以支持智能体通过强化学习主动探索。实验结果表明，在CodeGym中训练的模型展现出良好的分布外泛化性能，例如Qwen2.5-32B-Instruct在τ-Bench基准上准确率绝对提升8.7个百分点，这标志着向可扩展的通用工具使用行为训练环境迈出了重要一步。
Collaborative Temporal Feature Generation via Critic-Free Reinforcement Learning for Cross-User Sensor-Based Activity Recognition
Authors: Xiaozhou Ye, Feng Jiang, Zihan Wang, Xiulai Wang, Yutao Zhang, Kevin I-Kai Wang
First: 2026-03-17T01:03:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T01:03:21+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Human Activity Recognition using wearable inertial sensors is foundational to healthcare monitoring, fitness analytics, and context-aware computing, yet its deployment is hindered by cross-user variability arising from heterogeneous physiological traits, motor habits, and sensor placements. Existing domain generalization approaches either neglect temporal dependencies in sensor streams or depend on impractical target-domain annotations. We propose a different paradigm: modeling generalizable feature extraction as a collaborative sequential generation process governed by reinforcement learning. Our framework, CTFG (Collaborative Temporal Feature Generation), employs a Transformer-based autoregressive generator that incrementally constructs feature token sequences, each conditioned on prior context and the encoded sensor input. The generator is optimized via Group-Relative Policy Optimization, a critic-free algorithm that evaluates each generated sequence against a cohort of alternatives sampled from the same input, deriving advantages through intra-group normalization rather than learned value estimation. This design eliminates the distribution-dependent bias inherent in critic-based methods and provides self-calibrating optimization signals that remain stable across heterogeneous user distributions. A tri-objective reward comprising class discrimination, cross-user invariance, and temporal fidelity jointly shapes the feature space to separate activities, align user distributions, and preserve fine-grained temporal content. Evaluations on the DSADS and PAMAP2 benchmarks demonstrate state-of-the-art cross-user accuracy (88.53\% and 75.22\%), substantial reduction in inter-task training variance, accelerated convergence, and robust generalization under varying action-space dimensionalities.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于无评论者强化学习的跨用户传感器活动识别协同时序特征生成
利用可穿戴惯性传感器进行人体活动识别是健康监测、运动分析和情境感知计算的基础，但其部署受到跨用户差异性的阻碍，这种差异性源于异质的生理特征、运动习惯和传感器佩戴位置。现有领域泛化方法要么忽略传感器数据流中的时序依赖，要么依赖不切实际的目标域标注。我们提出一种新范式：将可泛化的特征提取建模为由强化学习驱动的协同序列生成过程。我们的CTFG框架采用基于Transformer的自回归生成器，逐步构建特征标记序列，每个序列均以前序上下文和编码后的传感器输入为条件。该生成器通过组相对策略优化进行优化——这是一种无评论者算法，通过将每个生成序列与同一输入采样的替代序列群组进行比较，利用组内归一化而非学习值估计来推导优势。该设计消除了基于评论者方法固有的分布依赖性偏差，并提供跨异质用户分布保持稳定的自校准优化信号。融合类别区分性、跨用户不变性和时序保真度的三重目标奖励，共同塑造特征空间以实现活动分离、用户分布对齐和细粒度时序内容保留。在DSADS和PAMAP2基准测试上的评估表明，本方法实现了最先进的跨用户准确率（88.53%和75.22%），显著降低了任务间训练方差，加速了收敛速度，并在不同动作空间维度下展现出鲁棒的泛化能力。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of cross-user variability in wearable sensor-based activity recognition, where differences in physiology, habits, and sensor placement degrade model performance. To overcome limitations of existing domain generalization methods that ignore temporal dependencies or require target-domain labels, the authors propose CTFG, a framework that formulates feature extraction as a collaborative sequential generation process using reinforcement learning. It employs a Transformer-based autoregressive generator optimized via a critic-free algorithm called Group-Relative Policy Optimization, which evaluates sequences against a group of alternatives to provide stable, bias-free training signals. Experiments on DSADS and PAMAP2 benchmarks show state-of-the-art cross-user accuracy (88.53% and 75.22%), reduced training variance, faster convergence, and robust generalization across different action spaces.
本文针对可穿戴传感器活动识别中的跨用户差异性问题展开研究，该问题因生理特征、运动习惯和传感器位置的不同而导致模型性能下降。为克服现有域泛化方法忽略时序依赖或需要目标域标注的局限，作者提出CTFG框架，将特征提取建模为基于强化学习的协作式序列生成过程。该方法采用基于Transformer的自回归生成器，并通过一种名为组相对策略优化的无评论家算法进行优化，该算法通过将生成序列与同组替代序列比较来提供稳定、无偏差的训练信号。在DSADS和PAMAP2基准测试上的实验表明，该方法实现了最先进的跨用户识别准确率（88.53%和75.22%），降低了训练方差，加速了收敛，并在不同动作空间维度下表现出鲁棒的泛化能力。
No More Blind Spots: Learning Vision-Based Omnidirectional Bipedal Locomotion for Challenging Terrain
Authors: Mohitvishnu S. Gadde, Pranay Dugar, Ashish Malik, Alan Fern
First: 2025-08-16T06:20:46+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T23:37:19+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Effective bipedal locomotion in dynamic environments, such as cluttered indoor spaces or uneven terrain, requires agile and adaptive movement in all directions. This necessitates omnidirectional terrain sensing and a controller capable of processing such input. We present a learning framework for vision-based omnidirectional bipedal locomotion, enabling seamless movement using depth images. A key challenge is the high computational cost of rendering omnidirectional depth images in simulation, making traditional sim-to-real reinforcement learning (RL) impractical. Our method combines a robust blind controller with a teacher policy that supervises a vision-based student policy, trained on noise-augmented terrain data to avoid rendering costs during RL and ensure robustness. We also introduce a data augmentation technique for supervised student training, accelerating training by up to 10 times compared to conventional methods. Our framework is validated through simulation and real-world tests, demonstrating effective omnidirectional locomotion with minimal reliance on expensive rendering. This is, to the best of our knowledge, the first demonstration of vision-based omnidirectional bipedal locomotion, showcasing its adaptability to diverse terrains.
中文标题/摘要
标题：消除盲区：面向复杂地形的视觉全向双足运动学习
在动态环境（如杂乱的室内空间或崎岖地形）中实现有效的双足运动，需要具备全向敏捷适应能力。这要求系统具备全向地形感知及能处理此类输入的控制器。本文提出一种基于视觉的全向双足运动学习框架，利用深度图像实现无缝运动。关键挑战在于仿真中渲染全向深度图像的高计算成本，使得传统的仿真到现实强化学习方法难以实施。我们的方法将鲁棒盲控控制器与教师策略相结合，通过监督基于视觉的学生策略进行训练。该策略在噪声增强地形数据上训练，避免了强化学习过程中的渲染成本并确保鲁棒性。我们还提出一种用于监督学生训练的数据增强技术，相比传统方法可加速训练达10倍。通过仿真和实际测试验证，该框架在最小化依赖昂贵渲染的情况下实现了有效的全向运动。据我们所知，这是首次展示基于视觉的全向双足运动，展现了其对多样化地形的适应能力。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of enabling bipedal robots to navigate complex, cluttered environments by developing a vision-based omnidirectional locomotion framework. The motivation stems from the need for agile, all-directional movement on uneven terrain, which requires processing omnidirectional visual input without the prohibitive computational cost of rendering full depth images in simulation for reinforcement learning. The proposed method combines a robust blind controller with a teacher-student policy approach, where a teacher supervises a vision-based student policy trained on noise-augmented terrain data to bypass rendering costs and enhance robustness; additionally, a data augmentation technique accelerates student training by up to 10 times. Experimental results from simulation and real-world tests validate the framework, demonstrating effective omnidirectional locomotion across diverse terrains with minimal reliance on expensive rendering, marking the first demonstration of vision-based omnidirectional bipedal locomotion.
本文针对双足机器人在复杂、杂乱环境中导航的挑战，提出了一种基于视觉的全向运动框架。其动机源于在崎岖地形上实现灵活、全向移动的需求，这需要处理全向视觉输入，同时避免在仿真中为强化学习渲染完整深度图像的高昂计算成本。所提方法结合了鲁棒的无视觉控制器与教师-学生策略方法，其中教师策略监督一个基于视觉的学生策略，该策略在噪声增强的地形数据上训练，以绕过渲染成本并提升鲁棒性；此外，一种数据增强技术将学生训练速度提升了高达10倍。仿真和真实世界实验结果表明，该框架在多种地形上实现了有效的全向运动，且对昂贵渲染的依赖最小，这标志着首次实现了基于视觉的双足全向运动。
Aligning Paralinguistic Understanding and Generation in Speech LLMs via Multi-Task Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Jingxiang Chen, Minseok Kim, Seong-Gyun Leem, Yin Huang, Rashi Rungta, Zhicheng Ouyang, Haibin Wu, Surya Teja Appini, Ankur Bansal, Yang Bai, Yue Liu, Florian Metze, Ahmed A Aly, Anuj Kumar, Ariya Rastrow, Zhaojiang Lin
First: 2026-03-16T22:54:12+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T22:54:12+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Speech large language models (LLMs) observe paralinguistic cues such as prosody, emotion, and non-verbal sounds--crucial for intent understanding. However, leveraging these cues faces challenges: limited training data, annotation difficulty, and models exploiting lexical shortcuts over paralinguistic signals. We propose multi-task reinforcement learning (RL) with chain-of-thought prompting that elicits explicit affective reasoning. To address data scarcity, we introduce a paralinguistics-aware speech LLM (PALLM) that jointly optimizes sentiment classification from audio and paralinguistics-aware response generation via a two-stage pipeline. Experiments demonstrate that our approach improves paralinguistics understanding over both supervised baselines and strong proprietary models (Gemini-2.5-Pro, GPT-4o-audio) by 8-12% on Expresso, IEMOCAP, and RAVDESS. The results show that modeling paralinguistic reasoning with multi-task RL is crucial for building emotionally intelligent speech LLMs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于多任务强化学习的语音大语言模型副语言理解与生成对齐研究
语音大语言模型（LLMs）能够感知韵律、情感和非语言声音等副语言线索——这对意图理解至关重要。然而，利用这些线索面临多重挑战：训练数据有限、标注困难，以及模型倾向于依赖词汇捷径而非副语言信号。我们提出结合思维链提示的多任务强化学习（RL）方法，以激发显式情感推理。为应对数据稀缺问题，我们引入具备副语言感知能力的语音大语言模型（PALLM），通过两阶段流程联合优化音频情感分类与副语言感知响应生成。实验表明，在Expresso、IEMOCAP和RAVDESS数据集上，我们的方法相较于监督基线模型及主流专有模型（Gemini-2.5-Pro、GPT-4o-audio），将副语言理解能力提升了8-12%。结果表明，采用多任务强化学习建模副语言推理对构建具备情感智能的语音大语言模型具有关键意义。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the challenge of enabling speech large language models (LLMs) to effectively understand and utilize paralinguistic cues like prosody and emotion, which are critical for intent understanding but hindered by data scarcity and models' tendency to rely on lexical shortcuts. The proposed method, named PALLM, employs a multi-task reinforcement learning framework with chain-of-thought prompting to elicit explicit affective reasoning, jointly optimizing sentiment classification from audio and paralinguistic-aware response generation in a two-stage pipeline. Experimental results on Expresso, IEMOCAP, and RAVDESS datasets show that this approach improves paralinguistic understanding by 8-12% over supervised baselines and strong proprietary models like Gemini-2.5-Pro and GPT-4o-audio, demonstrating its effectiveness for building emotionally intelligent speech LLMs.
