ExpertGen: Scalable Sim-to-Real Expert Policy Learning from Imperfect Behavior Priors
Authors: Zifan Xu, Ran Gong, Maria Vittoria Minniti, Ahmet Salih Gundogdu, Eric Rosen, Kausik Sivakumar, Riedana Yan, Zixing Wang, Di Deng, Peter Stone, Xiaohan Zhang, Karl Schmeckpeper
First: 2026-03-16T22:12:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T22:12:48+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Learning generalizable and robust behavior cloning policies requires large volumes of high-quality robotics data. While human demonstrations (e.g., through teleoperation) serve as the standard source for expert behaviors, acquiring such data at scale in the real world is prohibitively expensive. This paper introduces ExpertGen, a framework that automates expert policy learning in simulation to enable scalable sim-to-real transfer. ExpertGen first initializes a behavior prior using a diffusion policy trained on imperfect demonstrations, which may be synthesized by large language models or provided by humans. Reinforcement learning is then used to steer this prior toward high task success by optimizing the diffusion model's initial noise while keep original policy frozen. By keeping the pretrained diffusion policy frozen, ExpertGen regularizes exploration to remain within safe, human-like behavior manifolds, while also enabling effective learning with only sparse rewards. Empirical evaluations on challenging manipulation benchmarks demonstrate that ExpertGen reliably produces high-quality expert policies with no reward engineering. On industrial assembly tasks, ExpertGen achieves a 90.5% overall success rate, while on long-horizon manipulation tasks it attains 85% overall success, outperforming all baseline methods. The resulting policies exhibit dexterous control and remain robust across diverse initial configurations and failure states. To validate sim-to-real transfer, the learned state-based expert policies are further distilled into visuomotor policies via DAgger and successfully deployed on real robotic hardware.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ExpertGen：基于不完美行为先验的可扩展仿真到现实专家策略学习
学习泛化性强且鲁棒的行为克隆策略需要大量高质量的机器人数据。虽然人类演示（如通过遥操作）是专家行为的标准来源，但在现实世界中大规模获取此类数据成本极高。本文提出ExpertGen框架，通过在仿真中自动化专家策略学习来实现可扩展的仿真到现实迁移。ExpertGen首先利用在不完美演示数据上训练的扩散策略初始化行为先验，这些演示可由大语言模型合成或由人类提供。随后通过强化学习优化扩散模型的初始噪声（同时冻结原始策略），引导该先验实现高任务成功率。通过保持预训练扩散策略冻结，ExpertGen将探索范围正则化至安全、类人的行为流形，同时仅需稀疏奖励即可实现高效学习。在具有挑战性的操作基准测试中，实证评估表明ExpertGen无需奖励工程即可稳定生成高质量专家策略。在工业装配任务中达到90.5%的总成功率，在长时程操作任务中取得85%的总成功率，优于所有基线方法。所得策略展现出灵巧的控制能力，并在多样化初始配置与故障状态下保持鲁棒性。为验证仿真到现实迁移，习得的基于状态的专家策略通过DAgger进一步蒸馏为视觉运动策略，并成功部署于真实机器人硬件。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of acquiring large-scale, high-quality robotic demonstrations by introducing ExpertGen, a framework for scalable sim-to-real expert policy learning. The method initializes a behavior prior using a diffusion policy trained on imperfect demonstrations, then applies reinforcement learning to optimize the initial noise of the diffusion model while keeping the policy frozen, thereby steering it toward high task success without reward engineering. Experimental results on manipulation benchmarks show that ExpertGen achieves a 90.5% success rate on industrial assembly tasks and 85% on long-horizon tasks, outperforming baselines, with policies demonstrating robustness and successful sim-to-real transfer via distillation into visuomotor policies.
该论文针对获取大规模高质量机器人演示数据的挑战，提出了ExpertGen框架，用于实现可扩展的仿真到现实专家策略学习。该方法首先使用基于不完美演示训练的扩散策略初始化行为先验，然后通过强化学习优化扩散模型的初始噪声，同时保持策略冻结，从而无需奖励工程即可引导其实现高任务成功率。在操作基准测试中的实验结果表明，ExpertGen在工业装配任务上达到90.5%的成功率，在长时程操作任务上达到85%，优于所有基线方法，其策略表现出鲁棒性，并通过蒸馏为视觉运动策略成功实现了仿真到现实的迁移。
Data-Local Autonomous LLM-Guided Neural Architecture Search for Multiclass Multimodal Time-Series Classification
Authors: Emil Hardarson, Luka Biedebach, Ómar Bessi Ómarsson, Teitur Hrólfsson, Anna Sigridur Islind, María Óskarsdóttir
First: 2026-03-16T21:46:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T21:46:05+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Applying machine learning to sensitive time-series data is often bottlenecked by the iteration loop: Performance depends strongly on preprocessing and architecture, yet training often has to run on-premise under strict data-local constraints. This is a common problem in healthcare and other privacy-constrained domains (e.g., a hospital developing deep learning models on patient EEG). This bottleneck is particularly challenging in multimodal fusion, where sensor modalities must be individually preprocessed and then combined. LLM-guided neural architecture search (NAS) can automate this exploration, but most existing workflows assume cloud execution or access to data-derived artifacts that cannot be exposed. We present a novel data-local, LLM-guided search framework that handles candidate pipelines remotely while executing all training and evaluation locally under a fixed protocol. The controller observes only trial-level summaries, such as pipeline descriptors, metrics, learning-curve statistics, and failure logs, without ever accessing raw samples or intermediate feature representations. Our framework targets multiclass, multimodal learning via one-vs-rest binary experts per class and modality, a lightweight fusion MLP, and joint search over expert architectures and modality-specific preprocessing. We evaluate our method on two regimes: UEA30 (public multivariate time-series classification dataset) and SleepEDFx sleep staging (heterogeneous clinical modalities such as EEG, EOG, and EMG). The results show that the modular baseline model is strong, and the LLM-guided NAS further improves it. Notably, our method finds models that perform within published ranges across most benchmark datasets. Across both settings, our method reduces manual intervention by enabling unattended architecture search while keeping sensitive data on-premise.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向多类多模态时间序列分类的数据本地化自主LLM引导神经架构搜索
将机器学习应用于敏感时间序列数据常受限于迭代循环：性能高度依赖预处理与架构设计，但训练常需在严格的数据本地化约束下于本地执行。这在医疗等隐私敏感领域（如医院基于患者脑电图开发深度学习模型）尤为常见。多模态融合场景中该瓶颈更为突出，各传感器模态需分别预处理后再融合。LLM引导的神经架构搜索可自动化探索过程，但现有方案多假设云端执行或可访问无法公开的数据衍生产物。 我们提出一种新颖的数据本地化LLM引导搜索框架，在固定协议下远程处理候选流水线，所有训练与评估均在本地执行。控制器仅观测试验级摘要（如流水线描述符、指标、学习曲线统计与故障日志），不接触原始样本或中间特征表示。该框架通过为每个类别和模态构建一对多二元专家模型、轻量级融合多层感知机，以及对专家架构与模态特定预处理的联合搜索，实现多类多模态学习。 我们在两种场景评估方法：UEA30（公开多元时间序列分类数据集）与SleepEDFx睡眠分期（包含脑电图、眼动图、肌电图等异构临床模态）。结果表明模块化基线模型性能强劲，LLM引导的神经架构搜索可进一步提升其表现。值得注意的是，本方法在多数基准数据集上发现的模型性能均达到已发表范围。在两种场景中，本方法通过实现无人值守的架构搜索同时保持敏感数据本地化，显著减少了人工干预。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to develop machine learning models for sensitive time-series data, such as in healthcare, under strict data-local constraints that prevent cloud execution or data exposure, this paper introduces a novel data-local LLM-guided neural architecture search (NAS) framework. The method operates by having a remote controller propose candidate pipelines based only on trial-level summaries (e.g., metrics, logs) while all training and evaluation execute locally, and it specifically targets multiclass multimodal classification via per-class and per-modality binary experts with a fusion MLP, jointly searching over expert architectures and preprocessing. Experimental results on the UEA30 benchmark and a clinical sleep staging dataset (SleepEDFx) demonstrate that the framework improves upon a strong modular baseline, achieving performance within published ranges while enabling unattended search and keeping all sensitive data on-premise.
本文的动机是针对医疗等隐私敏感领域的时间序列数据，在严格的数据本地化约束下开发机器学习模型，避免云端执行或数据暴露。方法上提出了一种新颖的数据本地化、大语言模型引导的神经架构搜索框架，通过远程控制器仅基于试验级摘要提出候选流程，所有训练和评估均在本地执行，并针对多类多模态分类，采用每类每模态的二元专家和轻量级融合MLP，联合搜索专家架构和预处理。在UEA30公共数据集和SleepEDFx临床睡眠分期数据集上的实验结果表明，该框架在强模块化基线基础上进一步提升了性能，所得模型在大多数基准上达到已发表性能范围，同时实现了无人干预的架构搜索并确保敏感数据始终保留在本地。
Game-Theory-Assisted Reinforcement Learning for Border Defense: Early Termination based on Analytical Solutions
Authors: Goutam Das, Michael Dorothy, Kyle Volle, Daigo Shishika
First: 2026-03-16T20:54:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T20:54:07+00:00
Comments: 7 pages, ACC 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Game theory provides the gold standard for analyzing adversarial engagements, offering strong optimality guarantees. However, these guarantees often become brittle when assumptions such as perfect information are violated. Reinforcement learning (RL), by contrast, is adaptive but can be sample-inefficient in large, complex domains. This paper introduces a hybrid approach that leverages game-theoretic insights to improve RL training efficiency. We study a border defense game with limited perceptual range, where defender performance depends on both search and pursuit strategies, making classical differential game solutions inapplicable. Our method employs the Apollonius Circle (AC) to compute equilibrium in the post-detection phase, enabling early termination of RL episodes without learning pursuit dynamics. This allows RL to concentrate on learning search strategies while guaranteeing optimal continuation after detection. Across single- and multi-defender settings, this early termination method yields 10-20% higher rewards, faster convergence, and more efficient search trajectories. Extensive experiments validate these findings and demonstrate the overall effectiveness of our approach.
中文标题/摘要
标题：博弈论辅助的边境防御强化学习：基于解析解的早期终止策略
博弈论为分析对抗性博弈提供了黄金标准，具有强最优性保证。然而，当完美信息等假设被违反时，这些保证往往变得脆弱。相比之下，强化学习具有适应性，但在大规模复杂领域中可能存在样本效率低下的问题。本文提出一种混合方法，利用博弈论洞见提升强化学习训练效率。我们研究一种感知范围受限的边境防御博弈，其中防御者性能同时取决于搜索与追击策略，使得经典微分博弈解法不再适用。我们的方法采用阿波罗尼奥斯圆计算探测后阶段的均衡，实现强化学习回合的早期终止而无需学习追击动态。这使得强化学习能专注于学习搜索策略，同时保证探测后的最优延续。在单防御者与多防御者场景中，该早期终止方法获得10-20%的奖励提升、更快的收敛速度以及更高效的搜索轨迹。大量实验验证了这些发现，并证明了本方法的整体有效性。
Summary / 总结
This paper is motivated by the complementary strengths of game theory, which offers optimality guarantees under ideal assumptions, and reinforcement learning (RL), which is adaptive but sample-inefficient. The authors propose a hybrid method for a border defense game with limited perceptual range, where they use the Apollonius Circle to compute a game-theoretic equilibrium for the post-detection pursuit phase, enabling early termination of RL episodes. This allows the RL agent to focus solely on learning optimal search strategies while guaranteeing optimal pursuit. Experimental results show that this approach yields 10-20% higher rewards, faster convergence, and more efficient search trajectories in both single- and multi-defender scenarios.
本文的动机在于结合博弈论在理想假设下提供最优性保证的优势，与强化学习自适应但样本效率低的特性。针对感知范围有限的边境防御博弈，作者提出一种混合方法，利用阿波罗尼奥斯圆计算检测后追击阶段的博弈均衡，从而实现强化学习回合的提前终止。这使得智能体能专注于学习最优搜索策略，同时确保检测后的追击是最优的。实验结果表明，该方法在单防御者和多防御者场景下均能获得10-20%的更高奖励、更快的收敛速度以及更高效的搜索轨迹。
Counteractive RL: Rethinking Core Principles for Efficient and Scalable Deep Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Ezgi Korkmaz
Venue: NeurIPS 2025 Spotlight
First: 2026-03-16T19:59:37+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T19:59:37+00:00
Comments: NeurIPS 2025 Spotlight
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Following the pivotal success of learning strategies to win at tasks, solely by interacting with an environment without any supervision, agents have gained the ability to make sequential decisions in complex MDPs. Yet, reinforcement learning policies face exponentially growing state spaces in high dimensional MDPs resulting in a dichotomy between computational complexity and policy success. In our paper we focus on the agent's interaction with the environment in a high-dimensional MDP during the learning phase and we introduce a theoretically-founded novel paradigm based on experiences obtained through counteractive actions. Our analysis and method provide a theoretical basis for efficient, effective, scalable and accelerated learning, and further comes with zero additional computational complexity while leading to significant acceleration in training. We conduct extensive experiments in the Arcade Learning Environment with high-dimensional state representation MDPs. The experimental results further verify our theoretical analysis, and our method achieves significant performance increase with substantial sample-efficiency in high-dimensional environments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：对抗性强化学习：重新思考高效可扩展深度强化学习的核心原则
继仅通过与环境交互而无监督的学习策略在任务中取得关键成功后，智能体已能在复杂马尔可夫决策过程中进行序列决策。然而，在高维MDP中，强化学习策略面临状态空间指数级增长，导致计算复杂度与策略成功之间的二元对立。本文聚焦于学习阶段智能体在高维MDP中与环境的交互，提出一种基于对抗性行动经验的理论驱动新范式。我们的分析与方法为高效、可扩展的加速学习提供了理论基础，且不增加额外计算复杂度，同时显著加速训练过程。我们在具有高维状态表示的Arcade学习环境MDP中进行了广泛实验，结果进一步验证了理论分析，表明该方法在高维环境中实现了显著性能提升与样本效率突破。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of exponentially growing state spaces in high-dimensional Markov Decision Processes (MDPs), which creates a trade-off between computational complexity and policy success, this paper introduces a novel paradigm called Counteractive Reinforcement Learning. The method is theoretically grounded and leverages experiences obtained through counteractive actions during the agent's interaction with the environment, aiming to enable efficient, scalable, and accelerated learning without adding computational overhead. Main experimental results from extensive testing in the Arcade Learning Environment with high-dimensional state representations verify the theoretical analysis, showing that the method achieves significant performance improvements and substantial gains in sample efficiency.
本文的动机是解决高维马尔可夫决策过程中状态空间指数级增长所带来的计算复杂性与策略成功之间的权衡难题。方法上，论文提出了一种名为对抗性强化学习的新范式，其理论基础是在智能体与环境交互的学习阶段，利用通过对抗性行动获得的经验，旨在实现高效、可扩展且加速的学习，且不增加额外计算复杂度。主要实验结果基于在具有高维状态表示的街机学习环境中进行的广泛测试，验证了理论分析，表明该方法能显著提升性能并大幅提高样本效率。
Tail Distribution of Regret in Optimistic Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Sajad Khodadadian, Mehrdad Moharrami
First: 2025-11-23T02:23:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T19:23:19+00:00
Comments: 27 pages, 0 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We derive instance-dependent tail bounds for the regret of optimism-based reinforcement learning in finite-horizon tabular Markov decision processes with unknown transition dynamics. We first study a UCBVI-type (model-based) algorithm and characterize the tail distribution of the cumulative regret $R_K$ over $K$ episodes via explicit bounds on $P(R_K \ge x)$, going beyond analyses limited to $E[R_K]$ or a single high-probability quantile. We analyze two natural exploration-bonus schedules for UCBVI: (i) a $K$-dependent scheme that explicitly incorporates the total number of episodes $K$, and (ii) a $K$-independent (anytime) scheme that depends only on the current episode index. We then complement the model-based results with an analysis of optimistic Q-learning (model-free) under a $K$-dependent bonus schedule. Across both the model-based and model-free settings, we obtain upper bounds on $P(R_K \ge x)$ with a distinctive two-regime structure: a sub-Gaussian tail starting from an instance-dependent scale up to a transition threshold, followed by a sub-Weibull tail beyond that point. We further derive corresponding instance-dependent bounds on the expected regret $E[R_K]$. The proposed algorithms depend on a tuning parameter $α$, which balances the expected regret and the range over which the regret exhibits sub-Gaussian decay.
中文标题/摘要
标题：乐观强化学习中遗憾的尾部分布
我们在未知转移动态的有限时域表格化马尔可夫决策过程中，推导了基于乐观策略的强化学习遗憾的实例依赖性尾部边界。首先研究一种UCBVI型（基于模型）算法，通过显式边界 $P(R_K \ge x)$ 刻画 $K$ 幕中累积遗憾 $R_K$ 的尾部分布，突破了仅限于 $E[R_K]$ 或单一高概率分位数的分析框架。我们分析了UCBVI的两种自然探索奖励方案：（i）显式包含总幕数 $K$ 的 $K$ 依赖方案；（ii）仅依赖当前幕索引的 $K$ 无关（任意时间）方案。随后通过分析 $K$ 依赖奖励方案下的乐观Q学习（无模型方法）对基于模型的结果进行补充。在基于模型与无模型两种设定下，我们获得的 $P(R_K \ge x)$ 上界均呈现独特的双区制结构：从实例依赖尺度开始呈现亚高斯尾部直至过渡阈值，此后转为亚威布尔尾部。进一步推导了期望遗憾 $E[R_K]$ 的对应实例依赖边界。所提算法依赖调节参数 $α$，该参数平衡了期望遗憾与遗憾呈现亚高斯衰减的范围。
Summary / 总结
This paper is motivated by the need to understand the full tail distribution of regret in optimistic reinforcement learning, moving beyond analyses limited to expected regret or single high-probability bounds. The method involves deriving instance-dependent tail bounds for both model-based (UCBVI-type) and model-free (optimistic Q-learning) algorithms in finite-horizon tabular Markov decision processes, examining two exploration-bonus schedules: a K-dependent scheme and a K-independent anytime scheme. The main experimental results reveal a two-regime tail structure for the cumulative regret distribution: a sub-Gaussian tail up to an instance-dependent transition threshold, followed by a sub-Weibull tail beyond it, with corresponding bounds on expected regret that depend on a tuning parameter balancing regret magnitude and sub-Gaussian range.
本文的动机是研究乐观强化学习中遗憾值的完整尾部分布，超越仅限于期望遗憾或单一高概率界限的分析。方法上，针对有限时域表格马尔可夫决策过程，推导了模型基（UCBVI型）和模型无关（乐观Q学习）算法的实例依赖性尾部界限，并考察了两种探索奖励调度：K依赖方案和K无关的任意时间方案。主要实验结果表明，累积遗憾分布呈现双区制尾部结构：在实例依赖性转换阈值之前为亚高斯尾部，之后为亚威布尔尾部，同时得到了期望遗憾的相应界限，这些界限依赖于一个调节参数，以平衡遗憾大小和亚高斯衰减范围。
Descent-Guided Policy Gradient for Scalable Cooperative Multi-Agent Learning
Authors: Shan Yang, Yang Liu
First: 2026-02-23T17:45:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T18:56:19+00:00
Comments: 10 pages, 5 figures, 5 tables; plus 16 pages of appendices
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Scaling cooperative multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) is fundamentally limited by cross-agent noise. When agents share a common reward, the actions of all $N$ agents jointly determine each agent's learning signal, so cross-agent noise grows with $N$. In the policy gradient setting, per-agent gradient estimate variance scales as $Θ(N)$, yielding sample complexity $\mathcal{O}(N/ε)$. We observe that many domains, including cloud computing, transportation, and power systems, have differentiable analytical models that prescribe efficient system states. In this work, we propose Descent-Guided Policy Gradient (DG-PG), a framework that utilizes these analytical models to provide each agent with a noise-free gradient signal, decoupling each agent's gradient from the actions of all others. We prove that DG-PG reduces gradient variance from $Θ(N)$ to $\mathcal{O}(1)$, preserves the equilibria of the cooperative game, and achieves agent-independent sample complexity $\mathcal{O}(1/ε)$. On a heterogeneous cloud scheduling task with up to 200 agents, DG-PG converges within 10 episodes at every tested scale, from $N{=}5$ to $N{=}200$, directly confirming the predicted scale-invariant complexity, while MAPPO and IPPO fail to converge under identical architectures.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于下降引导策略梯度的可扩展协作多智能体学习
协作式多智能体强化学习（MARL）的可扩展性从根本上受限于跨智能体噪声。当智能体共享共同奖励时，所有N个智能体的行为共同决定每个智能体的学习信号，导致跨智能体噪声随N增长。在策略梯度设定中，单智能体梯度估计方差呈Θ(N)量级，样本复杂度达𝒪(N/ε)。我们观察到包括云计算、交通和电力系统在内的许多领域都存在可微分的解析模型，这些模型能规定高效的系统状态。本文提出下降引导策略梯度（DG-PG）框架，利用此类解析模型为每个智能体提供无噪声梯度信号，将各智能体梯度与其他所有智能体的行为解耦。我们证明DG-PG能将梯度方差从Θ(N)降至𝒪(1)，保持协作博弈的均衡性，并实现与智能体数量无关的样本复杂度𝒪(1/ε)。在最多200个智能体的异构云调度任务中，DG-PG在N=5至N=200的所有测试规模下均能在10个训练周期内收敛，直接验证了理论预测的规模无关复杂度，而相同架构下的MAPPO和IPPO方法均无法收敛。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the scalability challenge in cooperative multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL), where cross-agent noise causes per-agent gradient variance to scale linearly with the number of agents, leading to high sample complexity. To overcome this, the authors propose Descent-Guided Policy Gradient (DG-PG), a framework that leverages differentiable analytical models from domains like cloud computing to provide each agent with a noise-free, individualized gradient signal, thereby decoupling each agent's learning from others' actions. Theoretically, DG-PG reduces gradient variance from Θ(N) to O(1), preserves game equilibria, and achieves agent-independent sample complexity O(1/ε); experimentally, on a heterogeneous cloud scheduling task with up to 200 agents, DG-PG converges within 10 episodes across all scales, demonstrating scale-invariant performance, while baseline methods like MAPPO and IPPO fail to converge under the same conditions.
本文针对协作多智能体强化学习中的可扩展性问题，即跨智能体噪声导致每个智能体的梯度方差随智能体数量线性增长，从而带来高样本复杂度。为解决此问题，作者提出了下降引导策略梯度（DG-PG）框架，该框架利用来自云计算等领域的可微分分析模型，为每个智能体提供无噪声的个体化梯度信号，从而将每个智能体的学习与其他智能体的行为解耦。理论上，DG-PG将梯度方差从Θ(N)降低至O(1)，保持了博弈均衡，并实现了与智能体数量无关的样本复杂度O(1/ε)；实验上，在一个包含多达200个智能体的异构云调度任务中，DG-PG在从5到200的所有规模下均在10个回合内收敛，表现出规模不变的性能，而基线方法如MAPPO和IPPO在相同条件下无法收敛。
CorrectionPlanner: Self-Correction Planner with Reinforcement Learning in Autonomous Driving
Authors: Yihong Guo, Dongqiangzi Ye, Sijia Chen, Anqi Liu, Xianming Liu
First: 2026-03-16T18:03:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T18:03:21+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Autonomous driving requires safe planning, but most learning-based planners lack explicit self-correction ability: once an unsafe action is proposed, there is no mechanism to correct it. Thus, we propose CorrectionPlanner, an autoregressive planner with self-correction that models planning as motion-token generation within a propose, evaluate, and correct loop. At each planning step, the policy proposes an action, namely a motion token, and a learned collision critic predicts whether it will induce a collision within a short horizon. If the critic predicts a collision, we retain the sequence of historical unsafe motion tokens as a self-correction trace, generate the next motion token conditioned on it, and repeat this process until a safe motion token is proposed or the safety criterion is met. This self-correction trace, consisting of all unsafe motion tokens, represents the planner's correction process in motion-token space, analogous to a reasoning trace in language models. We train the planner with imitation learning followed by model-based reinforcement learning using rollouts from a pretrained world model that realistically models agents' reactive behaviors. Closed-loop evaluations show that CorrectionPlanner reduces collision rate by over 20% on Waymax and achieves state-of-the-art planning scores on nuPlan.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CorrectionPlanner：自动驾驶中基于强化学习的自校正规划器
自动驾驶需要安全规划，但多数基于学习的规划器缺乏显式自校正能力：一旦提出不安全动作，便无机制予以修正。为此，我们提出CorrectionPlanner——一种具备自校正能力的自回归规划器，它将规划建模为“提议-评估-校正”循环中的运动令牌生成过程。在每个规划步骤中，策略提出一个动作（即运动令牌），由习得的碰撞评判器预测该动作是否会在短期内引发碰撞。若评判器预测碰撞，则保留历史不安全运动令牌序列作为自校正轨迹，基于该轨迹生成下一运动令牌，并重复此过程直至提出安全运动令牌或满足安全准则。这条由所有不安全运动令牌构成的自校正轨迹，代表了规划器在运动令牌空间中的校正过程，类似于语言模型中的推理轨迹。我们通过模仿学习训练规划器，随后使用预训练世界模型（能真实模拟智能体反应行为）生成的推演数据进行基于模型的强化学习。闭环评估表明，CorrectionPlanner在Waymax数据集上降低碰撞率超20%，并在nuPlan基准上达到最先进的规划评分。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the lack of explicit self-correction mechanisms in learning-based autonomous driving planners, which can lead to unsafe actions without recovery. It introduces CorrectionPlanner, an autoregressive planner that operates in a propose-evaluate-correct loop: at each step, a policy proposes a motion token, a learned collision critic assesses its safety, and if unsafe, the planner retains a trace of unsafe tokens to condition further proposals until safety is achieved, akin to reasoning traces in language models. The method is trained with imitation learning followed by model-based reinforcement learning using a pretrained world model, and experimental results demonstrate a reduction in collision rate by over 20% on Waymax and state-of-the-art planning scores on nuPlan.
本文针对基于学习的自动驾驶规划器缺乏显式自我校正能力的问题，提出了一种自回归规划器CorrectionPlanner，它在提议-评估-校正循环中工作：每一步，策略提议一个运动令牌，学习的碰撞批评器评估其安全性，若不安全则保留不安全令牌轨迹以指导后续提议，直至满足安全标准，类似于语言模型中的推理轨迹。该方法通过模仿学习和基于模型的强化学习进行训练，使用预训练的世界模型生成模拟数据，实验结果表明，在Waymax上碰撞率降低超过20%，并在nuPlan上实现了最先进的规划分数。
Simulation Distillation: Pretraining World Models in Simulation for Rapid Real-World Adaptation
Authors: Jacob Levy, Tyler Westenbroek, Kevin Huang, Fernando Palafox, Patrick Yin, Shayegan Omidshafiei, Dong-Ki Kim, Abhishek Gupta, David Fridovich-Keil
First: 2026-03-16T18:00:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T18:00:23+00:00
Comments: Project website: https://sim-dist.github.io/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Simulation-to-real transfer remains a central challenge in robotics, as mismatches between simulated and real-world dynamics often lead to failures. While reinforcement learning offers a principled mechanism for adaptation, existing sim-to-real finetuning methods struggle with exploration and long-horizon credit assignment in the low-data regimes typical of real-world robotics. We introduce Simulation Distillation (SimDist), a sim-to-real framework that distills structural priors from a simulator into a latent world model and enables rapid real-world adaptation via online planning and supervised dynamics finetuning. By transferring reward and value models directly from simulation, SimDist provides dense planning signals from raw perception without requiring value learning during deployment. As a result, real-world adaptation reduces to short-horizon system identification, avoiding long-horizon credit assignment and enabling fast, stable improvement. Across precise manipulation and quadruped locomotion tasks, SimDist substantially outperforms prior methods in data efficiency, stability, and final performance. Project website and code: https://sim-dist.github.io/
中文标题/摘要
标题：仿真蒸馏：通过仿真预训练世界模型以实现快速现实世界适应
仿真到现实的迁移仍是机器人技术的核心挑战，仿真与真实世界动力学的不匹配常导致任务失败。虽然强化学习为适应提供了理论机制，但现有仿真到现实的微调方法在机器人领域典型的数据稀缺场景中，难以解决探索与长时程信用分配问题。我们提出仿真蒸馏（SimDist）框架，该框架将仿真器的结构化先验知识蒸馏至潜在世界模型，并通过在线规划与监督式动力学微调实现快速现实适应。通过直接从仿真迁移奖励与价值模型，SimDist能够从原始感知数据中提供密集的规划信号，无需在部署阶段进行价值学习。这使得现实世界适应简化为短时程系统辨识，规避了长时程信用分配问题，实现快速稳定的性能提升。在精密操控与四足机器人运动任务中，SimDist在数据效率、稳定性和最终性能上均显著超越现有方法。项目网站与代码：https://sim-dist.github.io/

From Passive Observer to Active Critic: Reinforcement Learning Elicits Process Reasoning for Robotic Manipulation
Authors: Yibin Liu, Yaxing Lyu, Daqi Gao, Zhixuan Liang, Weiliang Tang, Shilong Mu, Xiaokang Yang, Yao Mu
First: 2026-03-16T17:53:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T17:53:28+00:00
Comments: 31 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Accurate process supervision remains a critical challenge for long-horizon robotic manipulation. A primary bottleneck is that current video MLLMs, trained primarily under a Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) paradigm, function as passive "Observers" that recognize ongoing events rather than evaluating the current state relative to the final task goal. In this paper, we introduce PRIMO R1 (Process Reasoning Induced Monitoring), a 7B framework that transforms video MLLMs into active "Critics". We leverage outcome-based Reinforcement Learning to incentivize explicit Chain-of-Thought generation for progress estimation. Furthermore, our architecture constructs a structured temporal input by explicitly anchoring the video sequence between initial and current state images. Supported by the proposed PRIMO Dataset and Benchmark, extensive experiments across diverse in-domain environments and out-of-domain real-world humanoid scenarios demonstrate that PRIMO R1 achieves state-of-the-art performance. Quantitatively, our 7B model achieves a 50% reduction in the mean absolute error of specialized reasoning baselines, demonstrating significant relative accuracy improvements over 72B-scale general MLLMs. Furthermore, PRIMO R1 exhibits strong zero-shot generalization on difficult failure detection tasks. We establish state-of-the-art performance on RoboFail benchmark with 67.0% accuracy, surpassing closed-source models like OpenAI o1 by 6.0%.
中文标题/摘要
标题：从被动观察者到主动评判者：强化学习激发机器人操作的过程推理
精确的过程监督仍是长时程机器人操作的关键挑战。当前主要瓶颈在于，现有视频多模态大语言模型主要在监督微调范式下训练，仅作为被动“观察者”识别进行中的事件，而非评估当前状态相对于最终任务目标的进展。本文提出PRIMO R1（过程推理诱导监控）——一个70亿参数的框架，将视频多模态大语言模型转化为主动“评判者”。我们利用基于结果的强化学习激励显式的思维链生成以进行进度估计。此外，该架构通过将视频序列显式锚定在初始状态与当前状态图像之间，构建了结构化时序输入。基于提出的PRIMO数据集与基准测试，在多样域内环境及域外真实世界人形机器人场景中的大量实验表明，PRIMO R1实现了最先进的性能。量化数据显示，我们的70亿参数模型将专业推理基线的平均绝对误差降低50%，相对720亿参数通用多模态大语言模型实现显著精度提升。同时，PRIMO R1在困难故障检测任务上展现出强大的零样本泛化能力，在RoboFail基准测试中以67.0%准确率创下新纪录，较OpenAI o1等闭源模型提升6.0%。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the limitation of current video MLLMs, which act as passive observers in long-horizon robotic manipulation by merely recognizing events rather than actively evaluating progress toward task goals. To overcome this, the authors introduce PRIMO R1, a 7B framework that transforms video MLLMs into active critics using outcome-based reinforcement learning to incentivize explicit Chain-of-Thought reasoning for progress estimation, with a structured temporal input anchoring video between initial and current states. Experimental results show state-of-the-art performance, including a 50% reduction in mean absolute error compared to specialized baselines and a 67.0% accuracy on the RoboFail benchmark, surpassing larger models like OpenAI o1 by 6.0%, while demonstrating strong zero-shot generalization in failure detection tasks.
该论文针对当前视频多模态大语言模型在长时程机器人操作中仅作为被动观察者识别事件而非主动评估任务进展的局限性。为解决此问题，作者提出了PRIMO R1，一个7B规模的框架，通过基于结果的强化学习激励显式的思维链生成以进行进度估计，将视频MLLM转变为主动的“批评者”，并采用结构化时序输入将视频锚定在初始和当前状态图像之间。实验结果表明，该模型实现了最先进的性能，包括相比专用基线平均绝对误差降低50%，在RoboFail基准测试上达到67.0%的准确率，超过OpenAI o1等更大模型6.0%，同时在故障检测任务中展现出强大的零样本泛化能力。
Unbiased and Biased Variance-Reduced Forward-Reflected-Backward Splitting Methods for Stochastic Composite Inclusions
Authors: Quoc Tran-Dinh, Nghia Nguyen-Trung
First: 2026-03-16T17:39:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T17:39:25+00:00
Comments: 34 pages and 2 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper develops new variance-reduction techniques for the forward-reflected-backward splitting (FRBS) method to solve a class of possibly nonmonotone stochastic composite inclusions. Unlike unbiased estimators such as mini-batching, developing stochastic biased variants faces a fundamental technical challenge and has not been utilized before for inclusions and fixed-point problems. We fill this gap by designing a new framework that can handle both unbiased and biased estimators. Our main idea is to construct stochastic variance-reduced estimators for the forward-reflected direction and use them to perform iterate updates. First, we propose a class of unbiased variance-reduced estimators and show that increasing mini-batch SGD, loopless-SVRG, and SAGA estimators fall within this class. For these unbiased estimators, we establish a $\mathcal{O}(1/k)$ best-iterate convergence rate for the expected squared residual norm, together with almost-sure convergence of the iterate sequence to a solution. Consequently, we prove that the best oracle complexities for the $n$-finite-sum and expectation settings are $\mathcal{O}(n^{2/3}ε^{-2})$ and $\mathcal{O}(ε^{-10/3})$, respectively, when employing loopless-SVRG or SAGA, where $ε$ is a desired accuracy. Second, we introduce a new class of biased variance-reduced estimators for the forward-reflected direction, which includes SARAH, Hybrid SGD, and Hybrid SVRG as special instances. While the convergence rates remain valid for these biased estimators, the resulting oracle complexities are $\mathcal{O}(n^{3/4}ε^{-2})$ and $\mathcal{O}(ε^{-5})$ for the $n$-finite-sum and expectation settings, respectively. Finally, we conduct two numerical experiments on AUC optimization for imbalanced classification and policy evaluation in reinforcement learning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：无偏与有偏方差缩减前向反射后向分裂方法求解随机复合包含问题
本文针对求解一类可能非单调的随机复合包含问题，提出了新的前向反射后向分裂（FRBS）方法的方差缩减技术。与无偏估计器（如小批量采样）不同，开发有偏随机变体面临根本性技术挑战，此前尚未在包含问题与不动点问题中得到应用。我们通过设计一个能同时处理无偏与有偏估计器的新框架填补了这一空白。核心思想是构建前向反射方向的随机方差缩减估计器，并用于迭代更新。首先，我们提出一类无偏方差缩减估计器，证明递增小批量SGD、无环SVRG和SAGA估计器均属此类。针对这些无偏估计器，我们建立了期望残差平方范数的$\mathcal{O}(1/k)$最优迭代收敛率，以及迭代序列几乎必然收敛于解的结果。由此证明：当采用无环SVRG或SAGA时，$n$有限和与期望设置的最优Oracle复杂度分别为$\mathcal{O}(n^{2/3}ε^{-2})$和$\mathcal{O}(ε^{-10/3})$，其中$ε$为目标精度。其次，我们针对前向反射方向提出新的有偏方差缩减估计器类，其特例包括SARAH、混合SGD与混合SVRG。虽然收敛率对这些有偏估计器依然成立，但所得Oracle复杂度在$n$有限和与期望设置下分别为$\mathcal{O}(n^{3/4}ε^{-2})$和$\mathcal{O}(ε^{-5})$。最后，我们在不平衡分类的AUC优化与强化学习策略评估问题上进行了两组数值实验。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of solving stochastic composite inclusions, particularly nonmonotone ones, by developing new variance-reduction techniques for the forward-reflected-backward splitting method. The method constructs both unbiased and biased variance-reduced estimators for the forward-reflected direction to update iterates, incorporating estimators like increasing mini-batch SGD, SVRG, SAGA, SARAH, and Hybrid SGD. Experimental results demonstrate a best-iterate convergence rate of O(1/k) for unbiased estimators, with oracle complexities of O(n^{2/3}ε^{-2}) for finite-sum settings and O(ε^{-10/3}) for expectation settings, while biased estimators achieve complexities of O(n^{3/4}ε^{-2}) and O(ε^{-5}), validated through numerical tests on AUC optimization and reinforcement learning policy evaluation.
本文针对解决随机复合包含问题（特别是非单调情形）的挑战，开发了前向反射后向分裂方法的新方差缩减技术。该方法通过构建前向反射方向的无偏和有偏方差缩减估计器来更新迭代，整合了如递增小批量随机梯度下降、SVRG、SAGA、SARAH和混合随机梯度下降等估计器。实验结果表明，无偏估计器实现了O(1/k)的最佳迭代收敛率，在有限和设置下的Oracle复杂度为O(n^{2/3}ε^{-2})，期望设置下为O(ε^{-10/3})，而有偏估计器则达到O(n^{3/4}ε^{-2})和O(ε^{-5})的复杂度，并通过AUC优化和强化学习策略评估的数值实验得到验证。
Meta-TTRL: A Metacognitive Framework for Self-Improving Test-Time Reinforcement Learning in Unified Multimodal Models
Authors: Lit Sin Tan, Junzhe Chen, Xiaolong Fu, Lichen Ma, Junshi Huang, Jianzhong Shi, Yan Li, Lijie Wen
First: 2026-03-16T17:28:57+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T17:28:57+00:00
Comments: 8 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Existing test-time scaling (TTS) methods for unified multimodal models (UMMs) in text-to-image (T2I) generation primarily rely on search or sampling strategies that produce only instance-level improvements, limiting the ability to learn from prior inferences and accumulate knowledge across similar prompts. To overcome these limitations, we propose Meta-TTRL, a metacognitive test-time reinforcement learning framework. Meta-TTRL performs test-time parameter optimization guided by model-intrinsic monitoring signals derived from the meta-knowledge of UMMs, achieving self-improvement and capability-level improvement at test time. Extensive experiments demonstrate that Meta-TTRL generalizes well across three representative UMMs, including Janus-Pro-7B, BAGEL, and Qwen-Image, achieving significant gains on compositional reasoning tasks and multiple T2I benchmarks with limited data. We provide the first comprehensive analysis to investigate the potential of test-time reinforcement learning (TTRL) for T2I generation in UMMs. Our analysis further reveals a key insight underlying effective TTRL: metacognitive synergy, where monitoring signals align with the model's optimization regime to enable self-improvement.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Meta-TTRL：面向统一多模态模型自改进测试时强化学习的元认知框架
现有面向统一多模态模型文本到图像生成的测试时扩展方法主要依赖搜索或采样策略，仅能实现实例级改进，限制了从先前推理中学习及跨相似提示积累知识的能力。为突破这些局限，我们提出Meta-TTRL——一种元认知测试时强化学习框架。该框架基于从UMM元知识衍生的模型内在监控信号，指导测试时参数优化，实现测试阶段的自改进与能力层级提升。大量实验表明，Meta-TTRL在Janus-Pro-7B、BAGEL和Qwen-Image三种代表性UMM中均展现良好泛化性，在有限数据条件下于组合推理任务及多个T2I基准测试中取得显著提升。我们首次系统分析了测试时强化学习在UMM文本到图像生成中的潜力，并进一步揭示有效TTRL的核心机制：元认知协同效应——即监控信号与模型优化机制对齐以实现自改进。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the limitations of existing test-time scaling methods for unified multimodal models in text-to-image generation, which only achieve instance-level improvements and fail to accumulate knowledge across prompts. The proposed method, Meta-TTRL, is a metacognitive test-time reinforcement learning framework that uses model-intrinsic monitoring signals derived from meta-knowledge to guide parameter optimization, enabling self-improvement and capability-level enhancement during testing. Experimental results show that Meta-TTRL generalizes effectively across three models—Janus-Pro-7B, BAGEL, and Qwen-Image—yielding significant performance gains on compositional reasoning tasks and multiple benchmarks with limited data, while analysis reveals that metacognitive synergy between monitoring signals and optimization is key to its success.

Convergence of Distributionally Robust Q-Learning with Linear Function Approximation
Authors: Saptarshi Mandal, Yashaswini Murthy, R. Srikant
First: 2025-10-02T07:01:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T17:23:13+00:00
Comments: Preprint. 53 Pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Distributionally robust reinforcement learning (DRRL) focuses on designing policies that achieve good performance under model uncertainties. The goal is to maximize the worst-case long-term discounted reward, where the data for RL comes from a nominal model while the deployed environment can deviate from the nominal model within a prescribed uncertainty set. Existing convergence guarantees for DRRL are limited to tabular MDPs or are dependent on restrictive discount factor assumptions when function approximation is used. We present a convergence result for a robust Q-learning algorithm with linear function approximation without any discount factor restrictions. In this paper, the robustness is measured with respect to the total-variation distance uncertainty set. Our model free algorithm does not require generative access to the MDP and achieves an $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(1/ε^{4})$ sample complexity for an $ε$-accurate value estimate. Our results close a key gap between the empirical success of robust RL algorithms and the non-asymptotic guarantees enjoyed by their non-robust counterparts. The key ideas in the paper also extend in a relatively straightforward fashion to robust Temporal-Difference (TD) learning with function approximation. The robust TD learning algorithm is discussed in the Appendix.
中文标题/摘要
标题：分布鲁棒Q学习与线性函数逼近的收敛性
分布鲁棒强化学习（DRRL）专注于设计在模型不确定性下仍能保持良好性能的策略，其目标是在最坏情况下最大化长期折扣奖励。强化学习的数据来源于名义模型，而实际部署环境可能在预设的不确定性集合内偏离该模型。现有DRRL的收敛性保证仅限于表格化MDP，或在使用函数逼近时依赖于严格的折扣因子假设。本文提出了一种无折扣因子限制的线性函数逼近鲁棒Q学习算法的收敛性结果，其中鲁棒性通过全变差距离不确定性集合衡量。这种无模型算法无需生成MDP样本，对于ε精度值估计实现了$\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(1/ε^{4})$的样本复杂度。该研究填补了鲁棒强化学习算法实证成功与非鲁棒方法非渐近保证之间的关键空白。论文核心思想还可直接扩展至带函数逼近的鲁棒时序差分（TD）学习，相关算法在附录中讨论。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the lack of convergence guarantees for distributionally robust reinforcement learning (DRRL) with function approximation, which aims to optimize policies against worst-case model uncertainties. The authors propose a robust Q-learning algorithm using linear function approximation, with robustness defined via a total-variation distance uncertainty set, and prove its convergence without restrictive discount factor assumptions. Their model-free method achieves an Õ(1/ε⁴) sample complexity for an ε-accurate value estimate, bridging a theoretical gap between robust and non-robust RL algorithms, with extensions to robust TD learning also provided.
本文针对使用函数近似的分布鲁棒强化学习（DRRL）缺乏收敛性保证的问题展开研究，该领域旨在优化策略以应对最坏情况下的模型不确定性。作者提出了一种采用线性函数近似的鲁棒Q学习算法，其鲁棒性通过总变差距离不确定性集来定义，并在无限制性折扣因子假设的情况下证明了算法的收敛性。这种无模型方法实现了Õ(1/ε⁴)的样本复杂度以获得ε精确的值估计，从而弥合了鲁棒与非鲁棒强化学习算法之间的理论差距，文中还将其核心思想扩展至鲁棒时序差分学习。
Curriculum Reinforcement Learning from Easy to Hard Tasks Improves LLM Reasoning
Authors: Shubham Parashar, Shurui Gui, Xiner Li, Hongyi Ling, Sushil Vemuri, Blake Olson, Eric Li, Yu Zhang, James Caverlee, Dileep Kalathil, Shuiwang Ji
First: 2025-06-07T02:41:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T17:16:37+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
We aim to improve the reasoning capabilities of language models via reinforcement learning (RL). Recent RL post-trained models like DeepSeek-R1 have demonstrated reasoning abilities on mathematical and coding tasks. However, prior studies suggest that using RL alone to improve reasoning on inherently difficult tasks is less effective. Here, we draw inspiration from curriculum learning and propose to schedule tasks from easy to hard (E2H), allowing LLMs to build reasoning skills gradually. Our method is termed E2H Reasoner. Empirically, we observe that, although easy tasks are important initially, fading them out through appropriate scheduling is essential in preventing overfitting. Theoretically, we establish convergence guarantees for E2H Reasoner within an approximate policy iteration framework. We derive finite-sample complexity bounds and show that when tasks are appropriately decomposed and conditioned, learning through curriculum stages requires fewer total samples than direct learning. Experiments across multiple domains show that E2H Reasoner significantly improves the reasoning ability of small LLMs (1.5B to 3B), which otherwise struggle when trained with vanilla RL alone, highlighting the effectiveness of our method. Our code can be found on https://github.com/divelab/E2H-Reasoning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：从易到难任务的课程强化学习提升大语言模型推理能力
我们旨在通过强化学习提升语言模型的推理能力。近期经过强化学习后训练的模型（如DeepSeek-R1）已在数学与编程任务中展现出推理能力。然而，先前研究表明，单独使用强化学习改进固有困难任务的推理效果有限。受课程学习启发，我们提出从易到难的任务调度方法，使大语言模型能逐步构建推理技能，该方法称为E2H推理器。实证研究发现，虽然简单任务在初期至关重要，但通过合理调度逐步淡化这些任务对防止过拟合具有关键作用。理论上，我们在近似策略迭代框架内为E2H推理器建立了收敛保证，推导出有限样本复杂度边界，并证明当任务被恰当分解与条件化时，通过课程阶段学习所需总样本量少于直接学习。跨多领域实验表明，E2H推理器显著提升了中小规模大语言模型（1.5B至3B参数）的推理能力——这些模型若仅使用原始强化学习训练则表现欠佳，从而凸显了本方法的有效性。代码已开源：https://github.com/divelab/E2H-Reasoning。
Summary / 总结
This paper aims to enhance the reasoning capabilities of language models through reinforcement learning (RL), motivated by the observation that applying RL directly to difficult reasoning tasks is often ineffective. The proposed method, E2H Reasoner, introduces a curriculum learning strategy that schedules tasks from easy to hard, allowing models to build skills gradually; it also incorporates a fading mechanism for easy tasks to prevent overfitting. Theoretically, the approach is supported by convergence guarantees and sample complexity bounds showing efficiency gains. Experimentally, it significantly improves the reasoning performance of small LLMs (1.5B-3B parameters) on mathematical and coding tasks, outperforming standard RL training.

DOT: Dynamic Knob Selection and Online Sampling for Automated Database Tuning
Authors: Yifan Wang, Debabrota Basu, Pierre Bourhis, Romain Rouvoy, Patrick Royer
First: 2026-03-16T17:05:34+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T17:05:34+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Database Management Systems (DBMS) are crucial for efficient data management and access control, but their administration remains challenging for Database Administrators (DBAs). Tuning, in particular, is known to be difficult. Modern systems have many tuning parameters, but only a subset significantly impacts performance. Focusing on these influential parameters reduces the search space and optimizes performance. Current methods rely on costly warm-up phases and human expertise to identify important tuning parameters. In this paper, we present DOT, a dynamic knob selection and online sampling DBMS tuning algorithm. DOT uses Recursive Feature Elimination with Cross-Validation (RFECV) to prune low-importance tuning parameters and a Likelihood Ratio Test (LRT) strategy to balance exploration and exploitation. For parameter search, DOT uses a Bayesian Optimization (BO) algorithm to optimize configurations on-the-fly, eliminating the need for warm-up phases or prior knowledge (although existing knowledge can be incorporated). Experiments show that DOT achieves matching or outperforming performance compared to state-of-the-art tuners while substantially reducing tuning overhead.
中文标题/摘要
标题：DOT：面向自动化数据库调优的动态参数选择与在线采样方法
数据库管理系统（DBMS）对高效数据管理与访问控制至关重要，但其管理对数据库管理员（DBA）仍具挑战性，尤其调优环节尤为困难。现代系统包含大量调优参数，但仅部分参数对性能产生显著影响。聚焦关键参数可缩减搜索空间并优化性能。现有方法依赖高成本预热阶段与人工经验识别重要参数。本文提出DOT——一种动态参数选择与在线采样的DBMS调优算法。DOT采用交叉验证递归特征消除（RFECV）剪枝低重要性参数，并运用似然比检验（LRT）策略平衡探索与利用。在参数搜索层面，DOT采用贝叶斯优化（BO）算法实时优化配置，无需预热阶段或先验知识（但可兼容既有知识）。实验表明，DOT在显著降低调优开销的同时，其性能达到或超越现有先进调优器。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of tuning complex database systems with many parameters, where only a subset significantly affects performance, this paper introduces DOT, an automated tuning algorithm. The method dynamically selects influential tuning knobs using Recursive Feature Elimination with Cross-Validation (RFECV) and employs a Likelihood Ratio Test (LRT) strategy for exploration-exploitation balance, alongside Bayesian Optimization (BO) for online configuration search without requiring warm-up phases. Experimental results demonstrate that DOT matches or surpasses state-of-the-art tuners in performance while substantially reducing tuning overhead.
针对数据库系统调优参数众多且仅部分关键参数影响性能的挑战，本文提出了DOT自动调优算法。该方法采用递归特征消除与交叉验证动态选择重要调优旋钮，利用似然比检验策略平衡探索与利用，并结合贝叶斯优化进行在线配置搜索，无需预热阶段。实验结果表明，DOT在性能上达到或超越了先进调优器，同时显著降低了调优开销。
Deep Reinforcement Learning for Fano Hypersurfaces
Authors: Marc Truter
First: 2026-03-16T15:42:12+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T15:42:12+00:00
Comments: 10 pages, 10 figures, 1 table
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We design a deep reinforcement learning algorithm to explore a high-dimensional integer lattice with sparse rewards, training a feedforward neural network as a dynamic search heuristic to steer exploration toward reward dense regions. We apply this to the discovery of Fano 4-fold hypersurfaces with terminal singularities, objects of central importance in algebraic geometry. Fano varieties with terminal singularities are fundamental building blocks of algebraic varieties, and explicit examples serve as a vital testing ground for the development and generalisation of theory. Despite decades of effort, the combinatorial intractability of the underlying search space has left this classification severely incomplete. Our reinforcement learning approach yields thousands of previously unknown examples, hundreds of which we show are inaccessible to known search methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向Fano超曲面的深度强化学习
我们设计了一种深度强化学习算法，用于探索具有稀疏奖励的高维整数格点，训练前馈神经网络作为动态搜索启发式方法，引导探索朝向奖励密集区域。我们将此方法应用于发现具有终端奇点的Fano四重超曲面——这是代数几何中至关重要的研究对象。具有终端奇点的Fano簇是代数簇的基本构成单元，其具体实例为理论发展与推广提供了关键的验证平台。尽管经过数十年的努力，底层搜索空间的组合复杂性使得该分类工作仍极不完整。我们的强化学习方法产生了数千个先前未知的实例，其中数百个被证明是现有搜索方法无法触及的。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the long-standing and combinatorially intractable challenge of classifying Fano varieties with terminal singularities—fundamental objects in algebraic geometry—this paper develops a deep reinforcement learning algorithm to efficiently explore high-dimensional integer lattices with sparse rewards. The method trains a feedforward neural network as a dynamic heuristic to steer the search toward reward-dense regions, specifically targeting the discovery of Fano 4-fold hypersurfaces. The main experimental result is the successful generation of thousands of previously unknown examples, with hundreds confirmed to be inaccessible to traditional search techniques, thereby significantly advancing the explicit classification of these geometric structures.

Listening to the Echo: User-Reaction Aware Policy Optimization via Scalar-Verbal Hybrid Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Jing Ye, Xinpei Zhao, Lu Xiang, Yaping Zhang, Chengqing Zong
First: 2026-03-16T15:39:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T15:39:54+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
While current emotional support dialogue systems typically rely on expert-defined scalar rewards for alignment, these signals suffer from severe information sparsity. They cannot explain why a response failed or how to adapt to dynamic user states, often diverging from the actual goal of facilitating positive emotional shifts. In practice, the most direct and reliable learning signal emerges from the user's continuous reactions during ongoing interaction. We therefore propose Reaction Aware Policy Optimization (RAPO), a framework that optimizes over interaction consequences rather than rubric scores. RAPO treats dialogue as a reaction-driven process and utilizes simulated user responses to generate dense natural-language feedback through three core components: Hindsight Dialogue Selection, which isolates pivotal turns that meaningfully alter user emotional trajectories; Generative Hindsight Feedback, which transforms user reactions into contrastive ranking signals and natural-language critiques; and Scalar-Verbal Hybrid Policy Optimization, which couples scalar reward optimization for global alignment with verbal feedback distillation for fine-grained semantic refinement. Extensive experiments on ESC and Sotopia demonstrate that RAPO significantly outperforms strong reinforcement learning baselines in driving positive interaction outcomes.
中文标题/摘要
标题：倾听回声：基于标量-语言混合强化学习的用户反应感知策略优化
当前情感支持对话系统通常依赖专家定义的标量奖励进行对齐，但这些信号存在严重的信息稀疏性问题。它们无法解释响应失败的原因或如何适应动态用户状态，常偏离促进积极情绪转变的实际目标。实践中，最直接可靠的学习信号来自用户在持续交互中的实时反应。为此，我们提出反应感知策略优化框架，该框架基于交互结果而非评分规则进行优化，将对话视为反应驱动的过程，通过三大核心组件利用模拟用户反应生成稠密的自然语言反馈：后见对话选择——识别显著改变用户情绪轨迹的关键对话轮次；生成式后见反馈——将用户反应转化为对比排序信号与自然语言评述；标量-语言混合策略优化——耦合标量奖励优化实现全局对齐，结合语言反馈蒸馏完成细粒度语义优化。在ESC与Sotopia数据集上的大量实验表明，该框架在促进积极交互结果方面显著优于主流强化学习基线。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of sparse, expert-defined scalar rewards in emotional support dialogue systems, which fail to capture dynamic user states and explain response failures, this paper proposes Reaction Aware Policy Optimization (RAPO). The method treats dialogue as a reaction-driven process, using simulated user responses to generate dense natural-language feedback through three components: selecting pivotal dialogue turns, transforming reactions into contrastive rankings and critiques, and combining scalar rewards with verbal feedback for policy optimization. Experimental results on ESC and Sotopia datasets show that RAPO significantly outperforms strong reinforcement learning baselines in achieving positive interaction outcomes.
针对情感支持对话系统中专家定义的标量奖励信号稀疏、无法解释响应失败或适应动态用户状态的问题，本文提出了反应感知策略优化（RAPO）。该方法将对话视为反应驱动的过程，利用模拟用户响应生成密集的自然语言反馈，其核心包括：选择能改变用户情感轨迹的关键对话轮次，将用户反应转化为对比排序信号和自然语言批评，以及结合标量奖励优化与语言反馈精炼进行策略学习。在ESC和Sotopia数据集上的实验表明，RAPO在促进积极互动结果方面显著优于现有强化学习基线方法。
MA-VLCM: A Vision Language Critic Model for Value Estimation of Policies in Multi-Agent Team Settings
Authors: Shahil Shaik, Aditya Parameshwaran, Anshul Nayak, Jonathon M. Smereka, Yue Wang
First: 2026-03-16T15:29:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T15:29:41+00:00
Comments: 7 pages, 6 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) commonly relies on a centralized critic to estimate the value function. However, learning such a critic from scratch is highly sample-inefficient and often lacks generalization across environments. At the same time, large vision-language-action models (VLAs) trained on internet-scale data exhibit strong multimodal reasoning and zero-shot generalization capabilities, yet directly deploying them for robotic execution remains computationally prohibitive, particularly in heterogeneous multi-robot systems with diverse embodiments and resource constraints. To address these challenges, we propose Multi-Agent Vision-Language-Critic Models (MA-VLCM), a framework that replaces the learned centralized critic in MARL with a pretrained vision-language model fine-tuned to evaluate multi-agent behavior. MA-VLCM acts as a centralized critic conditioned on natural language task descriptions, visual trajectory observations, and structured multi-agent state information. By eliminating critic learning during policy optimization, our approach significantly improves sample efficiency while producing compact execution policies suitable for deployment on resource-constrained robots. Results show good zero-shot return estimation on models with differing VLM backbones on in-distribution and out-of-distribution scenarios in multi-agent team settings
中文标题/摘要
标题：MA-VLCM：面向多智能体团队策略价值评估的视觉语言评论家模型
多智能体强化学习通常依赖集中式评论家进行价值函数估计，但从头学习此类评论家样本效率低下且泛化能力不足。尽管基于互联网数据训练的大型视觉语言动作模型具备强大的多模态推理与零样本泛化能力，但其直接部署于机器人系统仍面临计算成本过高的问题，尤其在异构多机器人系统中。为此，我们提出多智能体视觉语言评论家模型框架，该框架通过微调预训练的视觉语言模型替代传统学习型集中式评论家，使其能够基于自然语言任务描述、视觉轨迹观测与结构化多智能体状态信息评估群体行为。该方法在策略优化过程中省去评论家学习环节，显著提升样本效率，同时生成适用于资源受限机器人的紧凑执行策略。实验表明，采用不同视觉语言模型骨干的MA-VLCM在多智能体团队场景的分布内与分布外任务中均展现出良好的零样本回报估计能力。

The paper is motivated by the sample inefficiency and limited generalization of learned centralized critics in multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL), alongside the prohibitive computational cost of directly deploying large vision-language-action models for robotic execution. The method introduces MA-VLCM, a framework that replaces the learned critic with a pretrained vision-language model fine-tuned to evaluate multi-agent behavior, using natural language task descriptions, visual trajectories, and structured state information as input. Experimental results demonstrate that this approach significantly improves sample efficiency, produces compact policies for resource-constrained robots, and shows good zero-shot return estimation across both in-distribution and out-of-distribution scenarios with different VLM backbones.
