Amplification Effects in Test-Time Reinforcement Learning: Safety and Reasoning Vulnerabilities
Authors: Vanshaj Khattar, Md Rafi ur Rashid, Moumita Choudhury, Jing Liu, Toshiaki Koike-Akino, Ming Jin, Ye Wang
First: 2026-03-16T15:28:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T15:28:59+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Test-time training (TTT) has recently emerged as a promising method to improve the reasoning abilities of large language models (LLMs), in which the model directly learns from test data without access to labels. However, this reliance on test data also makes TTT methods vulnerable to harmful prompt injections. In this paper, we investigate safety vulnerabilities of TTT methods, where we study a representative self-consistency-based test-time learning method: test-time reinforcement learning (TTRL), a recent TTT method that improves LLM reasoning by rewarding self-consistency using majority vote as a reward signal. We show that harmful prompt injection during TTRL amplifies the model's existing behaviors, i.e., safety amplification when the base model is relatively safe, and harmfulness amplification when it is vulnerable to the injected data. In both cases, there is a decline in reasoning ability, which we refer to as the reasoning tax. We also show that TTT methods such as TTRL can be exploited adversarially using specially designed "HarmInject" prompts to force the model to answer jailbreak and reasoning queries together, resulting in stronger harmfulness amplification. Overall, our results highlight that TTT methods that enhance LLM reasoning by promoting self-consistency can lead to amplification behaviors and reasoning degradation, highlighting the need for safer TTT methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：测试时强化学习中的放大效应：安全性与推理漏洞
测试时训练作为一种提升大语言模型推理能力的新兴方法，允许模型在无标签情况下直接从测试数据中学习，但这也使其易受有害提示注入攻击。本文聚焦于测试时强化学习这一基于自一致性的代表性方法，探讨其安全漏洞。研究发现，有害提示注入会放大模型的既有行为：当基础模型相对安全时，会引发安全性放大；当模型易受注入数据影响时，则导致危害性放大。两种情形均伴随推理能力下降，即“推理税”。研究进一步表明，攻击者可通过特制的“HarmInject”提示，迫使模型同时处理越狱查询与推理任务，加剧危害性放大。这些发现揭示，依赖自一致性的测试时训练方法在提升推理能力的同时，可能引发行为放大与推理退化，凸显了开发更安全测试时训练方法的迫切性。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates safety vulnerabilities in test-time reinforcement learning (TTRL), a method that enhances large language model reasoning by rewarding self-consistency using majority vote. The motivation stems from the risk that TTRL's reliance on unlabeled test data makes it susceptible to harmful prompt injections. The method involves analyzing how such injections during TTRL amplify the model's existing behaviors: safety amplification occurs if the base model is safe, while harmfulness amplification happens if it is vulnerable, both accompanied by a reasoning ability decline termed the "reasoning tax." Experimental results demonstrate that adversarial "HarmInject" prompts can exploit TTRL to force models to answer jailbreak and reasoning queries jointly, leading to stronger harmfulness amplification and highlighting the need for safer test-time training approaches.
本文研究了测试时强化学习（TTRL）的安全漏洞，该方法通过多数投票奖励自洽性来增强大语言模型的推理能力。研究动机在于TTRL依赖未标记测试数据，易受有害提示注入攻击。方法上，分析了在TTRL过程中此类注入如何放大模型的现有行为：若基础模型相对安全则出现安全放大，若易受攻击则出现有害性放大，两者均伴随推理能力下降，称为“推理税”。实验结果表明，对抗性设计的“HarmInject”提示可利用TTRL迫使模型同时处理越狱和推理查询，导致更强的有害性放大，凸显了开发更安全测试时训练方法的必要性。
CASHomon Sets: Efficient Rashomon Sets Across Multiple Model Classes and their Hyperparameters
Authors: Fiona Katharina Ewald, Martin Binder, Matthias Feurer, Bernd Bischl, Giuseppe Casalicchio
First: 2026-03-16T14:12:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T14:12:05+00:00
Comments: Equal contributions by Fiona Katharina Ewald and Martin Binder
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Rashomon sets are model sets within one model class that perform nearly as well as a reference model from the same model class. They reveal the existence of alternative well-performing models, which may support different interpretations. This enables selecting models that match domain knowledge, hidden constraints, or user preferences. However, efficient construction methods currently exist for only a few model classes. Applied machine learning usually searches many model classes, and the best class is unknown beforehand. We therefore study Rashomon sets in the combined algorithm selection and hyperparameter optimization (CASH) setting and call them CASHomon sets. We propose TruVaRImp, a model-based active learning algorithm for level set estimation with an implicit threshold, and provide convergence guarantees. On synthetic and real-world datasets, TruVaRImp reliably identifies CASHomon sets members and matches or outperforms naive sampling, Bayesian optimization, classical and implicit level set estimation methods, and other baselines. Our analyses of predictive multiplicity and feature-importance variability across model classes question the common practice of interpreting data through a single model class.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CASHomon集合：跨多模型类别及其超参数的高效Rashomon集合
Rashomon集合指同一模型类别中性能接近参考模型的模型集合，其揭示了存在其他性能优异的替代模型，这些模型可能支持不同的解释。这使得选择符合领域知识、隐藏约束或用户偏好的模型成为可能。然而，目前仅少数模型类别具备高效的构建方法。应用机器学习通常需搜索多个模型类别，且最佳类别事先未知。因此，我们研究组合算法选择与超参数优化（CASH）设定下的Rashomon集合，并将其称为CASHomon集合。我们提出TruVaRImp——一种基于模型的主动学习算法，用于具有隐式阈值的水平集估计，并提供收敛性保证。在合成和真实数据集上，TruVaRImp能可靠识别CASHomon集合成员，其性能匹配或优于朴素采样、贝叶斯优化、经典与隐式水平集估计方法及其他基线。我们对跨模型类别的预测多重性和特征重要性变异性的分析，对通过单一模型类别解释数据的常见实践提出了质疑。
Summary / 总结
The study is motivated by the need to identify diverse, well-performing models across multiple model classes and hyperparameters, moving beyond the limitations of Rashomon sets confined to a single model class. The authors introduce CASHomon sets within the combined algorithm selection and hyperparameter optimization (CASH) framework and propose TruVaRImp, a model-based active learning algorithm for level set estimation with implicit thresholds, supported by convergence guarantees. Experimental results on synthetic and real-world datasets show that TruVaRImp reliably identifies CASHomon set members and outperforms naive sampling, Bayesian optimization, and other baseline methods, while analyses reveal significant predictive multiplicity and feature-importance variability across model classes, challenging the reliance on single-model interpretations.
本研究旨在解决现有Rashomon集合仅限于单一模型类别的局限，需在多个模型类别和超参数中寻找多样化的高性能模型。作者在组合算法选择和超参数优化（CASH）框架下提出CASHomon集合，并设计了TruVaRImp算法，这是一种基于模型的主动学习方法，用于具有隐式阈值的水平集估计，且提供了收敛性保证。在合成和真实数据集上的实验结果表明，TruVaRImp能可靠识别CASHomon集合成员，其性能优于朴素采样、贝叶斯优化及其他基线方法；分析还揭示了跨模型类别的预测多重性和特征重要性变异，质疑了依赖单一模型进行数据解释的常见做法。
Evolutionary Transfer Learning for Dragonchess
Authors: Jim O'Connor, Annika Hoag, Sarah Goyette, Gary B. Parker
First: 2026-03-16T13:58:16+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T13:58:16+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Dragonchess, a three-dimensional chess variant introduced by Gary Gygax, presents unique strategic and computational challenges that make it an ideal environment for studying the transfer of artificial intelligence (AI) heuristics across domains. In this work, we introduce Dragonchess as a novel testbed for AI research and provide an open-source, Python-based game engine for community use. Our research investigates evolutionary transfer learning by adapting heuristic evaluation functions directly from Stockfish, a leading chess engine, and subsequently optimizing them using Covariance Matrix Adaptation Evolution Strategy (CMA-ES). Initial trials showed that direct heuristic transfers were inadequate due to Dragonchess's distinct multi-layer structure and movement rules. However, evolutionary optimization significantly improved AI agent performance, resulting in superior gameplay demonstrated through empirical evaluation in a 50-round Swiss-style tournament. This research establishes the effectiveness of evolutionary methods in adapting heuristic knowledge to structurally complex, previously unexplored game domains.
中文标题/摘要
标题：龙棋进化迁移学习研究
龙棋是由加里·吉盖克斯提出的三维象棋变体，其独特的战略与计算挑战使其成为研究跨领域人工智能启发式迁移的理想环境。本研究将龙棋确立为人工智能研究的新型测试平台，并提供了开源Python游戏引擎供社区使用。我们通过直接移植顶尖国际象棋引擎Stockfish的启发式评估函数，并采用协方差矩阵自适应进化策略进行优化，探索了进化迁移学习方法。初步实验表明，由于龙棋特有的多层结构与移动规则，直接启发式迁移效果有限。但进化优化显著提升了智能体性能，通过在50轮瑞士制锦标赛中的实证评估，验证了优化后智能体具备更优的对弈能力。本研究证实了进化方法在将启发式知识适配至结构复杂、未经探索游戏领域的有效性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to study AI heuristic transfer in complex, unexplored domains, this paper introduces Dragonchess as a novel testbed and provides an open-source engine. The method involves directly transferring heuristic evaluation functions from the Stockfish chess engine and then optimizing them using the Covariance Matrix Adaptation Evolution Strategy (CMA-ES). The main experimental results showed that direct transfer was insufficient for Dragonchess's unique structure, but subsequent evolutionary optimization significantly enhanced AI performance, as empirically validated in a 50-round tournament, establishing the effectiveness of this approach for complex game domains.
本研究旨在探索人工智能启发式知识在复杂、未开发领域的迁移，为此引入了龙棋作为新的测试平台并提供了开源引擎。方法上，它直接从顶级国际象棋引擎Stockfish迁移启发式评估函数，随后使用协方差矩阵自适应进化策略进行优化。主要实验结果表明，直接迁移因龙棋独特的立体结构和规则而效果不佳，但后续的进化优化显著提升了智能体的性能，这在50轮瑞士制锦标赛中得到了实证验证，从而确立了该方法在适应结构复杂的游戏领域上的有效性。
Evaluating the Robustness of Reinforcement Learning based Adaptive Traffic Signal Control
Authors: Dickens Kwesiga, Angshuman Guin, Khaled Abdelghany, Michael Hunter
First: 2026-03-16T13:47:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T13:47:08+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) has attracted increasing interest for adaptive traffic signal control due to its model-free ability to learn control policies directly from interaction with the traffic environment. However, several challenges remain before RL-based signal control can be considered ready for field deployment. Many existing studies rely on simplified signal timing structures, robustness of trained models under varying traffic demand conditions remains insufficiently evaluated, and runtime efficiency continues to pose challenges when training RL algorithms in traffic microscopic simulation environments. This study formulates an RL-based signal control algorithm capable of representing a full eight-phase ring-barrier configuration consistent with field signal controllers. The algorithm is trained and evaluated under varying traffic demand conditions and benchmarked against state-of-the-practice actuated signal control (ASC). To assess robustness, experiments are conducted across multiple traffic volumes and origin-destination (O-D) demand patterns with varying levels of structural similarity. To improve training efficiency, a distributed asynchronous training architecture is implemented that enables parallel simulation across multiple computing nodes. Results from a case study intersection show that the proposed RL-based signal control significantly outperforms optimized ASC, reducing average delay by 11-32% across movements. A model trained on a single O-D pattern generalizes well to similar unseen demand patterns but degrades under substantially different demand conditions. In contrast, a model trained on diverse O-D patterns demonstrates strong robustness, consistently outperforming ASC even under highly dissimilar unseen demand scenarios.
中文标题/摘要
标题：评估基于强化学习的自适应交通信号控制鲁棒性
强化学习因其无需模型、可直接通过与交通环境交互学习控制策略的能力，在自适应交通信号控制领域受到日益关注。然而，基于强化学习的信号控制在实际部署前仍面临诸多挑战：现有研究多依赖简化的信号配时结构，训练模型在不同交通需求条件下的鲁棒性评估不足，且在交通微观仿真环境中训练强化学习算法的运行效率仍存在瓶颈。本研究提出一种基于强化学习的信号控制算法，能够完整表征与现场信号控制器一致的八相位环栅栏配置。该算法在不同交通需求条件下进行训练与评估，并与当前最优实践的自适应信号控制进行对比。为评估鲁棒性，实验覆盖了多种交通流量和具有不同结构相似度的起讫点需求模式。为提高训练效率，采用分布式异步训练架构，实现多计算节点的并行仿真。案例交叉口结果表明，所提出的强化学习信号控制显著优于优化后的自适应信号控制，各流向平均延误降低11%-32%。在单一OD模式上训练的模型能良好泛化至相似的未知需求模式，但在差异显著的需求条件下性能下降；而在多样化OD模式上训练的模型则表现出强鲁棒性，即使在高度不同的未知需求场景下仍持续优于自适应信号控制。
Summary / 总结
This study addresses the need for robust and efficient reinforcement learning (RL) models for adaptive traffic signal control, motivated by challenges in deployment such as simplified signal structures, untested robustness under varying traffic, and slow training. The method develops an RL algorithm that models a full eight-phase ring-barrier signal configuration and employs a distributed asynchronous training architecture for efficiency, evaluating it against actuated signal control (ASC) under diverse traffic volumes and origin-destination patterns. Experimental results from a case study intersection show the RL control reduces average delay by 11-32% compared to ASC, with models trained on diverse demand patterns demonstrating strong robustness to unseen scenarios, while those trained on single patterns degrade under dissimilar conditions.
本研究针对强化学习在自适应交通信号控制中部署的挑战，如信号结构简化、多变交通下的鲁棒性不足及训练效率低，旨在开发鲁棒高效的模型。方法上，提出了一个能模拟完整八相位环栅栏信号配置的强化学习算法，并采用分布式异步训练架构提升效率，在不同交通量和起讫点需求模式下与感应信号控制进行对比评估。案例交叉口实验结果表明，该强化学习控制将平均延误降低了11-32%，且基于多样化需求模式训练的模型在未见场景中表现出强鲁棒性，而基于单一模式训练的模型在差异较大条件下性能下降。
Probe-then-Plan: Environment-Aware Planning for Industrial E-commerce Search
Authors: Mengxiang Chen, Zhouwei Zhai, Jin Li
First: 2026-03-16T13:28:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T13:28:01+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Modern e-commerce search is evolving to resolve complex user intents. While Large Language Models (LLMs) offer strong reasoning, existing LLM-based paradigms face a fundamental blindness-latency dilemma: query rewriting is agnostic to retrieval capabilities and real-time inventory, yielding invalid plans; conversely, deep search agents rely on iterative tool calls and reflection, incurring seconds of latency incompatible with industrial sub-second budgets. To resolve this conflict, we propose Environment-Aware Search Planning (EASP), reformulating search planning as a dynamic reasoning process grounded in environmental reality. EASP introduces a Probe-then-Plan mechanism: a lightweight Retrieval Probe exposes the retrieval snapshot, enabling the Planner to diagnose execution gaps and generate grounded search plans. The methodology comprises three stages: (1) Offline Data Synthesis: A Teacher Agent synthesizes diverse, execution-validated plans by diagnosing the probed environment. (2) Planner Training and Alignment: The Planner is initialized via Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) to internalize diagnostic capabilities, then aligned with business outcomes (conversion rate) via Reinforcement Learning (RL). (3) Adaptive Online Serving: A complexity-aware routing mechanism selectively activates planning for complex queries, ensuring optimal resource allocation. Extensive offline evaluations and online A/B testing on JD.com demonstrate that EASP significantly improves relevant recall and achieves substantial lifts in UCVR and GMV. EASP has been successfully deployed in JD.com's AI-Search system.
中文标题/摘要
标题：探后规划：面向工业电商搜索的环境感知规划
现代电商搜索正朝着解决复杂用户意图的方向演进。尽管大语言模型具备强大的推理能力，但现有基于大语言模型的范式面临根本性的盲区-延迟困境：查询改写无视检索能力与实时库存，导致生成无效计划；反之，深度搜索代理依赖迭代式工具调用与反思，产生数秒延迟，无法满足工业级亚秒级响应要求。为解决这一矛盾，本文提出环境感知搜索规划，将搜索规划重构为基于环境实况的动态推理过程。该方法引入“探后规划”机制：轻量级检索探针获取检索快照，使规划器能够诊断执行差距并生成基于实况的搜索计划。方法论包含三个阶段：（1）离线数据合成：教师代理通过诊断探测环境，合成多样化且经执行验证的计划。（2）规划器训练与对齐：通过监督微调初始化规划器以内化诊断能力，再通过强化学习将其与业务指标（转化率）对齐。（3）自适应在线服务：基于复杂度的路由机制选择性激活复杂查询的规划，确保资源最优分配。在京东进行的广泛离线评估与在线A/B测试表明，该方法显著提升相关召回率，并在UCVR和GMV上实现大幅增长，目前已成功部署于京东AI搜索系统。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the dilemma in industrial e-commerce search where existing LLM-based methods either produce invalid plans due to ignorance of real-time inventory and retrieval capabilities or incur high latency from iterative tool calls, conflicting with sub-second response requirements. It proposes Environment-Aware Search Planning (EASP), which employs a Probe-then-Plan mechanism: a lightweight Retrieval Probe first captures a retrieval snapshot, allowing a Planner to diagnose gaps and generate grounded search plans through a process involving offline data synthesis by a Teacher Agent, supervised fine-tuning and reinforcement learning alignment for the Planner, and adaptive online serving with complexity-aware routing. Experimental results from offline evaluations and online A/B testing on JD.com show that EASP significantly enhances relevant recall and achieves substantial improvements in user conversion rate and gross merchandise volume, leading to its successful deployment.
本文针对工业电商搜索中的困境提出解决方案：现有基于大语言模型的方法因忽略实时库存和检索能力而产生无效计划，或依赖迭代工具调用导致高延迟，无法满足亚秒级响应需求。为此，论文提出了环境感知搜索规划（EASP），采用“探测后规划”机制：首先通过轻量级检索探测获取检索快照，使规划器能够诊断执行差距并生成基于环境的搜索计划，该方法包括离线数据合成、规划器的监督微调与强化学习对齐，以及自适应在线服务与复杂度感知路由。在京东的离线评估和在线A/B测试中，EASP显著提升了相关召回率，并在用户转化率和商品交易总额上取得大幅增长，已成功部署于京东的AI搜索系统。
Towards Foundation Models for Consensus Rank Aggregation
Authors: Yijun Jin, Simon Klüttermann, Chiara Balestra, Emmanuel Müller
First: 2026-03-16T12:55:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T12:55:54+00:00
Comments: 16 pages, 5 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Aggregating a consensus ranking from multiple input rankings is a fundamental problem with applications in recommendation systems, search engines, job recruitment, and elections. Despite decades of research in consensus ranking aggregation, minimizing the Kemeny distance remains computationally intractable. Specifically, determining an optimal aggregation of rankings with respect to the Kemeny distance is an NP-hard problem, limiting its practical application to relatively small-scale instances. We propose the Kemeny Transformer, a novel Transformer-based algorithm trained via reinforcement learning to efficiently approximate the Kemeny optimal ranking. Experimental results demonstrate that our model outperforms classical majority-heuristic and Markov-chain approaches, achieving substantially faster inference than integer linear programming solvers. Our approach thus offers a practical, scalable alternative for real-world ranking-aggregation tasks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向共识排序聚合的基础模型研究
从多个输入排序中聚合出共识排序是推荐系统、搜索引擎、招聘选举等领域的基础性问题。尽管共识排序聚合研究已开展数十年，最小化Kemeny距离的计算复杂度问题仍未解决。具体而言，基于Kemeny距离的最优排序聚合属于NP难问题，导致其实际应用仅限于小规模场景。本文提出Kemeny Transformer——一种基于Transformer架构、通过强化学习训练的新型算法，可高效逼近Kemeny最优排序。实验表明，该模型在经典多数启发式和马尔可夫链方法上表现更优，且推理速度显著快于整数线性规划求解器。该方法为现实世界的排序聚合任务提供了可扩展的实用解决方案。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the long-standing computational challenge of aggregating consensus rankings, a task critical to recommendation systems and elections, where minimizing the Kemeny distance is NP-hard and thus impractical for large-scale use. To overcome this, the authors introduce the Kemeny Transformer, a method that leverages a Transformer architecture trained with reinforcement learning to efficiently approximate optimal Kemeny rankings. Experiments show that this model surpasses traditional heuristic and Markov-chain methods in performance and delivers significantly faster inference compared to integer linear programming solvers, providing a scalable solution for real-world ranking aggregation.
本文针对共识排名聚合这一长期存在的计算难题展开研究，该任务在推荐系统和选举等领域至关重要，但最小化Kemeny距离是NP难问题，限制了其大规模实际应用。为此，作者提出了Kemeny Transformer方法，该方法利用基于Transformer的架构，通过强化学习进行训练，以高效逼近最优Kemeny排名。实验结果表明，该模型在性能上超越了传统的多数启发式和马尔可夫链方法，并且相比整数线性规划求解器实现了显著更快的推理速度，为实际排名聚合任务提供了一种可扩展的解决方案。
Admission Control of Quasi-Reversible Queueing Systems: Optimization and Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Céline Comte, Pascal Moyal
First: 2025-05-22T08:05:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T12:48:36+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In this paper, we introduce a versatile scheme for optimizing the arrival rates of quasi-reversible queueing systems. We first propose an alternative definition of quasi-reversibility that encompasses reversibility and highlights the importance of the definition of customer classes. Then we introduce balanced arrival control policies, which generalize the notion of balanced arrival rates introduced in the context of Whittle networks, to the much broader class of quasi-reversible queueing systems. We prove that supplementing a quasi-reversible queueing system with a balanced arrival-control policy preserves the quasi-reversibility, and we specify the form of the stationary measures. We revisit two canonical examples of quasi-reversible queueing systems, Whittle networks and order-independent queues. Lastly, we focus on the problem of admission control and leverage our results in the frameworks of optimization and reinforcement learning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：准可逆排队系统的准入控制：优化与强化学习
本文提出了一种优化准可逆排队系统到达率的通用框架。首先提出一种涵盖可逆性并强调顾客类别定义重要性的准可逆性替代定义。随后引入平衡到达控制策略，将Whittle网络中提出的平衡到达率概念推广至更广泛的准可逆排队系统类别。我们证明在准可逆排队系统中补充平衡到达控制策略可保持准可逆性，并明确了稳态测度的形式。通过重新审视Whittle网络与顺序无关队列这两个准可逆排队系统的典型范例，最终聚焦于准入控制问题，并将研究成果应用于优化与强化学习框架。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to optimize arrival rates in quasi-reversible queueing systems, this paper proposes a new definition of quasi-reversibility that includes reversibility and emphasizes customer class definitions. The method introduces balanced arrival control policies, extending the concept of balanced arrival rates from Whittle networks to a broader class of quasi-reversible systems, and proves that such policies preserve quasi-reversibility while specifying stationary measures. Experimental results demonstrate the application to canonical examples like Whittle networks and order-independent queues, showing how the framework supports admission control in optimization and reinforcement learning contexts.
本文旨在优化拟可逆排队系统的到达率，提出了一种新的拟可逆性定义，该定义涵盖可逆性并强调顾客类别的重要性。方法上引入了平衡到达控制策略，将Whittle网络中的平衡到达率概念推广到更广泛的拟可逆排队系统，并证明该策略能保持拟可逆性且明确稳态测度形式。实验结果通过重访Whittle网络和顺序无关队列等典型示例，展示了该框架在优化和强化学习场景中如何有效支持准入控制问题。
Iterative Learning Control-Informed Reinforcement Learning for Batch Process Control
Authors: Runze Lin, Ziqi Zhuo, Junghui Chen, Lei Xie, Hongye Su
First: 2026-03-16T12:17:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T12:17:43+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
A significant limitation of Deep Reinforcement Learning (DRL) is the stochastic uncertainty in actions generated during exploration-exploitation, which poses substantial safety risks during both training and deployment. In industrial process control, the lack of formal stability and convergence guarantees further inhibits adoption of DRL methods by practitioners. Conversely, Iterative Learning Control (ILC) represents a well-established autonomous control methodology for repetitive systems, particularly in batch process optimization. ILC achieves desired control performance through iterative refinement of control laws, either between consecutive batches or within individual batches, to compensate for both repetitive and non-repetitive disturbances. This study introduces an Iterative Learning Control-Informed Reinforcement Learning (IL-CIRL) framework for training DRL controllers in dual-layer batch-to-batch and within-batch control architectures for batch processes. The proposed method incorporates Kalman filter-based state estimation within the iterative learning structure to guide DRL agents toward control policies that satisfy operational constraints and ensure stability guarantees. This approach enables the systematic design of DRL controllers for batch processes operating under multiple disturbance conditions.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向间歇过程控制的迭代学习控制启发的强化学习方法
深度强化学习（DRL）的一个显著局限在于探索-利用过程中生成动作的随机不确定性，这在训练和部署阶段均会带来重大安全风险。在工业过程控制中，缺乏形式化的稳定性与收敛性保证进一步阻碍了从业者采用DRL方法。相比之下，迭代学习控制（ILC）是一种针对重复系统的成熟自主控制方法，尤其适用于间歇过程优化。ILC通过在连续批次间或单个批次内迭代优化控制律，以补偿重复性与非重复性扰动，从而实现期望的控制性能。本研究提出一种迭代学习控制启发的强化学习（IL-CIRL）框架，用于在间歇过程的双层（批间与批内）控制架构中训练DRL控制器。该方法在迭代学习结构中引入基于卡尔曼滤波的状态估计，以引导DRL智能体学习满足操作约束并确保稳定性保证的控制策略。该框架为在多重扰动条件下运行的间歇过程DRL控制器提供了系统化设计途径。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the safety and stability concerns of Deep Reinforcement Learning (DRL) in industrial batch process control by integrating it with the established methodology of Iterative Learning Control (ILC). The proposed IL-CIRL framework employs a dual-layer control architecture and incorporates Kalman filter-based state estimation within an iterative learning structure to guide DRL agents. Experimental results demonstrate that this approach enables the systematic design of DRL controllers that satisfy operational constraints and ensure stability guarantees under multiple disturbance conditions.
本文针对深度强化学习在工业批次过程控制中的安全性与稳定性问题，将其与成熟的迭代学习控制方法相结合。所提出的IL-CIRL框架采用双层控制架构，并在迭代学习结构中融入基于卡尔曼滤波的状态估计，以引导深度强化学习智能体。实验结果表明，该方法能够系统化地设计出满足操作约束、确保稳定性保证的深度强化学习控制器，以应对多种扰动条件。
Feature-driven reinforcement learning for photovoltaic in continuous intraday trading
Authors: Arega Getaneh Abate, Xiao-Bing Zhang, Xiufeng Liu, Ruyu Liu
First: 2025-10-15T15:19:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T11:29:00+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Sequential intraday electricity trading allows photovoltaic (PV) operators to reduce imbalance settlement costs as forecasts improve throughout the day. Yet deployable trading policies must jointly handle forecast uncertainty, intraday prices, liquidity, and the asymmetric economics of PV imbalance exposure. This paper proposes a feature-driven reinforcement learning (FDRL) framework for intraday PV trading in the Nordic market. Its main methodological contribution is a corrected reward that evaluates performance relative to a no-trade baseline, removing policy-independent noise that can otherwise push reinforcement learning toward inactive policies in high-price regimes. The framework combines this objective with a predominantly linear policy and a closed-form execution surrogate for efficient, interpretable training. In a strict walk-forward evaluation over 2021-2024 across four Nordic bidding zones (DK1, DK2, SE3, SE4), the method delivers statistically significant profit improvements over the spot-only baseline in every zone. Portfolio experiments show that a pooled cross-zone policy can match zone-specific models, while transfer-learning results indicate a two-cluster market structure and effective deployment in new zones with limited local data. The proposed framework offers an interpretable and computationally practical way to reduce imbalance costs, while the transfer results provide guidance for scaling strategies across bidding zones with different market designs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向光伏连续日内交易的特征驱动强化学习
时序性日内电力交易允许光伏运营商在日内预测精度提升时降低不平衡结算成本。然而，可部署的交易策略必须同时处理预测不确定性、日内价格、流动性以及光伏不平衡风险的非对称经济性。本文提出了一种适用于北欧市场的日内光伏交易特征驱动强化学习框架。其主要方法论贡献是引入一种修正奖励函数，该函数以无交易基准为参照评估策略表现，消除了与策略无关的噪声——这类噪声在高价格区间可能迫使强化学习策略趋于无效。该框架将此目标与主导线性策略及闭式执行代理相结合，实现高效且可解释的训练。在2021-2024年间对北欧四个竞价区（DK1、DK2、SE3、SE4）的严格滚动前进评估表明，该方法在所有区域均实现了较纯现货基准的统计显著利润提升。组合实验显示，跨区域聚合策略可达到与区域专用模型相当的效果，而迁移学习结果揭示了市场的双簇结构，并证明在本地数据有限的新区域仍能有效部署。所提框架为降低不平衡成本提供了可解释且计算可行的路径，迁移结果则为在不同市场设计的竞价区间扩展策略提供了实践指导。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge for photovoltaic (PV) operators to reduce imbalance costs through sequential intraday electricity trading, which must account for forecast uncertainty, price dynamics, liquidity, and asymmetric economic exposure. The proposed method is a feature-driven reinforcement learning (FDRL) framework that introduces a corrected reward function to evaluate performance against a no-trade baseline, mitigating noise that could lead to inactive policies, and combines it with a largely linear policy and a closed-form execution surrogate for efficient and interpretable training. In a rigorous walk-forward evaluation from 2021 to 2024 across four Nordic bidding zones, the approach achieved statistically significant profit improvements over a spot-only baseline in all zones, with portfolio experiments demonstrating that a pooled cross-zone policy performs comparably to zone-specific models and transfer learning revealing a two-cluster market structure enabling effective deployment in new zones with limited data.
本文针对光伏运营商在连续日内电力交易中降低不平衡成本的挑战，该交易需共同处理预测不确定性、日内价格、流动性以及光伏不平衡暴露的非对称经济性。提出的方法是一种特征驱动的强化学习框架，其核心是引入一个相对于无交易基准的校正奖励函数，以消除可能驱使策略在价格高位时趋于无效的独立噪声，并结合了以线性为主的策略和闭式执行代理，以实现高效且可解释的训练。在2021年至2024年对北欧四个竞价区的严格向前走评估中，该方法在所有区域均实现了相对于仅现货基准的统计显著利润提升；组合实验表明，跨区池化策略可与特定区域模型相媲美，而迁移学习结果则揭示了市场存在两簇结构，并能在本地数据有限的新区域有效部署。
Safe Flow Q-Learning: Offline Safe Reinforcement Learning with Reachability-Based Flow Policies
Authors: Mumuksh Tayal, Manan Tayal, Ravi Prakash
First: 2026-03-16T11:28:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T11:28:47+00:00
Comments: 24 pages, 6 figures, 4 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Offline safe reinforcement learning (RL) seeks reward-maximizing policies from static datasets under strict safety constraints. Existing methods often rely on soft expected-cost objectives or iterative generative inference, which can be insufficient for safety-critical real-time control. We propose Safe Flow Q-Learning (SafeFQL), which extends FQL to safe offline RL by combining a Hamilton--Jacobi reachability-inspired safety value function with an efficient one-step flow policy. SafeFQL learns the safety value via a self-consistency Bellman recursion, trains a flow policy by behavioral cloning, and distills it into a one-step actor for reward-maximizing safe action selection without rejection sampling at deployment. To account for finite-data approximation error in the learned safety boundary, we add a conformal prediction calibration step that adjusts the safety threshold and provides finite-sample probabilistic safety coverage. Empirically, SafeFQL trades modestly higher offline training cost for substantially lower inference latency than diffusion-style safe generative baselines, which is advantageous for real-time safety-critical deployment. Across boat navigation, and Safety Gymnasium MuJoCo tasks, SafeFQL matches or exceeds prior offline safe RL performance while substantially reducing constraint violations.
中文标题/摘要
标题：安全流Q学习：基于可达性流策略的离线安全强化学习
离线安全强化学习旨在从静态数据集中学习满足严格安全约束的奖励最大化策略。现有方法常依赖软期望成本目标或迭代生成推断，对安全关键实时控制存在不足。本文提出安全流Q学习（SafeFQL），通过将汉密尔顿-雅可比可达性启发的安全值函数与高效单步流策略结合，将FQL扩展至安全离线强化学习。SafeFQL通过自洽贝尔曼递归学习安全值函数，通过行为克隆训练流策略，并将其蒸馏为单步执行器，在部署时无需拒绝采样即可实现奖励最大化的安全动作选择。针对学习安全边界的有限数据近似误差，我们增加了共形预测校准步骤以调整安全阈值并提供有限样本概率安全覆盖。实验表明，与扩散式安全生成基线相比，SafeFQL以适度增加的离线训练成本显著降低推理延迟，这对实时安全关键部署具有优势。在船舶导航和安全体育馆MuJoCo任务中，SafeFQL达到或超越现有离线安全强化学习性能，同时大幅减少约束违反。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of offline safe reinforcement learning, where policies must maximize reward from static datasets while strictly adhering to safety constraints, a critical need for real-time control applications where existing methods relying on soft cost objectives or iterative inference can be inadequate. The proposed method, Safe Flow Q-Learning (SafeFQL), extends Flow Q-Learning by integrating a Hamilton-Jacobi reachability-inspired safety value function with an efficient one-step flow policy; it learns the safety value via a self-consistency Bellman recursion, trains the flow policy through behavioral cloning, and distills it into a one-step actor for safe action selection without deployment-time rejection sampling, supplemented by a conformal prediction step to adjust safety thresholds and provide probabilistic safety coverage against finite-data errors. Experimental results on boat navigation and Safety Gymnasium MuJoCo tasks demonstrate that SafeFQL matches or surpasses prior offline safe RL performance with significantly fewer constraint violations, trading moderately higher offline training costs for substantially lower inference latency compared to diffusion-based baselines, making it advantageous for safety-critical real-time deployment.
本文针对离线安全强化学习中的挑战，即从静态数据集中学习策略时需在严格安全约束下最大化奖励，这对实时控制应用至关重要，而现有基于软成本目标或迭代推理的方法往往不足。所提出的方法Safe Flow Q-Learning（SafeFQL）扩展了流Q学习，通过将汉密尔顿-雅可比可达性启发的安全值函数与高效的一步流策略相结合；它通过自洽贝尔曼递归学习安全值，通过行为克隆训练流策略，并将其蒸馏为一步执行器以实现无需部署时拒绝采样的安全动作选择，并辅以共形预测步骤来调整安全阈值并提供针对有限数据误差的概率安全覆盖。在船舶导航和安全健身房MuJoCo任务上的实验结果表明，SafeFQL匹配或超越了先前离线安全强化学习的性能，同时显著减少了约束违反，尽管离线训练成本略有增加，但相比基于扩散的基线方法大幅降低了推理延迟，这使其在安全关键的实时部署中具有优势。
Sampling-guided exploration of active feature selection policies
Authors: Gabriel Bernardino, Anders Jonsson, Patrick Clarysse, Nicolas Duchateau
First: 2026-03-16T11:07:00+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T11:07:00+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Determining the most appropriate features for machine learning predictive models is challenging regarding performance and feature acquisition costs. In particular, global feature choice is limited given that some features will only benefit a subset of instances. In previous work, we proposed a reinforcement learning approach to sequentially recommend which modality to acquire next to reach the best information/cost ratio, based on the instance-specific information already acquired. We formulated the problem as a Markov Decision Process where the state's dimensionality changes during the episode, avoiding data imputation, contrary to existing works. However, this only allowed processing a small number of features, as all possible combinations of features were considered. Here, we address these limitations with two contributions: 1) we expand our framework to larger datasets with a heuristic-based strategy that focuses on the most promising feature combinations, and 2) we introduce a post-fit regularisation strategy that reduces the number of different feature combinations, leading to compact sequences of decisions. We tested our method on four binary classification datasets (one involving high-dimensional variables), the largest of which had 56 features and 4500 samples. We obtained better performance than state-of-the-art methods, both in terms of accuracy and policy complexity.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于采样的主动特征选择策略探索
为机器学习预测模型确定最合适的特征在性能和特征获取成本方面均具挑战性。特别是全局特征选择受限，因为某些特征仅对部分实例有益。先前工作中，我们提出一种强化学习方法，基于已获取的实例特定信息，按顺序推荐下一步应获取哪种模态以达到最佳信息/成本比。我们将该问题建模为马尔可夫决策过程，其状态维度在过程中动态变化，避免了数据插补，与现有方法不同。然而，由于需考虑所有可能的特征组合，该方法仅能处理少量特征。本文通过两项改进突破这些限制：1）采用启发式策略扩展框架至更大数据集，聚焦于最有潜力的特征组合；2）引入后拟合正则化策略，减少不同特征组合的数量，从而生成紧凑的决策序列。我们在四个二元分类数据集（其中一个包含高维变量）上测试了方法，最大数据集含56个特征和4500个样本。实验表明，该方法在准确率和策略复杂度方面均优于现有先进方法。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of active feature selection in machine learning, where the goal is to sequentially acquire features for each instance to optimize predictive performance while minimizing acquisition costs, moving beyond static global feature sets. The method extends a prior reinforcement learning framework formulated as a Markov Decision Process with variable state dimensionality by introducing a heuristic to focus on promising feature combinations for scalability and a post-fit regularization strategy to simplify decision policies. Experimental results on four binary classification datasets, including one high-dimensional set with up to 56 features and 4500 samples, demonstrate that the approach outperforms state-of-the-art methods in both accuracy and policy complexity.
本文针对机器学习中的主动特征选择问题，旨在通过为每个实例顺序获取特征来优化预测性能并最小化获取成本，从而超越静态的全局特征选择方法。该方法扩展了先前基于强化学习的框架，该框架将问题建模为状态维度可变的马尔可夫决策过程，通过引入启发式策略来聚焦有潜力的特征组合以提高可扩展性，并采用后拟合正则化策略来简化决策序列。在四个二分类数据集（包括一个具有56个特征和4500个样本的高维数据集）上的实验结果表明，该方法在准确性和策略复杂性方面均优于现有先进方法。
PrototypeNAS: Rapid Design of Deep Neural Networks for Microcontroller Units
Authors: Mark Deutel, Simon Geis, Axel Plinge
First: 2026-03-16T10:59:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T10:59:19+00:00
Comments: 16 pages, 6 figures, 4 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Enabling efficient deep neural network (DNN) inference on edge devices with different hardware constraints is a challenging task that typically requires DNN architectures to be specialized for each device separately. To avoid the huge manual effort, one can use neural architecture search (NAS). However, many existing NAS methods are resource-intensive and time-consuming because they require the training of many different DNNs from scratch. Furthermore, they do not take the resource constraints of the target system into account. To address these shortcomings, we propose PrototypeNAS, a zero-shot NAS method to accelerate and automate the selection, compression, and specialization of DNNs to different target microcontroller units (MCUs). We propose a novel three-step search method that decouples DNN design and specialization from DNN training for a given target platform. First, we present a novel search space that not only cuts out smaller DNNs from a single large architecture, but instead combines the structural optimization of multiple architecture types, as well as optimization of their pruning and quantization configurations. Second, we explore the use of an ensemble of zero-shot proxies during optimization instead of a single one. Third, we propose the use of Hypervolume subset selection to distill DNN architectures from the Pareto front of the multi-objective optimization that represent the most meaningful tradeoffs between accuracy and FLOPs. We evaluate the effectiveness of PrototypeNAS on 12 different datasets in three different tasks: image classification, time series classification, and object detection. Our results demonstrate that PrototypeNAS is able to identify DNN models within minutes that are small enough to be deployed on off-the-shelf MCUs and still achieve accuracies comparable to the performance of large DNN models.
中文标题/摘要
标题：PrototypeNAS：面向微控制器单元的深度神经网络快速设计方法
在具有不同硬件约束的边缘设备上实现高效的深度神经网络推理是一项挑战性任务，通常需要为每个设备单独定制DNN架构。为避免巨大的人工成本，可采用神经架构搜索技术。然而，现有许多NAS方法因需从头训练大量不同DNN而资源密集且耗时，且未考虑目标系统的资源约束。为此，我们提出PrototypeNAS——一种零样本NAS方法，用于加速和自动化DNN的选择、压缩及针对不同微控制器的定制化。我们提出新颖的三步搜索法，将DNN设计与定制从目标平台的训练过程中解耦：首先构建新型搜索空间，不仅能从单一大型架构中裁剪小型DNN，还能融合多种架构类型的结构优化及其剪枝与量化配置优化；其次在优化过程中采用零样本代理集成而非单一代理；最后提出使用超体积子集选择法，从多目标优化的帕累托前沿中提炼出最能体现精度与计算量权衡的DNN架构。我们在图像分类、时间序列分类和目标检测三类任务的12个数据集上评估PrototypeNAS，结果表明该方法能在数分钟内识别出足够小、可部署于商用MCU且精度媲美大型DNN的模型。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for PrototypeNAS is to automate the design of efficient deep neural networks for microcontroller units (MCUs) without the resource-intensive training of many models from scratch, as typical neural architecture search (NAS) methods do. The method introduces a zero-shot NAS approach with a three-step process: it defines a novel search space for structural optimization, pruning, and quantization; employs an ensemble of zero-shot proxies for evaluation; and uses Hypervolume subset selection to extract optimal architectures from a Pareto front balancing accuracy and computational cost (FLOPs). Experimental results across 12 datasets for image classification, time-series classification, and object detection show that PrototypeNAS can quickly identify compact DNN models deployable on off-the-shelf MCUs while maintaining accuracy comparable to larger models.
PrototypeNAS 的动机是为微控制器单元（MCU）自动设计高效的深度神经网络，避免传统神经架构搜索（NAS）方法需要从头训练大量模型的高资源消耗问题。该方法提出了一种零样本NAS，采用三步流程：定义了一个结合结构优化、剪枝和量化的新型搜索空间；使用零样本代理集成进行评估；并应用超体积子集选择从平衡精度与计算成本（FLOPs）的帕累托前沿中提取最优架构。在图像分类、时间序列分类和目标检测的12个数据集上的实验结果表明，PrototypeNAS 能快速识别出可在现成MCU上部署的紧凑DNN模型，同时保持与大型模型相当的精度。
Delphos: A reinforcement learning framework for assisting discrete choice model specification
Authors: Gabriel Nova, Stephane Hess, Sander van Cranenburgh
First: 2025-06-06T15:40:16+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T10:58:11+00:00
Comments: 13 pages, 7 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We introduce Delphos, a deep reinforcement learning framework for assisting the discrete choice model specification process. Delphos aims to support the modeller by providing automated, data-driven suggestions for utility specifications, thereby reducing the effort required to develop and refine utility functions. Delphos conceptualises model specification as a sequential decision-making problem, inspired by the way human choice modellers iteratively construct models through a series of reasoned specification decisions. In this setting, an agent learns to specify high-performing candidate models by choosing a sequence of modelling actions, such as selecting variables, accommodating both generic and alternative-specific taste parameters, applying non-linear transformations, and including interactions with covariates, while interacting with a modelling environment that estimates each candidate and returns a reward signal. Specifically, Delphos uses a Deep Q-Network that receives delayed rewards based on modelling outcomes (e.g., log-likelihood) and behavioural expectations (e.g., parameter signs), and distributes this signal across the sequence of actions to learn which modelling decisions lead to well-performing candidates. We evaluate Delphos on both simulated and empirical datasets using multiple reward settings. In simulated cases, learning curves, Q-value patterns, and performance metrics show that the agent learns to adaptively explore strategies to propose well-performing models across search spaces, while covering only a small fraction of the feasible modelling space. We further apply the framework to two empirical datasets to demonstrate its practical use. These experiments illustrate the ability of Delphos to generate competitive, behaviourally plausible models and highlight the potential of this adaptive, learning-based framework to assist the model specification process.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Delphos：一种辅助离散选择模型设定的强化学习框架
本文介绍Delphos——一个用于辅助离散选择模型设定过程的深度强化学习框架。该框架旨在通过提供数据驱动的效用函数自动设定建议，降低构建与优化效用函数所需的工作量。Delphos将模型设定概念化为序列决策问题，其设计灵感来源于人类建模者通过一系列理性设定决策迭代构建模型的方式。在此框架中，智能体通过与建模环境交互（该环境负责评估每个候选模型并返回奖励信号），学习通过选择建模动作序列（如变量选择、通用/备选特定偏好参数设置、非线性变换应用、协变量交互项引入等）来设定高性能候选模型。具体而言，Delphos采用深度Q网络接收基于建模结果（如对数似然值）和行为预期（如参数符号）的延迟奖励，并将该信号分配到动作序列中以学习哪些建模决策能产生性能优异的候选模型。我们通过模拟与实证数据集在多种奖励设置下评估Delphos：模拟案例中的学习曲线、Q值模式和性能指标表明，智能体能够学习自适应探索策略，在仅覆盖可行建模空间极小部分的情况下，提出跨搜索空间的高性能模型；两个实证数据集的应用进一步展示了框架的实际效用。实验证明了Delphos生成具有竞争力且行为合理的模型的能力，凸显了这种基于自适应学习的框架在辅助模型设定过程中的潜力。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces Delphos, a reinforcement learning framework designed to automate and assist the specification of discrete choice models, motivated by the need to reduce the manual effort in developing utility functions. The method formulates model specification as a sequential decision-making problem, employing a Deep Q-Network agent that selects modeling actions—such as variable selection and parameter transformations—based on rewards derived from outcomes like log-likelihood and behavioral plausibility. Experimental results on simulated and empirical datasets show that the agent efficiently explores the search space to propose high-performing, behaviorally plausible models while covering only a small fraction of possible specifications, demonstrating its practical utility in automating model refinement.

Affordable Precision Agriculture: A Deployment-Oriented Review of Low-Cost, Low-Power Edge AI and TinyML for Resource-Constrained Farming Systems
Authors: Riya Samanta, Bidyut Saha
First: 2026-03-16T10:38:31+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T10:38:31+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Precision agriculture increasingly integrates artificial intelligence to enhance crop monitoring, irrigation management, and resource efficiency. Nevertheless, the vast majority of the current systems are still mostly cloud-based and require reliable connectivity, which hampers the adoption to smaller scale, smallholder farming and underdeveloped country systems. Using recent literature reviews, ranging from 2023 to 2026, this review covers deployments of Edge AI, focused on the evolution and acceptance of Tiny Machine Learning, in low-cost and low-powered agriculture. A hardware-targeted deployment-oriented study has shown pronounced variation in architecture with microcontroller-class platforms i.e. ESP32, STM32, ATMega dominating the inference options, in parallel with single-board computers and UAV-assisted solutions. Quantitative synthesis shows quantization is the dominant optimization strategy; the approach in many works identified: around 50% of such works are quantized, while structured pruning, multi-objective compression and hardware aware neural architecture search are relatively under-researched. Also, resource profiling practices are not uniform: while model size is occasionally reported, explicit flash, RAM, MAC, latency and millijoule level energy metrics are not well documented, hampering reproducibility and cross-system comparison. Moreoever, to bridge the gap between research prototypes and deployment-ready systems, the review also presents a literature-informed deployment perspective in the form of a privacy-preserving layered Edge AI architecture for agriculture, synthesizing the key system-level design insights emerging from the surveyed works. Overall, the findings demonstrate a clear architectural shift toward localized inference with centralized training asymmetry.
中文标题/摘要
标题：经济型精准农业：面向资源受限农业系统的低成本、低功耗边缘AI与微型机器学习部署综述
精准农业日益融合人工智能技术以提升作物监测、灌溉管理和资源利用效率。然而，当前绝大多数系统仍主要基于云端部署并依赖稳定网络连接，这阻碍了其在小规模农户及欠发达地区农业系统的推广应用。本文基于2023至2026年的近期文献，系统综述了边缘AI在低成本、低功耗农业场景中的部署实践，重点关注微型机器学习的技术演进与应用现状。一项面向硬件部署的研究显示，系统架构呈现显著差异：微控制器级平台（如ESP32、STM32、ATMega）在推理方案中占据主导地位，同时单板计算机与无人机辅助解决方案并行发展。量化分析表明，模型量化是主流的优化策略——约50%的研究采用该技术，而结构化剪枝、多目标压缩及硬件感知的神经架构搜索等领域研究相对不足。资源评估实践亦未标准化：模型尺寸偶有报道，但闪存占用、内存消耗、乘加运算量、推理延迟及毫焦级能耗等关键指标普遍缺失，制约了研究的可复现性与跨系统比较。为弥合研究原型与可部署系统之间的差距，本文进一步提出一种基于文献的隐私保护分层边缘AI农业架构，整合了现有研究中的关键系统级设计洞见。总体而言，研究发现农业AI系统正朝着'本地化推理-集中化训练'的非对称架构范式清晰转型。
Summary / 总结
This review is motivated by the need to adapt precision agriculture's AI capabilities for resource-constrained, small-scale farming systems where cloud dependency and connectivity are barriers. The method involves a deployment-oriented analysis of recent literature (2023-2026) on low-cost Edge AI and TinyML, evaluating hardware platforms, model optimization techniques like quantization, and system architectures. The main experimental results highlight a dominant use of microcontroller platforms like ESP32 for inference, with quantization being the primary optimization strategy in about 50% of studied works, while noting a lack of standardized resource profiling and under-exploration of techniques like pruning. The review culminates in proposing a privacy-preserving layered Edge AI architecture to bridge the gap between research and practical deployment, illustrating a broader shift towards localized, asymmetric AI systems in agriculture.
本综述的动机在于，需要使精准农业的人工智能能力适应资源受限的小规模农业系统，因为这些系统中云依赖和网络连接是主要障碍。其方法是对近期文献（2023-2026年）进行以部署为导向的分析，评估低成本边缘AI和微型机器学习，涵盖硬件平台、量化等模型优化技术以及系统架构。主要实验结果表明，ESP32等微控制器平台在推理中占主导地位，量化是约50%研究中的主要优化策略，同时指出资源分析缺乏标准化，且剪枝等技术探索不足。该综述最终提出了一个隐私保护的层次化边缘AI架构，以弥合研究与实际部署之间的差距，阐明了农业领域向本地化、不对称AI系统转变的明显趋势。
Interference-Aware K-Step Reachable Communication in Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Ziyu Cheng, Jinsheng Ren, Zhouxian Jiang, Chenzhihang Li, Rongye Shi, Bin Liang, Jun Yang
First: 2026-03-16T10:07:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T10:07:33+00:00
Comments: multi-agent reinforcement learning, communication
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Effective communication is pivotal for addressing complex collaborative tasks in multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL). Yet, limited communication bandwidth and dynamic, intricate environmental topologies present significant challenges in identifying high-value communication partners. Agents must consequently select collaborators under uncertainty, lacking a priori knowledge of which partners can deliver task-critical information. To this end, we propose Interference-Aware K-Step Reachable Communication (IA-KRC), a novel framework that enhances cooperation via two core components: (1) a K-Step reachability protocol that confines message passing to physically accessible neighbors, and (2) an interference-prediction module that optimizes partner choice by minimizing interference while maximizing utility. Compared to existing methods, IA-KRC enables substantially more persistent and efficient cooperation despite environmental interference. Comprehensive evaluations confirm that IA-KRC achieves superior performance compared to state-of-the-art baselines, while demonstrating enhanced robustness and scalability in complex topological and highly dynamic multi-agent scenarios.
中文标题/摘要
标题：多智能体强化学习中的干扰感知K步可达通信
在多智能体强化学习（MARL）中，有效通信对解决复杂协作任务至关重要。然而，有限的通信带宽和动态复杂的环境拓扑给识别高价值通信伙伴带来显著挑战。智能体需在不确定性下选择合作者，且缺乏对哪些伙伴能提供任务关键信息的先验知识。为此，我们提出干扰感知K步可达通信（IA-KRC）框架，通过两个核心组件增强协作：（1）K步可达协议，将消息传递限制在物理可访问的邻居范围内；（2）干扰预测模块，通过最小化干扰同时最大化效用优化伙伴选择。与现有方法相比，IA-KRC能在环境干扰下实现更持久高效的协作。综合评估表明，IA-KRC在复杂拓扑和高动态多智能体场景中，相比前沿基线方法具有更优性能，同时展现出更强的鲁棒性和可扩展性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenges of limited bandwidth and dynamic topologies in multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL), which hinder the identification of high-value communication partners, this paper proposes the Interference-Aware K-Step Reachable Communication (IA-KRC) framework. The method introduces a K-step reachability protocol to restrict messaging to physically accessible neighbors and an interference-prediction module to optimize partner selection by balancing utility maximization with interference minimization. Experimental results demonstrate that IA-KRC achieves superior performance, robustness, and scalability over state-of-the-art baselines in complex, dynamic multi-agent scenarios, enabling more persistent and efficient cooperation.
本文针对多智能体强化学习中因带宽有限和拓扑动态变化导致难以识别高价值通信伙伴的挑战，提出了干扰感知K步可达通信（IA-KRC）框架。该方法的核心包括一个将消息传递限制在物理可达邻居的K步可达协议，以及一个通过最小化干扰、最大化效用来优化伙伴选择的干扰预测模块。实验结果表明，在复杂动态的多智能体场景中，IA-KRC相比现有先进基线方法实现了更优的性能、鲁棒性和可扩展性，促进了更持久高效的合作。
Shorten After You're Right: Lazy Length Penalties for Reasoning RL
Authors: Danlong Yuan, Tian Xie, Shaohan Huang, Zhuocheng Gong, Huishuai Zhang, Chong Luo, Furu Wei, Dongyan Zhao
First: 2025-05-18T07:46:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T10:03:58+00:00
Comments: Under review
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large reasoning models, such as OpenAI o1 or DeepSeek R1, have demonstrated remarkable performance on reasoning tasks but often incur a long reasoning path with significant memory and time costs. Existing methods primarily aim to shorten reasoning paths by introducing additional training data and stages. In this paper, we propose three critical reward designs integrated directly into the reinforcement learning process of large reasoning models, which reduce the response length without extra training stages. Experiments on four settings show that our method significantly decreases response length while maintaining or even improving performance. Specifically, in a logic reasoning setting, we achieve a 40% reduction in response length averaged by steps alongside a 14% gain in performance. For math problems, we reduce response length averaged by steps by 33% while preserving performance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：正确后即缩短：推理强化学习中的惰性长度惩罚机制
大型推理模型（如OpenAI o1或DeepSeek R1）在推理任务中展现出卓越性能，但其冗长的推理路径常伴随高昂的内存与时间开销。现有方法主要通过引入额外训练数据和阶段来缩短推理路径。本文提出三种关键奖励设计，直接集成至大型推理模型的强化学习过程中，无需额外训练阶段即可缩减响应长度。在四种实验场景中，本方法在保持甚至提升性能的同时显著降低响应长度。具体而言，在逻辑推理场景中，我们实现了步骤平均响应长度减少40%，同时性能提升14%；在数学问题场景中，步骤平均响应长度减少33%且性能保持不变。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the inefficiency of large reasoning models, which often produce lengthy reasoning paths that incur high memory and time costs, without requiring additional training stages. The method introduces three critical reward designs integrated directly into the reinforcement learning process to penalize unnecessary reasoning steps and encourage concise outputs. Experimental results across four settings demonstrate that this approach significantly reduces response length while maintaining or improving performance, with a 40% reduction in steps and a 14% performance gain in logic reasoning, and a 33% step reduction while preserving performance on math problems.
本研究旨在解决大型推理模型因生成冗长推理路径而导致高内存和时间成本的问题，且无需额外训练阶段。方法是在强化学习过程中直接集成三种关键奖励设计，以惩罚不必要的推理步骤并鼓励简洁输出。在四个实验设置中的结果表明，该方法在保持或提升性能的同时显著减少了响应长度，在逻辑推理中平均步骤减少40%且性能提升14%，在数学问题上平均步骤减少33%且性能保持不变。
RoboMD: Uncovering Robot Vulnerabilities through Semantic Potential Fields
Authors: Som Sagar, Jiafei Duan, Sreevishakh Vasudevan, Yifan Zhou, Heni Ben Amor, Dieter Fox, Ransalu Senanayake
First: 2024-12-03T20:34:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T09:03:20+00:00
Comments: 26 Pages, 20 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Robot manipulation policies, while central to the promise of physical AI, are highly vulnerable in the presence of external variations in the real world. Diagnosing these vulnerabilities is hindered by two key challenges: (i) the relevant variations to test against are often unknown, and (ii) direct testing in the real world is costly and unsafe. We introduce a framework that tackles both issues by learning a separate deep reinforcement learning (deep RL) policy for vulnerability prediction through virtual runs on a continuous vision-language embedding trained with limited success-failure data. By treating this embedding space, which is rich in semantic and visual variations, as a potential field, the policy learns to move toward vulnerable regions while being repelled from success regions. This vulnerability prediction policy, trained on virtual rollouts, enables scalable and safe vulnerability analysis without expensive physical trials. By querying this policy, our framework builds a probabilistic vulnerability-likelihood map. Experiments across simulation benchmarks and a physical robot arm show that our framework uncovers up to 23% more unique vulnerabilities than state-of-the-art vision-language baselines, revealing subtle vulnerabilities overlooked by heuristic testing. Additionally, we show that fine-tuning the manipulation policy with the vulnerabilities discovered by our framework improves manipulation performance with much less fine-tuning data.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RoboMD：通过语义势场揭示机器人脆弱性
机器人操作策略作为物理AI实现的核心，在现实世界外部变化下极为脆弱。诊断这些脆弱性面临两大挑战：(1) 需测试的相关变化往往未知；(2) 现实世界直接测试成本高且不安全。我们提出一种框架，通过在经有限成败数据训练的连续视觉-语言嵌入空间进行虚拟推演，学习独立的深度强化学习策略以预测脆弱性。该嵌入空间富含语义与视觉变化，将其视为势场后，策略学会向脆弱区域移动并远离成功区域。这种通过虚拟推演训练的脆弱性预测策略，无需昂贵物理试验即可实现可扩展的安全脆弱性分析。通过查询该策略，框架构建出概率化脆弱性似然图。在仿真基准与实体机械臂上的实验表明，本框架比最先进的视觉-语言基线多发现23%的独特脆弱性，能揭示启发式测试忽略的细微漏洞。此外，利用本框架发现的脆弱性对操作策略进行微调，能以更少的微调数据显著提升操作性能。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the need to diagnose vulnerabilities in robot manipulation policies, which are sensitive to real-world variations, but direct testing is costly and unknown variations hinder diagnosis. The method introduces a framework that learns a deep RL policy for vulnerability prediction by performing virtual rollouts on a continuous vision-language embedding, treating the embedding space as a semantic potential field to guide exploration toward vulnerable regions and away from success areas. Experimental results across simulation and a physical robot arm demonstrate that this approach uncovers up to 23% more unique vulnerabilities than vision-language baselines, revealing subtle issues, and fine-tuning with discovered vulnerabilities improves manipulation performance with less data.
本文的动机是诊断机器人操作策略的脆弱性，这些策略对现实世界变化敏感，但直接测试成本高且未知变化阻碍诊断。方法提出一个框架，通过在连续视觉语言嵌入上进行虚拟运行来学习深度强化学习策略进行脆弱性预测，将该嵌入空间视为语义势场以引导探索朝向脆弱区域并远离成功区域。实验结果表明，在仿真和物理机械臂上，该方法比先进的视觉语言基线多发现高达23%的独特脆弱性，揭示了细微问题，并且利用发现的脆弱性进行微调能以更少数据提升操作性能。
Fuz-RL: A Fuzzy-Guided Robust Framework for Safe Reinforcement Learning under Uncertainty
Authors: Xu Wan, Chao Yang, Cheng Yang, Jie Song, Mingyang Sun
First: 2026-02-24T09:50:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T08:28:16+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Safe Reinforcement Learning (RL) is crucial for achieving high performance while ensuring safety in real-world applications. However, the complex interplay of multiple uncertainty sources in real environments poses significant challenges for interpretable risk assessment and robust decision-making. To address these challenges, we propose Fuz-RL, a fuzzy measure-guided robust framework for safe RL. Specifically, our framework develops a novel fuzzy Bellman operator for estimating robust value functions using Choquet integrals. Theoretically, we prove that solving the Fuz-RL problem (in Constrained Markov Decision Process (CMDP) form) is equivalent to solving distributionally robust safe RL problems (in robust CMDP form), effectively avoiding min-max optimization. Empirical analyses on safe-control-gym and safety-gymnasium scenarios demonstrate that Fuz-RL effectively integrates with existing safe RL baselines in a model-free manner, significantly improving both safety and control performance under various types of uncertainties in observation, action, and dynamics.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Fuz-RL：一种模糊引导的鲁棒框架，用于不确定性下的安全强化学习
安全强化学习（RL）对于在现实应用中确保安全的同时实现高性能至关重要。然而，真实环境中多种不确定性源的复杂交互，为可解释的风险评估和鲁棒决策带来了重大挑战。为应对这些挑战，我们提出了Fuz-RL，一种基于模糊测度引导的鲁棒框架，用于安全RL。具体而言，该框架通过Choquet积分构建了一种新颖的模糊贝尔曼算子，用于估计鲁棒值函数。理论上，我们证明求解Fuz-RL问题（以约束马尔可夫决策过程（CMDP）形式）等价于求解分布鲁棒的安全RL问题（以鲁棒CMDP形式），从而有效避免了极小极大优化。在safe-control-gym和safety-gymnasium场景上的实证分析表明，Fuz-RL能以无模型方式有效整合现有安全RL基线方法，在观测、动作和动力学等多种不确定性条件下，显著提升安全性和控制性能。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces Fuz-RL, a fuzzy-guided robust framework for safe reinforcement learning, motivated by the need to handle multiple uncertainty sources in real environments for interpretable risk assessment and robust decision-making. The method develops a novel fuzzy Bellman operator using Choquet integrals to estimate robust value functions, theoretically linking it to distributionally robust safe RL problems and avoiding min-max optimization. Experimental results on safe-control-gym and safety-gymnasium scenarios show that Fuz-RL integrates model-free with existing safe RL baselines, significantly improving both safety and control performance under uncertainties in observation, action, and dynamics.
本文提出了Fuz-RL，一种模糊引导的鲁棒安全强化学习框架，其动机在于解决现实环境中多种不确定性来源带来的可解释风险评估和鲁棒决策挑战。该方法通过使用Choquet积分开发了一种新颖的模糊贝尔曼算子来估计鲁棒值函数，理论上将其与分布鲁棒安全强化学习问题等价，有效避免了最小-最大优化。在safe-control-gym和safety-gymnasium场景上的实验结果表明，Fuz-RL以无模型方式与现有安全强化学习基线有效集成，在观测、动作和动力学等多种不确定性下显著提升了安全性和控制性能。
On the Adversarial Transferability of Generalized "Skip Connections"
Authors: Yisen Wang, Yichuan Mo, Dongxian Wu, Mingjie Li, Xingjun Ma, Zhouchen Lin
Venue: IEEE Transactions on Pattern Analysis and Machine Intelligence, 2026
First: 2024-10-11T16:17:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T07:53:32+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Skip connection is an essential ingredient for modern deep models to be deeper and more powerful. Despite their huge success in normal scenarios (state-of-the-art classification performance on natural examples), we investigate and identify an interesting property of skip connections under adversarial scenarios, namely, the use of skip connections allows easier generation of highly transferable adversarial examples. Specifically, in ResNet-like models (with skip connections), we find that biasing backpropagation to favor gradients from skip connections--while suppressing those from residual modules via a decay factor--allows one to craft adversarial examples with high transferability. Based on this insight, we propose the Skip Gradient Method (SGM). Although starting from ResNet-like models in vision domains, we further extend SGM to more advanced architectures, including Vision Transformers (ViTs), models with varying-length paths, and other domains such as natural language processing. We conduct comprehensive transfer-based attacks against diverse model families, including ResNets, Transformers, Inceptions, Neural Architecture Search-based models, and Large Language Models (LLMs). The results demonstrate that employing SGM can greatly improve the transferability of crafted attacks in almost all cases. Furthermore, we demonstrate that SGM can still be effective under more challenging settings such as ensemble-based attacks, targeted attacks, and against defense equipped models. At last, we provide theoretical explanations and empirical insights on how SGM works. Our findings not only motivate new adversarial research into the architectural characteristics of models but also open up further challenges for secure model architecture design. Our code is available at https://github.com/mo666666/SGM.
中文标题/摘要
标题：论广义“跳跃连接”的对抗迁移性
跳跃连接是现代深度模型实现更深层、更强大性能的关键要素。尽管其在正常场景下（在自然样本上达到最先进的分类性能）取得了巨大成功，本研究探索并揭示了跳跃连接在对抗场景下的一个有趣特性：跳跃连接的使用使得生成高迁移性的对抗样本更为容易。具体而言，在类ResNet模型（含跳跃连接）中，我们发现通过衰减因子抑制残差模块梯度、同时偏置反向传播以强化跳跃连接梯度的方式，能够构造出具有高迁移性的对抗样本。基于这一洞见，我们提出了跳跃梯度方法（SGM）。虽然最初针对视觉领域的类ResNet模型，我们进一步将SGM扩展至更先进的架构，包括视觉Transformer（ViT）、可变路径长度模型以及自然语言处理等其他领域。我们对多种模型族开展了全面的基于迁移的攻击实验，涵盖ResNet、Transformer、Inception、基于神经架构搜索的模型以及大语言模型（LLM）。结果表明，在几乎所有情况下，采用SGM都能显著提升所构造攻击的迁移性。此外，我们验证了SGM在更具挑战性的场景中依然有效，包括基于集成的攻击、定向攻击以及针对具备防御机制的模型。最后，我们从理论解释和实证角度阐明了SGM的作用机理。本研究不仅为模型架构特性的对抗性研究提供了新方向，也为安全模型架构设计提出了进一步挑战。代码已开源：https://github.com/mo666666/SGM。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to understand the security implications of skip connections in deep learning architectures, this paper investigates their role in adversarial transferability. The method introduces the Skip Gradient Method (SGM), which biases backpropagation to prioritize gradients from skip connections over residual modules via a decay factor, thereby crafting more transferable adversarial examples. Experimental results demonstrate that SGM significantly enhances attack transferability across diverse model families, including ResNets, Vision Transformers, and Large Language Models, and remains effective in challenging scenarios like ensemble attacks and against defended models.
本文旨在探究深度学习架构中跳跃连接在对抗性攻击中的安全性影响，发现其有助于生成高迁移性的对抗样本。方法上提出了跳跃梯度方法（SGM），通过在反向传播中偏置跳跃连接的梯度并抑制残差模块的梯度，以生成更具迁移性的对抗样本。实验结果表明，SGM能显著提升攻击在多种模型家族（如ResNet、Vision Transformer和大语言模型）中的迁移性，并在集成攻击、目标攻击及对抗防御模型等挑战性场景中保持有效。
Buffer Matters: Unleashing the Power of Off-Policy Reinforcement Learning in Large Language Model Reasoning
Authors: Xu Wan, Yansheng Wang, Wenqi Huang, Mingyang Sun
First: 2026-02-24T09:35:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T07:07:21+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Traditional on-policy Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) frameworks suffer from experience waste and reward homogeneity, which directly hinders learning efficiency on difficult samples during large language models post-training. In this paper, we introduce Batch Adaptation Policy Optimization (BAPO), an off-policy RLVR framework to improve the data efficiency in large language models post-training. It dynamically selects training batches by re-evaluating historically difficult samples and reusing high-quality ones, while holding a lower bound guarantee for policy improvement. Extensive experiments further demonstrate that BAPO achieves an average 12.5% improvement over GRPO across mathematics, planning, and visual reasoning tasks. Crucially, BAPO successfully resolves 40.7% of problems that base models consistently fail to solve.
中文标题/摘要
标题：缓冲区的重要性：释放离线策略强化学习在大语言模型推理中的潜力
传统的基于可验证奖励的在线策略强化学习框架存在经验浪费和奖励同质化问题，这直接阻碍了大语言模型后训练阶段在困难样本上的学习效率。本文提出批量自适应策略优化，一种离线策略的RLVR框架，旨在提升大语言模型后训练的数据效率。该框架通过重新评估历史困难样本并复用高质量样本，动态选择训练批次，同时为策略改进提供下界保证。大量实验进一步表明，在数学、规划和视觉推理任务上，BAPO相比GRPO平均提升12.5%。关键的是，BAPO成功解决了基础模型持续无法解决的40.7%的问题。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the inefficiencies of on-policy reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) in large language model post-training, which suffers from experience waste and reward homogeneity, this paper introduces Batch Adaptation Policy Optimization (BAPO), an off-policy RLVR framework designed to enhance data efficiency. The method dynamically selects training batches by re-evaluating historically difficult samples and reusing high-quality ones, all while maintaining a theoretical lower bound guarantee for policy improvement. Experimental results show that BAPO achieves an average 12.5% performance improvement over GRPO across mathematics, planning, and visual reasoning tasks, and crucially resolves 40.7% of problems that base models consistently fail to solve.
针对传统基于策略的、带可验证奖励的强化学习在大语言模型后训练中存在经验浪费和奖励同质化、阻碍困难样本学习效率的问题，本文提出了批量自适应策略优化（BAPO），这是一种离策略的强化学习框架，旨在提高后训练的数据效率。该方法通过重新评估历史困难样本并重用高质量样本，动态选择训练批次，同时为策略改进提供了理论上的下界保证。大量实验结果表明，BAPO在数学、规划和视觉推理任务上平均性能比GRPO提升了12.5%，并且关键性地解决了基础模型持续无法解决的40.7%的问题。
Generating solution paths of Markovian stochastic differential equations using diffusion models
Authors: Xuefeng Gao, Jiale Zha, Xun Yu Zhou
First: 2025-09-10T16:17:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T06:58:35+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper introduces a new approach to generating sample paths of unknown Markovian stochastic differential equations (SDEs) using diffusion models, a class of generative AI methods commonly employed in image and video applications. Unlike the traditional Monte Carlo methods for simulating SDEs, which require explicit specifications of the drift and diffusion coefficients, ours takes a model-free, data-driven approach. Given a finite set of sample paths from an SDE, we utilize conditional diffusion models to generate new, synthetic paths of the same SDE. Numerical experiments show that our method consistently outperforms two alternative methods in terms of the Kullback--Leibler (KL) divergence between the distributions of the target SDE paths and the generated ones. Moreover, we present a theoretical error analysis deriving an explicit bound on the said KL divergence. Finally, in simulation and empirical studies, we leverage these synthetically generated sample paths to boost the performance of reinforcement learning algorithms for continuous-time mean--variance portfolio selection, hinting promising applications of our study in financial analysis and decision-making.
中文标题/摘要
标题：利用扩散模型生成马尔可夫随机微分方程的解路径
本文提出了一种新方法，利用扩散模型（一类常用于图像和视频生成的生成式人工智能方法）生成未知马尔可夫随机微分方程（SDE）的样本路径。与模拟SDE的传统蒙特卡洛方法需明确指定漂移和扩散系数不同，本方法采用无模型、数据驱动的策略。给定SDE的有限样本路径集，我们利用条件扩散模型生成同一SDE的新合成路径。数值实验表明，在目标SDE路径分布与生成路径分布的Kullback-Leibler（KL）散度方面，本方法持续优于两种替代方法。此外，我们提出了理论误差分析，推导了上述KL散度的显式边界。最后，在模拟与实证研究中，我们利用这些合成样本路径提升连续时间均值-方差投资组合选择强化学习算法的性能，预示了本研究在金融分析与决策中的潜在应用前景。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to generate sample paths for Markovian stochastic differential equations (SDEs) without requiring explicit drift and diffusion coefficients, this paper proposes a model-free, data-driven method using conditional diffusion models. The approach learns from a finite set of existing SDE paths to synthesize new, realistic trajectories, bypassing traditional Monte Carlo simulations. Experimental results demonstrate that the method consistently achieves lower Kullback-Leibler divergence between generated and target path distributions compared to alternatives, and theoretical error bounds are provided. Additionally, applications in continuous-time mean-variance portfolio selection show that the synthetic paths can enhance reinforcement learning performance, indicating potential in financial analysis.
本文针对无需显式漂移和扩散系数即可生成马尔可夫随机微分方程样本路径的需求，提出了一种基于条件扩散模型的无模型数据驱动方法。该方法从有限的历史路径数据中学习，以合成新的逼真轨迹，从而绕过传统的蒙特卡洛模拟。实验结果表明，与替代方法相比，该方法在生成路径与目标路径分布的Kullback-Leibler散度上持续表现更优，并提供了理论误差界。此外，在连续时间均值-方差投资组合选择中的应用表明，合成路径能够提升强化学习算法的性能，展现了在金融分析与决策中的潜在价值。
GlobalRAG: Enhancing Global Reasoning in Multi-hop Question Answering via Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Jinchang Luo, Mingquan Cheng, Fan Wan, Ni Li, Xiaoling Xia, Shuangshuang Tian, Tingcheng Bian, Haiwei Wang, Haohuan Fu, Yan Tao
First: 2025-10-23T13:35:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T06:51:44+00:00
Comments: 8 pages, 3 figures, 4 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning has recently shown promise in improving retrieval-augmented generation (RAG). Despite these advances, its effectiveness in multi-hop question answering (QA) remains limited by two fundamental limitations: (i) global planning absence to structure multi-step reasoning, and (ii) unfaithful execution, which hinders effective query formulation and consistent use of retrieved evidence. We propose GlobalRAG, a reinforcement learning framework designed to enhance global reasoning in multi-hop QA. GlobalRAG decomposes questions into subgoals, coordinates retrieval with reasoning, and refines evidence iteratively. To guide this process, we introduce Planning Quality Reward and SubGoal Completion Reward, which encourage coherent planning and reliable subgoal execution. In addition, a progressive weight annealing strategy balances process-oriented and outcome-based objectives. Extensive experiments on both in-domain and out-of-domain benchmarks demonstrate that GlobalRAG significantly outperforms strong baselines while using only 8k training data (42% of the training data used by strong baselines), achieving average improvements of 14.2% in both EM and F1.
中文标题/摘要
标题：GlobalRAG：通过强化学习增强多跳问答中的全局推理能力
强化学习近期在改进检索增强生成（RAG）方面展现出潜力。然而，其在多跳问答（QA）中的有效性仍受限于两个根本问题：（i）缺乏构建多步推理的全局规划；（ii）执行不忠实，阻碍了有效查询构建和检索证据的一致性使用。我们提出GlobalRAG，一个旨在增强多跳QA中全局推理的强化学习框架。该框架将问题分解为子目标，协调检索与推理过程，并迭代优化证据。为引导此过程，我们引入了规划质量奖励和子目标完成奖励，以促进连贯规划和可靠子目标执行。此外，渐进权重退火策略平衡了过程导向与结果导向的目标。在领域内和领域外基准上的大量实验表明，GlobalRAG仅使用8k训练数据（仅为强基线训练数据的42%）即显著超越现有基线，在EM和F1指标上平均提升14.2%。

It proposes GlobalRAG, a framework that decomposes questions into subgoals, coordinates retrieval with reasoning, and iteratively refines evidence using novel rewards for planning quality and subgoal completion, alongside a progressive weight annealing strategy to balance process and outcome objectives. Experimental results on in-domain and out-of-domain benchmarks show that GlobalRAG significantly outperforms strong baselines with only 8k training data, achieving average improvements of 14.2% in both EM and F1 scores.

MARVL: Multi-Stage Guidance for Robotic Manipulation via Vision-Language Models
Authors: Xunlan Zhou, Xuanlin Chen, Shaowei Zhang, Xiangkun Li, ShengHua Wan, Xiaohai Hu, Lei Yuan, Le Gan, De-chuan Zhan
First: 2026-01-28T11:25:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T06:30:03+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Designing dense reward functions is pivotal for efficient robotic Reinforcement Learning (RL). However, most dense rewards rely on manual engineering, which fundamentally limits the scalability and automation of reinforcement learning. While Vision-Language Models (VLMs) offer a promising path to reward design, naive VLM rewards often misalign with task progress, struggle with spatial grounding, and show limited understanding of task semantics. To address these issues, we propose MARVL-Multi-stAge guidance for Robotic manipulation via Vision-Language models. MARVL fine-tunes a VLM for spatial and semantic consistency and decomposes tasks into multi-stage subtasks with task direction projection for trajectory sensitivity. Empirically, MARVL significantly outperforms existing VLM-reward methods on the Meta-World benchmark, demonstrating superior sample efficiency and robustness on sparse-reward manipulation tasks.
中文标题/摘要

设计密集奖励函数对高效机器人强化学习至关重要，但现有方法多依赖人工设计，制约了强化学习的可扩展性与自动化。视觉语言模型为奖励设计提供了新路径，但其原始奖励常存在任务进度失准、空间定位困难及语义理解局限等问题。为此，我们提出MARVL——基于视觉语言模型的多阶段机器人操作引导框架。该框架通过微调视觉语言模型提升空间与语义一致性，并利用任务方向投影将任务分解为具有轨迹敏感性的多阶段子任务。实验表明，MARVL在Meta-World基准测试中显著优于现有视觉语言模型奖励方法，在稀疏奖励操作任务中展现出更优的样本效率与鲁棒性。

Experimental results on the Meta-World benchmark show that MARVL significantly outperforms existing VLM-reward methods, achieving superior sample efficiency and robustness in sparse-reward manipulation tasks.
