Sample-Efficient Hypergradient Estimation for Decentralized Bi-Level Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Mikoto Kudo, Takumi Tanabe, Akifumi Wachi, Youhei Akimoto
First: 2026-03-16T06:11:00+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T06:11:00+00:00
Comments: 26 pages. Accepted at ICAPS 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Many strategic decision-making problems, such as environment design for warehouse robots, can be naturally formulated as bi-level reinforcement learning (RL), where a leader agent optimizes its objective while a follower solves a Markov decision process (MDP) conditioned on the leader's decisions. In many situations, a fundamental challenge arises when the leader cannot intervene in the follower's optimization process; it can only observe the optimization outcome. We address this decentralized setting by deriving the hypergradient of the leader's objective, i.e., the gradient of the leader's strategy that accounts for changes in the follower's optimal policy. Unlike prior hypergradient-based methods that require extensive data for repeated state visits or rely on gradient estimators whose complexity can increase substantially with the high-dimensional leader's decision space, we leverage the Boltzmann covariance trick to derive an alternative hypergradient formulation. This enables efficient hypergradient estimation solely from interaction samples, even when the leader's decision space is high-dimensional. Additionally, to our knowledge, this is the first method that enables hypergradient-based optimization for 2-player Markov games in decentralized settings. Experiments highlight the impact of hypergradient updates and demonstrate our method's effectiveness in both discrete and continuous state tasks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：去中心化双层强化学习中的样本高效超梯度估计方法
许多战略决策问题（如仓库机器人的环境设计）可自然建模为双层强化学习：领导者智能体优化其目标函数，而跟随者在领导者决策条件下求解马尔可夫决策过程。当领导者无法干预跟随者优化过程、仅能观测优化结果时，便面临核心挑战。本文通过推导领导者目标函数的超梯度（即考虑跟随者最优策略变化的领导者策略梯度）来解决这一去中心化场景。相较于现有需要大量重复状态访问数据、或梯度估计器复杂度随高维决策空间急剧增加的超梯度方法，我们利用玻尔兹曼协方差技巧推导出替代的超梯度形式，仅通过交互样本即可实现高效估计，且适用于高维决策空间。据我们所知，这是首个支持去中心化场景下双人马尔可夫博弈超梯度优化的方法。实验验证了超梯度更新的有效性，并在离散与连续状态任务中证明了方法的优越性。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of decentralized bi-level reinforcement learning, where a leader agent must optimize its objective based only on observing the outcomes of a follower's independent optimization process, without direct intervention. To tackle this, the authors derive a hypergradient for the leader's objective by employing the Boltzmann covariance trick, which allows for efficient estimation of this gradient using only interaction samples, even in high-dimensional decision spaces, and extends hypergradient-based optimization to decentralized two-player Markov games. Experimental results demonstrate that the proposed method effectively enables hypergradient updates and performs well across both discrete and continuous state tasks, showcasing its sample efficiency and applicability.
本文针对去中心化双层强化学习中的挑战，即领导者智能体只能观察跟随者独立优化过程的结果，而无法直接干预，需据此优化自身目标。为解决此问题，作者利用玻尔兹曼协方差技巧推导了领导者目标的超梯度，使得仅通过交互样本即可高效估计该梯度，即使在高维决策空间中也能适用，并将基于超梯度的优化方法首次扩展到去中心化的双人马尔可夫博弈中。实验结果表明，所提方法能有效实现超梯度更新，在离散和连续状态任务中均表现良好，证明了其样本高效性和适用性。
Overthinking Reduction with Decoupled Rewards and Curriculum Data Scheduling
Authors: Shuyang Jiang, Yusheng Liao, Ya Zhang, Yanfeng Wang, Yu Wang
Venue: ICLR 2026 oral presentation
First: 2025-09-30T06:04:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T05:33:52+00:00
Comments: 30 pages; Accepted as an oral presentation at ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
While large reasoning models trained with critic-free reinforcement learning and verifiable rewards (RLVR) represent the state-of-the-art, their practical utility is hampered by ``overthinking'', a critical issue where models generate excessively long reasoning paths without any performance benefit. Existing solutions that penalize length often fail, inducing performance degradation due to a fundamental misalignment between trajectory-level rewards and token-level optimization. In this work, we introduce a novel framework, DECS, built on our theoretical discovery of two previously unaddressed flaws in current length rewards: (1) the erroneous penalization of essential exploratory tokens and (2) the inadvertent rewarding of partial redundancy. Our framework's innovations include (i) a first-of-its-kind decoupled token-level reward mechanism that surgically distinguishes and penalizes redundant tokens, and (ii) a novel curriculum batch scheduling strategy to master the efficiency-efficacy equilibrium. Experimental results show DECS can achieve a dramatic reduction in reasoning tokens by over 50\% across seven benchmarks while simultaneously maintaining or even improving performance. It demonstrates conclusively that substantial gains in reasoning efficiency can be achieved without compromising a model's underlying reasoning power. Code is available at https://github.com/pixas/DECS.
中文标题/摘要
标题：解耦奖励与课程数据调度：对过度思考问题的优化研究
尽管采用无评判强化学习与可验证奖励（RLVR）训练的大型推理模型代表了当前最高水平，但其实际应用受到“过度思考”问题的严重制约——模型生成过长的推理路径却未带来性能提升。现有惩罚长度的方案常因轨迹级奖励与词元级优化的根本错位而失效，甚至导致性能下降。本研究基于对当前长度奖励机制两个未受重视缺陷的理论发现：（1）对必要探索性词元的错误惩罚；（2）对部分冗余内容的无意奖励，提出了创新框架DECS。该框架包含两大突破：（i）首创的解耦词元级奖励机制，能精准识别并惩罚冗余词元；（ii）创新的课程批次调度策略，以掌握效率与效能的平衡。实验表明，DECS在七个基准测试中实现推理词元量减少超50%，同时保持甚至提升模型性能，确证了在不损害模型底层推理能力的前提下显著提升推理效率的可行性。代码发布于https://github.com/pixas/DECS。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the problem of 'overthinking' in large reasoning models, where models produce excessively long reasoning paths without performance gains, this paper introduces the DECS framework. The method addresses flaws in existing length-penalty approaches by proposing a decoupled token-level reward mechanism that specifically penalizes redundant tokens and a curriculum batch scheduling strategy to balance efficiency and efficacy. Experimental results across seven benchmarks demonstrate that DECS reduces reasoning tokens by over 50% while maintaining or improving performance, showing that reasoning efficiency can be enhanced without compromising reasoning power.
本文针对大型推理模型中存在的'过度思考'问题，即模型生成过长的推理路径却无性能提升，提出了DECS框架。该方法通过引入解耦的令牌级奖励机制来精准惩罚冗余令牌，并采用课程批次调度策略以平衡效率与效果，从而解决了现有长度惩罚方法的缺陷。在七个基准测试上的实验结果表明，DECS能将推理令牌减少超过50%，同时保持或提升性能，证明了推理效率可在不损害推理能力的情况下显著提高。
Breaking the SFT Plateau: Multimodal Structured Reinforcement Learning for Chart-to-Code Generation
Authors: Lei Chen, Xuanle Zhao, Zhixiong Zeng, Jing Huang, Liming Zheng, Yufeng Zhong, Lin Ma
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-08-19T07:40:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T04:37:34+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
While reinforcement learning (RL) has proven highly effective for general reasoning in vision-language models, its application to tasks requiring deep understanding of information-rich images and structured output generation remains underexplored. Chart-to-code generation exemplifies this challenge, demanding complex reasoning over visual charts to produce structured code. Supervised fine-tuning (SFT) alone is often insufficient, highlighting the need for effective RL strategies tailored to structured outputs. In this paper, we systematically investigate the performance plateau of SFT through large-scale experiments and propose Multimodal Structured Reinforcement Learning (MSRL) for chart-to-code generation. We construct the largest training corpus to date, with 3 million chart-code pairs curated from real-world tables in arXiv papers, addressing the limitations of previous synthetic datasets. Despite achieving state-of-the-art performance, our experiments show that simply increasing SFT data eventually leads to diminishing improvements. To break this plateau, MSRL employs a multi-granularity reward system that integrates both textual and visual feedback. At the textual level, rule-based rewards validate fine-grained code details, while at the visual level, a model-based reward assesses the structural similarity between rendered code and ground-truth charts. We implement a two-stage curriculum training strategy, first optimizing the model with textual rewards and then incorporating visual signals for further enhancement. Experimental results demonstrate that MSRL substantially breaks the SFT plateau, improving high-level metrics by 6.2% and 9.9% on ChartMimic and ReachQA benchmarks, respectively. Notably, our method outperforms all existing approaches in the chart domain and achieves competitive results with advanced closed-source models.
中文标题/摘要
标题：突破SFT瓶颈：面向图表转代码生成的多模态结构化强化学习
尽管强化学习在视觉语言模型的通用推理任务中成效显著，但其在需要深度理解信息密集型图像并生成结构化输出的任务中仍待深入探索。图表转代码生成正是此类挑战的典型代表，它要求对视觉图表进行复杂推理以生成结构化代码。仅靠监督微调往往不足，凸显了针对结构化输出定制有效强化学习策略的必要性。本文通过大规模实验系统研究了SFT的性能瓶颈，并提出面向图表转代码生成的多模态结构化强化学习框架。我们构建了迄今最大的训练语料库，包含从arXiv论文真实表格中精选的300万图表-代码对，解决了以往合成数据集的局限性。实验表明，尽管实现了最先进性能，但单纯增加SFT数据最终会导致改进收益递减。为突破此瓶颈，MSRL采用融合文本与视觉反馈的多粒度奖励系统：文本层面通过基于规则的奖励验证细粒度代码细节，视觉层面则通过基于模型的奖励评估渲染代码与真实图表间的结构相似性。我们实施两阶段课程训练策略，先以文本奖励优化模型，再融入视觉信号进行增强。实验结果表明，MSRL显著突破了SFT瓶颈，在ChartMimic和ReachQA基准上分别将高层级指标提升6.2%和9.9%。值得注意的是，本方法在图表领域超越所有现有方案，并与先进闭源模型取得相当成果。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the performance plateau of supervised fine-tuning (SFT) in chart-to-code generation, a task requiring complex reasoning from information-rich images to produce structured code. The authors propose Multimodal Structured Reinforcement Learning (MSRL), which utilizes a multi-granularity reward system combining rule-based textual feedback for code details and a model-based visual reward for structural similarity between rendered and ground-truth charts, trained via a two-stage curriculum. Experiments on a large-scale corpus of 3 million real-world chart-code pairs show MSRL breaks the SFT plateau, improving high-level metrics by 6.2% and 9.9% on ChartMimic and ReachQA benchmarks, outperforming existing chart-domain methods and achieving competitive results with advanced closed-source models.
本文针对监督微调在图表到代码生成任务中出现的性能瓶颈问题展开研究，该任务需要从信息丰富的图像中进行复杂推理以生成结构化代码。作者提出了多模态结构化强化学习方法，采用多粒度奖励系统，结合了基于规则的文本反馈来验证代码细节，以及基于模型的视觉奖励来评估生成代码渲染后与真实图表的结构相似性，并通过两阶段课程策略进行训练。基于构建的300万真实世界图表-代码对的大规模语料实验表明，该方法有效突破了监督微调的性能瓶颈，在ChartMimic和ReachQA基准上分别将高级指标提升了6.2%和9.9%，超越了现有图表领域方法，并与先进的闭源模型取得了具有竞争力的结果。
LLM-Driven Instance-Specific Heuristic Generation and Selection
Authors: Shaofeng Zhang, Shengcai Liu, Ning Lu, Jiahao Wu, Ji Liu, Yew-Soon Ong, Ke Tang
First: 2025-05-31T09:54:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T04:10:52+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Combinatorial optimization problems are widely encountered in real-world applications. A critical research challenge lies in designing high-quality heuristic algorithms that efficiently approximate optimal solutions within a reasonable time. In recent years, many works have explored integrating Large Language Models (LLMs) with Evolutionary Algorithms to automate heuristic algorithm design through prompt engineering. However, these approaches generally adopt a problem-specific paradigm, applying a single algorithm across all problem instances, failing to account for the heterogeneity across instances. In this paper, we propose InstSpecHH, a novel framework that introduces the concept of instance-specific heuristic generation. InstSpecHH partitions the overall problem class into sub-classes based on instance features and performs differentiated, automated heuristic design for each problem subclass. By tailoring heuristics to the unique features of different sub-classes, InstSpecHH achieves better performance at the problem class level while avoiding redundant heuristic generation for similar instances, thus reducing computational overhead. This approach effectively balances the trade-off between the cost of automatic heuristic design and the quality of the obtained solutions. To evaluate the performance of InstSpecHH, we conduct comprehensive experiments on 4,500 subclasses of the Online Bin Packing Problem (OBPP) and 365 subclasses of the Capacitated Vehicle Routing Problem (CVRP). Experimental results show that InstSpecHH demonstrates strong intra-subclass and inter-subclass generalization capabilities. Compared to previous problem-specific methods, InstSpecHH reduces the average optimality gap by 6.06\% for OBPP and 0.66\% for CVRP. These results highlight the potential of instance-aware automatic heuristic design to further enhance solution quality.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于大语言模型的实例特定启发式生成与选择
组合优化问题在现实应用中广泛存在。核心研究挑战在于设计高质量的启发式算法，以在合理时间内高效逼近最优解。近年来，许多研究探索通过提示工程将大语言模型与进化算法结合，实现启发式算法的自动化设计。然而，这些方法通常采用问题特定范式，对所有问题实例应用单一算法，未能考虑实例间的异质性。本文提出InstSpecHH框架，引入实例特定启发式生成概念。该框架基于实例特征将整体问题类别划分为子类，并对每个问题子类进行差异化的自动化启发式设计。通过为不同子类的独特特征定制启发式，InstSpecHH在问题类别层面实现了更优性能，同时避免对相似实例的冗余启发式生成，从而降低计算开销。该方法有效平衡了自动启发式设计成本与所得解质量之间的权衡。为评估InstSpecHH性能，我们在在线装箱问题的4500个子类和容量约束车辆路径问题的365个子类上进行了全面实验。结果表明，InstSpecHH展现出强大的子类内与子类间泛化能力。与先前问题特定方法相比，InstSpecHH将在线装箱问题的平均最优间隙降低了6.06%，容量约束车辆路径问题降低了0.66%。这些结果凸显了实例感知的自动启发式设计在进一步提升解质量方面的潜力。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of existing LLM-driven heuristic design methods that apply a single algorithm to all instances of a combinatorial optimization problem, ignoring instance heterogeneity, this paper proposes InstSpecHH, a framework for instance-specific heuristic generation. The method partitions a problem class into sub-classes based on instance features and performs automated, differentiated heuristic design for each subclass, balancing design cost and solution quality. Experimental results on Online Bin Packing and Capacitated Vehicle Routing problems, involving thousands of subclasses, demonstrate strong generalization and reduced optimality gaps of 6.06% and 0.66% respectively compared to prior problem-specific approaches.
针对现有基于大语言模型的启发式设计方法通常采用单一算法处理组合优化问题的所有实例、忽略实例异质性的局限，本文提出了InstSpecHH框架，旨在实现实例特定的启发式生成。该方法根据实例特征将问题类别划分为子类，并为每个子类进行差异化的自动化启发式设计，以平衡设计成本与求解质量。在在线装箱问题和带容量车辆路径问题上的实验，涉及数千个子类，结果表明该方法具有良好的子类内和子类间泛化能力，与先前问题特定方法相比，平均最优性差距分别降低了6.06%和0.66%。
Bayesian Optimization with Gaussian Processes to Accelerate Stationary Point Searches
Authors: Rohit Goswami
First: 2026-03-11T17:20:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T04:02:24+00:00
Comments: 60 pages, 24 figures. Invited article for ACS Physical Chemistry Au
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Accelerating the explorations of stationary points on potential energy surfaces building local surrogates spans decades of effort. Done correctly, surrogates reduce required evaluations by an order of magnitude while preserving the accuracy of the underlying theory. We present a unified Bayesian Optimization view of minimization, single point saddle searches, and double ended saddle searches through a unified six-step surrogate loop, differing only in the inner optimization target and acquisition criterion. The framework uses Gaussian process regression with derivative observations, inverse-distance kernels, and active learning. The Optimal Transport GP extensions of farthest point sampling with Earth mover's distance, MAP regularization via variance barrier and oscillation detection, and adaptive trust radius form concrete extensions of the same basic methodology, improving accuracy and efficiency. We also demonstrate random Fourier features decouple hyperparameter training from predictions enabling favorable scaling for high-dimensional systems. Accompanying pedagogical Rust code demonstrates that all applications use the exact same Bayesian optimization loop, bridging the gap between theoretical formulation and practical execution.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于高斯过程的贝叶斯优化加速势能面驻点搜索
通过构建局部代理模型加速势能面驻点探索已历经数十年研究。正确实施的代理模型能在保持底层理论精度的同时，将所需计算量降低一个数量级。本文提出统一的贝叶斯优化框架，通过六步代理循环统一处理极小值点搜索、单点鞍点搜索和双端鞍点搜索，仅在内层优化目标和采集准则上存在差异。该框架采用含导数观测的高斯过程回归、反距离核函数及主动学习策略。通过最远点采样与推土机距离的最优传输GP扩展、基于方差屏障与振荡检测的MAP正则化、自适应信任半径等方法，在基础方法论上形成具体扩展，提升了精度与效率。随机傅里叶特征的应用实现超参数训练与预测解耦，为高维系统提供优越的扩展性。配套的Rust教学代码表明所有应用均采用完全相同的贝叶斯优化循环，弥合了理论构建与实际执行间的鸿沟。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the long-standing challenge of efficiently exploring stationary points on potential energy surfaces, this paper presents a unified Bayesian Optimization framework using Gaussian processes to accelerate such searches. The method employs a six-step surrogate loop with Gaussian process regression incorporating derivative observations, inverse-distance kernels, and active learning, extended with techniques like Optimal Transport GP for sampling and random Fourier features for scalable hyperparameter training. Key experimental results demonstrate that the framework reduces required evaluations by an order of magnitude while maintaining accuracy, effectively unifying minimization and saddle point searches, and its practical implementation is showcased through accompanying pedagogical code.
本文旨在解决势能面上平稳点高效搜索这一长期存在的挑战，提出了一个基于高斯过程的统一贝叶斯优化框架来加速此类搜索。该方法采用一个六步代理循环，结合了导数观测、反距离核和主动学习的高斯过程回归，并通过最优传输高斯过程进行采样扩展以及随机傅里叶特征实现可扩展的超参数训练。主要实验结果表明，该框架在保持精度的同时将所需评估次数减少了一个数量级，有效统一了最小化和鞍点搜索，并通过配套的教学代码展示了其实际应用。
CRAFT: Calibrated Reasoning with Answer-Faithful Traces via Reinforcement Learning for Multi-Hop Question Answering
Authors: Yu Liu, Wenxiao Zhang, Diandian Guo, Cong Cao, Fangfang Yuan, Qiang Sun, Yanbing Liu, Jin B. Hong, Zhiyuan Ma
First: 2026-02-01T17:33:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T03:48:31+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Retrieval-augmented large language models, when optimized with outcome-level rewards, can achieve strong answer accuracy on multi-hop questions. However, under noisy retrieval, models frequently suffer from "right-answer-wrong-reason failures": they may exploit spurious shortcuts or produce reasoning traces weakly grounded in the supporting evidence. Furthermore, the lack of structured output control prevents reliable auditing of the underlying reasoning quality. To address this, we propose CRAFT (Calibrated Reasoning with Answer-Faithful Traces), a reinforcement learning framework for the response generation stage of retrieval-augmented multi-hop question answering. CRAFT trains models to produce structured reasoning traces with configurable levels of auditability (e.g., by selectively retaining planning, evidence citation, or reasoning steps). Training combines two complementary forms of supervision: deterministic rewards enforce verifiable constraints, including format compliance, answer correctness, and citation-set validity, while a judge-based reward audits semantic faithfulness by evaluating reasoning consistency and evidence grounding. Experiments show that CRAFT improves both answer accuracy and reasoning faithfulness across model scales. Notably, semantic judge-based rewards improve answer accuracy rather than compromise it, enabling CRAFT (7B) to achieve performance competitive with strong closed-source models.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CRAFT：基于强化学习的答案忠实轨迹校准推理用于多跳问答
检索增强的大型语言模型在通过结果级奖励优化后，能在多跳问题上实现较高的答案准确率。然而，在噪声检索条件下，模型常出现“答案正确但推理错误”的故障：它们可能利用虚假捷径或生成与支持证据关联薄弱的推理轨迹。此外，缺乏结构化输出控制阻碍了对底层推理质量的可靠审计。为此，我们提出CRAFT（答案忠实轨迹校准推理），一个用于检索增强多跳问答响应生成阶段的强化学习框架。CRAFT训练模型生成具有可配置审计层级（如选择性保留规划、证据引用或推理步骤）的结构化推理轨迹。训练结合两种互补的监督形式：确定性奖励强制执行可验证约束（包括格式合规性、答案正确性和引用集有效性），而基于评判器的奖励通过评估推理一致性和证据锚定性来审计语义忠实度。实验表明，CRAFT在不同规模模型上均提升了答案准确率和推理忠实度。值得注意的是，基于语义评判器的奖励不仅未损害答案准确率，反而提升了该指标，使CRAFT（7B参数版本）达到了与强闭源模型相竞争的性能水平。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the issue that retrieval-augmented large language models, when optimized for answer accuracy, often produce reasoning traces that are weakly grounded in evidence or rely on spurious shortcuts, especially under noisy retrieval, making it hard to audit reasoning quality. To address this, the authors propose CRAFT, a reinforcement learning framework that trains models to generate structured reasoning traces with configurable auditability by combining deterministic rewards for format compliance, answer correctness, and citation validity with judge-based rewards for semantic faithfulness. Experimental results demonstrate that CRAFT improves both answer accuracy and reasoning faithfulness across model scales, with semantic judge-based rewards boosting accuracy rather than compromising it, allowing a 7B model to achieve performance competitive with strong closed-source models.
本文的动机在于，检索增强的大型语言模型在针对答案准确性进行优化时，尤其是在噪声检索下，经常产生与证据关联薄弱或依赖虚假捷径的推理轨迹，使得推理质量难以审计。为解决此问题，作者提出了CRAFT，一个强化学习框架，通过结合确定性奖励（用于格式合规性、答案正确性和引用有效性）与基于评判者的奖励（用于语义忠实度），训练模型生成具有可配置可审计性的结构化推理轨迹。实验结果表明，CRAFT在不同模型规模上均提高了答案准确性和推理忠实度，其中语义评判者奖励不仅未损害准确性反而提升了它，使得一个7B模型能够达到与强大闭源模型竞争的性能。
BadLLM-TG: A Backdoor Defender powered by LLM Trigger Generator
Authors: Ruyi Zhang, Heng Gao, Songlei Jian, Yusong Tan, Haifang Zhou
First: 2026-03-16T03:31:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T03:31:54+00:00
Comments: 5pages, 2 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Backdoor attacks compromise model reliability by using triggers to manipulate outputs. Trigger inversion can accurately locate these triggers via a generator and is therefore critical for backdoor defense. However, the discrete nature of text prevents existing noise-based trigger generator from being applied to nature language processing (NLP). To overcome the limitations, we employ the rich knowledge embedded in large language models (LLMs) and propose a Backdoor defender powered by LLM Trigger Generator, termed BadLLM-TG. It is optimized through prompt-driven reinforcement learning, using the victim model's feedback loss as the reward signal. The generated triggers are then employed to mitigate the backdoor via adversarial training. Experiments show that our method reduces the attack success rate by 76.2\% on average, outperforming the second-best defender by 13.7.
中文标题/摘要
标题：BadLLM-TG：基于大语言模型触发器生成器的后门防御器
后门攻击通过触发器操纵模型输出，损害模型可靠性。触发器反演能通过生成器准确定位这些触发器，对后门防御至关重要。然而，文本的离散性使现有基于噪声的触发器生成器无法应用于自然语言处理（NLP）。为突破此限制，我们利用大语言模型（LLM）中蕴含的丰富知识，提出一种基于LLM触发器生成器的后门防御器，命名为BadLLM-TG。该方法通过提示驱动的强化学习进行优化，以受害模型的反馈损失作为奖励信号。生成的触发器随后通过对抗训练来缓解后门影响。实验表明，我们的方法平均降低攻击成功率76.2%，较次优防御器提升13.7%。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of defending against backdoor attacks in natural language processing models, where existing noise-based trigger generation methods are ineffective due to the discrete nature of text. The authors propose BadLLM-TG, a backdoor defender that leverages the knowledge of large language models to generate triggers through prompt-driven reinforcement learning, using the victim model's feedback loss as a reward signal, and then applies adversarial training to mitigate the backdoor. Experimental results demonstrate that the method reduces the attack success rate by an average of 76.2%, outperforming the second-best defender by 13.7%.
本文针对自然语言处理模型中后门攻击的防御挑战，由于文本的离散特性，现有基于噪声的触发器生成方法难以适用。作者提出BadLLM-TG，一种利用大语言模型知识、通过提示驱动的强化学习生成触发器的后门防御器，以受害模型的反馈损失作为奖励信号，并采用对抗训练来缓解后门。实验结果表明，该方法平均将攻击成功率降低了76.2%，优于次优防御器13.7%。
DeFRiS: Silo-Cooperative IoT Applications Scheduling via Decentralized Federated Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Zhiyu Wang, Mohammad Goudarzi, Mingming Gong, Rajkumar Buyya
First: 2026-03-16T02:02:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T02:02:38+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Next-generation IoT applications increasingly span across autonomous administrative entities, necessitating silo-cooperative scheduling to leverage diverse computational resources while preserving data privacy. However, realizing efficient cooperation faces significant challenges arising from infrastructure heterogeneity, Non-IID workload shifts, and the inherent risks of adversarial environments. Existing approaches, relying predominantly on centralized coordination or independent learning, fail to address the incompatibility of state-action spaces across heterogeneous silos and lack robustness against malicious attacks. This paper proposes DeFRiS, a Decentralized Federated Reinforcement Learning framework for robust and scalable Silo-cooperative IoT application scheduling. DeFRiS integrates three synergistic innovations: (i) an action-space-agnostic policy utilizing candidate resource scoring to enable seamless knowledge transfer across heterogeneous silos; (ii) a silo-optimized local learning mechanism combining Generalized Advantage Estimation (GAE) with clipped policy updates to resolve sparse delayed reward challenges; and (iii) a Dual-Track Non-IID robust decentralized aggregation protocol leveraging gradient fingerprints for similarity-aware knowledge transfer and anomaly detection, and gradient tracking for optimization momentum. Extensive experiments on a distributed testbed with 20 heterogeneous silos and realistic IoT workloads demonstrate that DeFRiS significantly outperforms state-of-the-art baselines, reducing average response time by 6.4% and energy consumption by 7.2%, while lowering tail latency risk (CVaR$_{0.95}$) by 10.4% and achieving near-zero deadline violations. Furthermore, DeFRiS achieves over 3 times better performance retention as the system scales and over 8 times better stability in adversarial environments compared to the best-performing baseline.
中文标题/摘要
标题：DeFRiS：基于去中心化联邦强化学习的孤岛协同物联网应用调度
新一代物联网应用日益跨越自主管理实体，需通过孤岛协同调度以整合异构计算资源并保障数据隐私。然而，基础设施异构性、非独立同分布负载偏移及对抗性环境风险，为高效协同带来严峻挑战。现有方法主要依赖集中协调或独立学习，难以解决异构孤岛间状态-动作空间不兼容问题，且缺乏对抗恶意攻击的鲁棒性。本文提出DeFRiS——一种基于去中心化联邦强化学习的鲁棒可扩展孤岛协同物联网应用调度框架。该框架融合三项协同创新：（1）采用候选资源评分的动作空间无关策略，实现跨异构孤岛的无缝知识迁移；（2）结合广义优势估计与截断策略更新的孤岛优化本地学习机制，解决稀疏延迟奖励难题；（3）基于梯度指纹的双轨非独立同分布鲁棒去中心化聚合协议，通过相似性感知知识迁移与异常检测实现梯度追踪优化动量。在含20个异构孤岛的分布式测试平台上，针对真实物联网负载的广泛实验表明：DeFRiS显著优于现有基线方法，平均响应时间降低6.4%，能耗减少7.2%，尾部延迟风险（CVaR$_{0.95}$）下降10.4%，近乎实现零截止时间违规。此外，在系统扩展时DeFRiS性能保持能力超最优基线3倍以上，在对抗环境中稳定性提升超8倍。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for privacy-preserving and efficient scheduling of IoT applications across autonomous administrative silos with heterogeneous resources and non-IID workloads, this paper proposes DeFRiS, a decentralized federated reinforcement learning framework. The method introduces an action-space-agnostic policy for cross-silo knowledge transfer, a local learning mechanism with Generalized Advantage Estimation to handle sparse rewards, and a dual-track robust aggregation protocol for non-IID resilience and security. Experimental results on a 20-silo testbed show DeFRiS reduces average response time by 6.4% and energy consumption by 7.2%, significantly lowers tail latency risk and deadline violations, and demonstrates superior scalability and adversarial robustness compared to baselines.
本文针对跨自治管理域、资源异构且工作负载非独立同分布的物联网应用调度需求，旨在实现隐私保护下的高效协同，提出了名为DeFRiS的去中心化联邦强化学习框架。该方法融合了三项创新：采用与动作空间无关的策略以实现跨异构孤岛的知识迁移，结合广义优势估计的本地学习机制处理稀疏延迟奖励，以及利用梯度指纹和跟踪的双轨聚合协议保证非独立同分布环境下的鲁棒性。在包含20个异构孤岛的分布式测试平台上的实验表明，DeFRiS显著优于现有基线，平均响应时间降低6.4%，能耗降低7.2%，尾部延迟风险大幅下降，几乎无截止时间违规，并且在可扩展性和对抗环境稳定性方面表现优异。
Deterministic Policy Gradient for Reinforcement Learning with Continuous Time and State
Authors: Ziheng Cheng, Xin Guo, Yufei Zhang
First: 2025-09-28T07:53:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T00:09:34+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The theory of continuous-time reinforcement learning (RL) has progressed rapidly in recent years. While the ultimate objective of RL is typically to learn deterministic control policies, most existing continuous-time RL methods rely on stochastic policies. Such approaches often require sampling actions at very high frequencies, and involve computationally expensive expectations over continuous action spaces, resulting in high-variance gradient estimates and slow convergence. In this paper, we introduce and develop deterministic policy gradient (DPG) methods for continuous-time RL. We derive a continuous-time policy gradient formula expressed as the expected gradient of an advantage rate function and establish a martingale characterization for both the value function and the advantage rate. These theoretical results provide tractable estimators for deterministic policy gradients in continuous-time RL. Building on this foundation, we propose a model-free continuous-time Deep Deterministic Policy Gradient (CT-DDPG) algorithm that enables stable learning for general reinforcement learning problems with continuous time-and-state. Numerical experiments show that CT-DDPG achieves superior stability and faster convergence compared to existing stochastic-policy methods, across a wide range of learning tasks with varying time discretizations and noise levels.
中文标题/摘要
标题：连续时间与状态强化学习的确定性策略梯度方法
近年来，连续时间强化学习理论发展迅速。尽管强化学习的最终目标通常是学习确定性控制策略，但现有连续时间强化学习方法大多依赖随机策略。这类方法通常需要以极高频率采样动作，并涉及对连续动作空间进行计算代价高昂的期望运算，导致梯度估计方差大、收敛速度慢。本文针对连续时间强化学习提出并发展了确定性策略梯度方法。我们推导出以优势率函数梯度期望形式表达的连续时间策略梯度公式，并为值函数和优势率建立了鞅表征。这些理论结果为连续时间强化学习中的确定性策略梯度提供了可处理的估计量。在此基础上，我们提出一种无模型的连续时间深度确定性策略梯度算法，该算法能够为具有连续时间与状态的通用强化学习问题实现稳定学习。数值实验表明，在具有不同时间离散化程度和噪声水平的一系列学习任务中，该算法相比现有随机策略方法具有更优的稳定性和更快的收敛速度。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the computational inefficiency and high variance of stochastic policies in continuous-time reinforcement learning, which require frequent action sampling and expensive expectations, this paper introduces deterministic policy gradient methods for continuous-time RL. The method derives a policy gradient formula as the expected gradient of an advantage rate function, establishes martingale characterizations for value and advantage, and proposes a model-free CT-DDPG algorithm. Experimental results demonstrate that CT-DDPG achieves superior stability and faster convergence compared to stochastic-policy methods across various tasks with different time discretizations and noise levels.
针对连续时间强化学习中随机策略计算效率低、方差高的问题，该方法引入了确定性策略梯度。通过推导优势率函数的期望梯度公式，建立价值和优势的鞅表征，并提出了无模型的CT-DDPG算法。实验结果表明，在不同时间离散化和噪声水平的学习任务中，CT-DDPG相比随机策略方法具有更优的稳定性和更快的收敛速度。
MapReduce LoRA: Advancing the Pareto Front in Multi-Preference Optimization for Generative Models
Authors: Chieh-Yun Chen, Zhonghao Wang, Qi Chen, Zhifan Ye, Min Shi, Yue Zhao, Yinan Zhao, Hui Qu, Wei-An Lin, Yiru Shen, Ajinkya Kale, Irfan Essa, Humphrey Shi
Venue: CVPR 2026
First: 2025-11-25T18:49:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T23:35:20+00:00
Comments: CVPR 2026; Code: https://github.com/SHI-Labs/MapReduce-LoRA
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF) with reward models has advanced alignment of generative models to human aesthetic and perceptual preferences. However, jointly optimizing multiple rewards often incurs an alignment tax, improving one dimension while degrading others. To address this, we introduce two complementary methods: MapReduce LoRA and Reward-aware Token Embedding (RaTE). MapReduce LoRA trains preference-specific LoRA experts in parallel and iteratively merges them to refine a shared base model; RaTE learns reward-specific token embeddings that compose at inference for flexible preference control. Experiments on Text-to-Image generation (Stable Diffusion 3.5 Medium and FLUX.1-dev) show improvements of 36.1%, 4.6%, and 55.7%, and 32.7%, 4.3%, and 67.1% on GenEval, PickScore, and OCR, respectively. On Text-to-Video generation (HunyuanVideo), visual and motion quality improve by 48.1% and 90.0%, respectively. On the language task, Helpful Assistant, with Llama-2 7B, helpful and harmless improve by 43.4% and 136.7%, respectively. Our framework sets a new state-of-the-art multi-preference alignment recipe across modalities.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MapReduce LoRA：推进生成模型多偏好优化的帕累托前沿
基于奖励模型的人类反馈强化学习（RLHF）提升了生成模型与人类审美及感知偏好的对齐能力。然而，联合优化多个奖励常引发对齐代价，即提升某一维度时其他维度会退化。为此，我们提出两种互补方法：MapReduce LoRA 与奖励感知词元嵌入（RaTE）。MapReduce LoRA 并行训练针对特定偏好的LoRA专家模型，并通过迭代融合优化共享基础模型；RaTE 学习奖励特定的词元嵌入，在推理时组合以实现灵活的偏好控制。在文生图任务（Stable Diffusion 3.5 Medium 与 FLUX.1-dev）的实验中，GenEval、PickScore 与 OCR 指标分别提升36.1%、4.6%、55.7% 和 32.7%、4.3%、67.1%。在文生视频任务（HunyuanVideo）中，视觉与运动质量分别提升48.1% 与 90.0%。在语言任务（Helpful Assistant，基于Llama-2 7B）中，助益性与无害性分别提升43.4% 与 136.7%。本框架为跨模态多偏好对齐确立了新的最优方案。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the alignment tax in generative models, where optimizing for multiple human preferences often leads to trade-offs that degrade some qualities while improving others. To mitigate this, the authors propose two methods: MapReduce LoRA, which trains and merges preference-specific Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) experts in parallel to refine a base model, and Reward-aware Token Embedding (RaTE), which learns reward-specific embeddings for flexible preference control at inference. Experimental results across text-to-image (Stable Diffusion 3.5 Medium and FLUX.1-dev), text-to-video (HunyuanVideo), and language (Llama-2 7B) tasks show significant improvements, such as up to 67.1% on OCR scores for images and 136.7% on harmlessness for language, establishing a new state-of-the-art in multi-preference alignment.
本文针对生成模型中的对齐税问题，即优化多个人类偏好时常常导致某些质量下降而其他质量提升的权衡。为解决此问题，作者提出了两种方法：MapReduce LoRA，通过并行训练并合并偏好特定的低秩适应（LoRA）专家来优化基础模型；以及奖励感知词嵌入（RaTE），学习奖励特定的词嵌入以在推理时灵活控制偏好。在文本到图像（Stable Diffusion 3.5 Medium 和 FLUX.1-dev）、文本到视频（HunyuanVideo）和语言（Llama-2 7B）任务上的实验结果显示显著改进，例如图像OCR分数最高提升67.1%，语言无害性提升136.7%，从而在多偏好对齐方面确立了新的最先进方法。
VisionCoach: Reinforcing Grounded Video Reasoning via Visual-Perception Prompting
Authors: Daeun Lee, Shoubin Yu, Yue Zhang, Mohit Bansal
First: 2026-03-15T23:32:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T23:32:02+00:00
Comments: Project website: https://visioncoach.github.io/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Video reasoning requires models to locate and track question-relevant evidence across frames. While reinforcement learning (RL) with verifiable rewards improves accuracy, it still struggles to achieve reliable spatio-temporal grounding during the reasoning process. Moreover, improving grounding typically relies on scaled training data or inference-time perception tools, which increases annotation cost or computational cost. To address this challenge, we propose VisonCoach, an input-adaptive RL framework that improves spatio-temporal grounding through visual prompting as training-time guidance. During RL training, visual prompts are selectively applied to challenging inputs to amplify question-relevant evidence and suppress distractors. The model then internalizes these improvements through self-distillation, enabling grounded reasoning directly on raw videos without visual prompting at inference. VisonCoach consists of two components: (1) Visual Prompt Selector, which predicts appropriate prompt types conditioned on the video and question, and (2) Spatio-Temporal Reasoner, optimized with RL under visual prompt guidance and object-aware grounding rewards that enforce object identity consistency and multi-region bounding-box overlap. Extensive experiments demonstrate that VisonCoach achieves state-of-the-art performance under comparable settings, across diverse video reasoning, video understanding, and temporal grounding benchmarks (V-STAR, VideoMME, World-Sense, VideoMMMU, PerceptionTest, and Charades-STA), while maintaining a single efficient inference pathway without external tools. Our results show that visual prompting during training improves grounded video reasoning, while self-distillation enables the model to internalize this ability without requiring prompts at inference time.
中文标题/摘要
标题：VisionCoach：通过视觉感知提示强化视频推理的时空定位能力
视频推理要求模型在连续帧中定位并追踪与问题相关的证据。尽管基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RL）提升了准确性，但在推理过程中仍难以实现可靠的时空定位。此外，改进定位能力通常依赖大规模训练数据或推理时的感知工具，这会增加标注成本或计算开销。为解决这一挑战，我们提出VisionCoach——一种输入自适应的强化学习框架，通过视觉提示作为训练阶段的引导来提升时空定位能力。在强化学习训练过程中，视觉提示被选择性地应用于具有挑战性的输入，以增强问题相关证据并抑制干扰信息。模型随后通过自蒸馏将这些改进内化，从而在推理时无需视觉提示即可直接对原始视频进行定位推理。VisionCoach包含两个核心组件：（1）视觉提示选择器：根据视频和问题内容预测适用的提示类型；（2）时空推理器：在视觉提示引导及对象感知定位奖励（强化对象身份一致性与多区域边界框重叠）的联合优化下进行强化学习训练。大量实验表明，在可比较的设置下，VisionCoach在多样化视频推理、视频理解和时序定位基准（V-STAR、VideoMME、World-Sense、VideoMMMU、PerceptionTest和Charades-STA）上均达到最先进性能，同时保持单一高效推理路径且无需外部工具。研究结果表明：训练阶段的视觉提示能有效提升视频定位推理能力，而自蒸馏技术使模型无需推理时提示即可内化这种能力。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of achieving reliable spatio-temporal grounding in video reasoning tasks, where existing reinforcement learning methods often struggle without costly data scaling or inference-time perception tools. The authors propose VisionCoach, an input-adaptive RL framework that uses visual-perception prompting during training to selectively amplify question-relevant evidence and suppress distractors in challenging inputs, followed by self-distillation to internalize these improvements. Experimental results show state-of-the-art performance across multiple video reasoning benchmarks, including V-STAR and VideoMME, while maintaining a single efficient inference pathway without external tools at test time.
该论文针对视频推理任务中时空定位不可靠的挑战，现有强化学习方法常依赖昂贵的数据扩展或推理时感知工具。作者提出VisionCoach框架，在训练时通过视觉提示自适应地增强问题相关证据并抑制干扰，再通过自蒸馏内化这些改进。实验结果表明，该方法在V-STAR、VideoMME等多个视频推理基准上达到最先进性能，且推理时无需外部工具，保持高效单一路径。
